---

NOW NEXT = STEP 2: BUILD GPS DEVICE COMMUNICATION ENGINE

This is the most critical technical step in a GPS business.

If this is solid → everything else works
If this is weak → business fails (no matter how good UI is)

🧠 WHAT STEP 2 REALLY IS

You are building a 24×7 device listener server that:

Accepts GPS devices (TCP/UDP)

Authenticates by IMEI

Receives live GPS packets

Stores live + history data

Sends commands (ignition off/on, restart)

Handles ACK & retries

Detects device online/offline

This runs separately from backend & UI.

🧱 STEP 2.1 — CHOOSE INITIAL PROTOCOL (IMPORTANT)

Do NOT try all devices at once.

Start with:

✅ GT06 protocol (most common, cheap, widely used)

Later you add:

Teltonika

Concox

Queclink

SinoTrack

🗂️ STEP 2.2 — TCP SERVER STRUCTURE

Create folder:

tcp-server/
├── server.js / server.py
├── protocol/
│   └── gt06.js
├── decoder/
├── encoder/
├── command_queue/
├── ack_handler/
├── device_sessions/
├── config/
└── logs/

This server:

Does NOT handle users

Does NOT handle UI

Only talks to devices

🔐 STEP 2.3 — DEVICE HANDSHAKE FLOW (VERY IMPORTANT)
Flow:

1️⃣ Device connects
2️⃣ Sends IMEI packet
3️⃣ Server validates IMEI from devices table
4️⃣ If valid → ACK sent
5️⃣ Device marked ONLINE
6️⃣ Session stored in memory (Redis or RAM)

❌ If IMEI not in DB → connection closed

📍 STEP 2.4 — LIVE DATA HANDLING

On each GPS packet:

Decode latitude, longitude, speed, course

Update gps_live_data

Insert into gps_history

Update last_seen timestamp

Trigger alerts (geofence, overspeed)

💡 Never query gps_history for live data

🔁 STEP 2.5 — ONLINE / OFFLINE LOGIC

Heartbeat interval (30–60 sec)

If no packet for X mins → OFFLINE

Write status to DB

Trigger offline alert

🔜 WHAT IS NEXT AFTER STEP 2?

Once:

Devices connect

Data flows

Live table updates

👉 STEP 3 = COMMAND ENGINE

This is where:

Ignition OFF/ON

Restart

Custom commands

Safety rules

OTP verification

Admin/client permissions

⚠️ VERY IMPORTANT WARNINGS

❌ Do not send commands directly from UI
❌ Do not hardcode device commands
❌ Do not store socket IDs in DB
❌ Do not block TCP thread with DB calls

STEP 3: Build DEVICE COMMAND ENGINE (Most Critical) 🔥
Problem you raised (very important):

Each GPS device has different commands

Solution (Industry-grade):
1️⃣ Create a Command Abstraction Layer

Admin / Client sends:

IGNITION_OFF

System converts internally:

Device Model → Actual Command
Example Table
Device Model	Logical Action	Actual Command
Concox GT06	IGN_OFF	DYD#
Teltonika	IGN_OFF	setdigout 0
SinoTrack	IGN_OFF	RELAY,0#

👉 Device never talks directly to UI.

STEP 4: Role-Based Command Control 🔐
Role	Can Track	Can Stop Engine	Can Restart	Can Change Settings
Admin	✅	✅	✅	✅
Reseller	✅	❌	❌	❌
Client	✅	⚠️ (optional)	❌	❌
Driver App	❌	❌	❌	❌

⚠️ Engine ON/OFF:

Client allowed only if enabled by Admin

OTP + audit log mandatory

STEP 2 — MAP DEVICE COMMAND (1 hour)

In DB / config:

device_model	logical_command	actual_command
GT06	IGNITION_OFF	RELAY,1#

👉 This allows multiple device brands later.

STEP 3 — COMMAND FLOW (THIS IS CRITICAL)
When admin/client clicks “Ignition OFF”:

UI calls backend API

Backend:

Checks permission

Checks vehicle state (speed = 0)

Creates command record → PENDING

Command engine:

Finds device socket

Sends command

Device:

Executes ignition cut

Sends ACK

Server:

Marks command SUCCESS

Writes audit log

Sends notification

⚠️ If ACK not received → retry → fail → alert

STEP 4 — SAFETY RULES (MANDATORY)

You MUST enforce:

❌ Ignition OFF if speed > 5 km/h

❌ Ignition OFF if vehicle already OFF

❌ Client allowed only if admin enabled

This avoids legal & accident risk.

STEP 5 — TEST WITH REAL HARDWARE

Do this with one physical GPS device:

Engine ON → speed 0 → ignition OFF works

Engine ON → speed > 0 → command rejected

Device offline → command queued

If any fails → fix before moving on

Because:

80% GPS companies fail here

Customers buy GPS for control, not maps

File: /database/schema.sql
sql
-- ============================================
-- GPS TRACKING SAAS - COMPLETE PRODUCTION SCHEMA
-- Based on requirements from files 1-15
-- ============================================

-- Enable extensions
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "postgis"; -- For geospatial queries
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "btree_gin"; -- For advanced indexing

-- ============================================
-- CORE TABLES (File 3, 6, 9)
-- ============================================

-- Roles & Permissions
CREATE TABLE roles (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    name VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    permissions JSONB DEFAULT '[]', -- Array of permissions
    is_system_role BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_by UUID
);

CREATE TABLE users (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password_hash TEXT NOT NULL,
    full_name VARCHAR(255),
    phone VARCHAR(20),
    avatar_url TEXT,
    
    -- 2FA & Security
    two_factor_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    two_factor_secret TEXT,
    otp_required BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    
    -- Status
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    is_locked BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    login_attempts INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    last_login_at TIMESTAMP,
    last_login_ip INET,
    
    -- Metadata
    timezone VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'UTC',
    language VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'en',
    notification_preferences JSONB DEFAULT '{"push": true, "email": true, "sms": false}',
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    
    CONSTRAINT email_format CHECK (email ~* '^[A-Za-z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+\.[A-Za-z]{2,}$')
);

CREATE TABLE user_roles (
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    role_id UUID REFERENCES roles(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    assigned_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    assigned_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    expires_at TIMESTAMP,
    PRIMARY KEY (user_id, role_id)
);

-- Resellers (File 14)
CREATE TABLE resellers (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    company_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    contact_name VARCHAR(255),
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    phone VARCHAR(20),
    address TEXT,
    
    -- White-label settings
    subdomain VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    custom_domain VARCHAR(255),
    logo_url TEXT,
    favicon_url TEXT,
    primary_color VARCHAR(7) DEFAULT '#2563eb',
    secondary_color VARCHAR(7) DEFAULT '#1e40af',
    
    -- Business
    commission_percent DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0,
    monthly_fee DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0,
    min_device_commitment INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Status
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    subscription_tier VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'basic',
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- Clients (File 1)
CREATE TABLE clients (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    reseller_id UUID REFERENCES resellers(id),
    user_id UUID UNIQUE REFERENCES users(id),
    
    company_name VARCHAR(255),
    tax_id VARCHAR(50),
    billing_address TEXT,
    billing_email VARCHAR(255),
    billing_phone VARCHAR(20),
    
    -- Preferences
    alert_webhook_url TEXT,
    report_frequency VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'daily',
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- ============================================
-- DEVICE MANAGEMENT (File 5, 6)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE device_models (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    manufacturer VARCHAR(100),
    protocol VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- GT06, Teltonika, Concox, Queclink
    protocol_version VARCHAR(20),
    
    -- Capabilities
    supports_ignition BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    supports_fuel BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    supports_temperature BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    supports_canbus BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    supports_ble BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    
    -- Command formats (File 11)
    command_format JSONB DEFAULT '{
        "ignition_on": null,
        "ignition_off": null,
        "restart": null,
        "reboot": null,
        "get_location": null
    }',
    
    -- Packet structure
    packet_structure JSONB,
    
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE sim_cards (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    iccid VARCHAR(30) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    imsi VARCHAR(20),
    phone_number VARCHAR(20),
    operator VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Plan
    data_plan VARCHAR(50),
    data_limit_mb INTEGER,
    data_used_mb INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Status
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    activation_date DATE,
    expiry_date DATE,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE devices (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    imei VARCHAR(20) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    model_id UUID REFERENCES device_models(id),
    sim_id UUID REFERENCES sim_cards(id),
    
    -- Identification
    serial_number VARCHAR(50),
    mac_address VARCHAR(17),
    firmware_version VARCHAR(50),
    hardware_version VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Ownership
    client_id UUID REFERENCES clients(id),
    current_vehicle_id UUID, -- Will reference vehicles
    
    -- Status
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'offline', -- online, offline, inactive, suspended
    connection_status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'disconnected', -- connected, disconnected, connecting
    last_seen TIMESTAMP,
    last_ip INET,
    last_packet_time TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Connection stats
    total_uptime_minutes INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_downtime_minutes INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    packet_count BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Subscription
    subscription_start DATE,
    subscription_expiry DATE,
    grace_period_end DATE,
    is_subscription_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    
    -- Location (latest)
    last_latitude DECIMAL(10,8),
    last_longitude DECIMAL(11,8),
    last_speed DECIMAL(6,2),
    last_heading DECIMAL(5,2),
    last_altitude DECIMAL(8,2),
    
    -- Metadata
    installation_date DATE,
    installation_notes TEXT,
    qr_code TEXT,
    qr_scanned_at TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Security
    auth_key TEXT,
    is_blacklisted BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    blacklist_reason TEXT,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    
    CONSTRAINT valid_imei CHECK (imei ~ '^[0-9]{15,17}$')
);

CREATE TABLE vehicles (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    client_id UUID REFERENCES clients(id) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Identification
    registration_number VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    vin VARCHAR(17),
    chassis_number VARCHAR(50),
    engine_number VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Vehicle details
    make VARCHAR(50),
    model VARCHAR(50),
    year INTEGER,
    fuel_type VARCHAR(20), -- petrol, diesel, electric, hybrid
    fuel_capacity_liters DECIMAL(8,2),
    color VARCHAR(30),
    
    -- Specs
    engine_capacity_cc INTEGER,
    horsepower INTEGER,
    gross_weight_kg INTEGER,
    seating_capacity INTEGER,
    
    -- Current status
    current_device_id UUID REFERENCES devices(id),
    current_driver_id UUID, -- Will reference drivers
    odometer_reading INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    last_maintenance_at TIMESTAMP,
    next_maintenance_due TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Documents
    insurance_expiry DATE,
    registration_expiry DATE,
    fitness_expiry DATE,
    permit_expiry DATE,
    
    -- Metadata
    notes TEXT,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- Link devices to vehicles (history)
CREATE TABLE device_vehicle_history (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    device_id UUID REFERENCES devices(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    vehicle_id UUID REFERENCES vehicles(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    assigned_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    removed_at TIMESTAMP,
    assigned_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    is_current BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    
    -- Metadata at time of assignment
    vehicle_odometer INTEGER,
    device_packet_count BIGINT
);

-- ============================================
-- GPS TRACKING DATA (File 5, 10)
-- ============================================

-- Live data - latest position only (File 5)
CREATE TABLE gps_live_data (
    device_id UUID PRIMARY KEY REFERENCES devices(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    latitude DECIMAL(10,8) NOT NULL,
    longitude DECIMAL(11,8) NOT NULL,
    altitude DECIMAL(8,2),
    speed DECIMAL(6,2),
    heading DECIMAL(5,2),
    
    -- Location context
    location_point GEOGRAPHY(POINT),
    reverse_geocoded_address TEXT,
    city VARCHAR(100),
    state VARCHAR(100),
    country VARCHAR(100),
    postal_code VARCHAR(20),
    
    -- Status
    satellites INTEGER,
    gsm_signal INTEGER,
    ignition BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    motion BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    charging BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    battery_level DECIMAL(5,2),
    external_power BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    
    -- Movement
    distance_since_start DECIMAL(10,2),
    trip_id UUID,
    
    -- Raw data
    raw_data JSONB,
    protocol_data JSONB,
    
    -- Timestamps
    device_time TIMESTAMP,
    server_time TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Create spatial index
CREATE INDEX idx_gps_live_location ON gps_live_data USING GIST(location_point);

-- Partitioned history table (File 3)
CREATE TABLE gps_history (
    id UUID DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    device_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES devices(id),
    latitude DECIMAL(10,8) NOT NULL,
    longitude DECIMAL(11,8) NOT NULL,
    altitude DECIMAL(8,2),
    speed DECIMAL(6,2),
    heading DECIMAL(5,2),
    satellites INTEGER,
    gsm_signal INTEGER,
    ignition BOOLEAN,
    motion BOOLEAN,
    charging BOOLEAN,
    battery_level DECIMAL(5,2),
    external_power BOOLEAN,
    distance_delta DECIMAL(10,2),
    location_point GEOGRAPHY(POINT),
    raw_data JSONB,
    protocol_data JSONB,
    device_time TIMESTAMP,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    trip_id UUID,
    PRIMARY KEY (id, created_at)
) PARTITION BY RANGE (created_at);

-- Create partitions for current and future months
DO $$
DECLARE
    start_date DATE;
    end_date DATE;
    partition_name TEXT;
BEGIN
    FOR i IN 0..11 LOOP
        start_date := DATE_TRUNC('month', CURRENT_DATE + (i || ' months')::INTERVAL);
        end_date := DATE_TRUNC('month', CURRENT_DATE + ((i+1) || ' months')::INTERVAL);
        partition_name := 'gps_history_' || TO_CHAR(start_date, 'YYYY_MM');
        
        EXECUTE format('
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS %I PARTITION OF gps_history
            FOR VALUES FROM (%L) TO (%L)',
            partition_name, start_date, end_date
        );
    END LOOP;
END $$;

-- Default partition for any data outside range
CREATE TABLE gps_history_default PARTITION OF gps_history DEFAULT;

-- ============================================
-- COMMAND SYSTEM (File 11 - CRITICAL)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE logical_commands (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    name VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    category VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- ignition, immobilizer, location, config
    description TEXT,
    parameters_schema JSONB, -- Define expected parameters
    requires_otp BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    requires_approval BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    safety_check_required BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    is_reversible BOOLEAN DEFAULT true, -- Can be undone
    timeout_seconds INTEGER DEFAULT 30,
    max_retries INTEGER DEFAULT 3,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Insert standard commands (File 6)
INSERT INTO logical_commands (name, category, description, requires_otp, safety_check_required) VALUES
    ('IGNITION_ON', 'ignition', 'Turn ignition ON', true, true),
    ('IGNITION_OFF', 'ignition', 'Turn ignition OFF', true, true),
    ('ENGINE_RESTART', 'ignition', 'Restart engine', true, true),
    ('ARM_IMMOBILIZER', 'immobilizer', 'Arm immobilizer', true, false),
    ('DISARM_IMMOBILIZER', 'immobilizer', 'Disarm immobilizer', true, false),
    ('GET_LOCATION', 'location', 'Request immediate location', false, false),
    ('REBOOT_DEVICE', 'config', 'Reboot GPS device', false, true),
    ('SET_SLEEP_MODE', 'config', 'Put device in sleep mode', false, true),
    ('SET_WAKE_MODE', 'config', 'Wake device from sleep', false, true),
    ('CUSTOM_COMMAND', 'custom', 'Send custom command', false, false);

-- Device-specific command mapping (File 11)
CREATE TABLE device_command_map (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    device_model_id UUID REFERENCES device_models(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    logical_command_id UUID REFERENCES logical_commands(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    actual_command TEXT NOT NULL,
    command_format VARCHAR(50), -- text, hex, binary
    parameters_mapping JSONB, -- How to map parameters
    timeout_seconds INTEGER,
    retry_count INTEGER,
    requires_ack BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    success_response_pattern TEXT,
    failure_response_pattern TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(device_model_id, logical_command_id)
);

-- Command queue and logs
CREATE TABLE command_queue (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    device_id UUID REFERENCES devices(id) NOT NULL,
    command_log_id UUID, -- Will reference command_logs
    
    priority INTEGER DEFAULT 0, -- Higher = higher priority
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'QUEUED', -- QUEUED, PROCESSING, SENT, COMPLETED, FAILED
    
    -- Execution
    execute_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    expires_at TIMESTAMP,
    last_attempt TIMESTAMP,
    attempt_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- Command execution log (IMMUTABLE - File 6)
CREATE TABLE command_logs (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    device_id UUID REFERENCES devices(id) NOT NULL,
    logical_command_id UUID REFERENCES logical_commands(id),
    command_text TEXT NOT NULL,
    parameters JSONB,
    
    -- Request context
    requested_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    requested_from_ip INET,
    requested_from_user_agent TEXT,
    approval_required BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    approved_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    approved_at TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Safety
    safety_checks_passed BOOLEAN,
    vehicle_speed_at_command DECIMAL,
    vehicle_ignition_state BOOLEAN,
    otp_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    otp_code VARCHAR(10),
    
    -- Execution
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, -- PENDING, SENT, SUCCESS, FAILED, TIMEOUT, REJECTED
    attempt_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    response_data JSONB,
    error_message TEXT,
    execution_time_ms INTEGER,
    
    -- Device response
    ack_received BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    ack_data JSONB,
    device_response_time_ms INTEGER,
    
    -- Timestamps
    queued_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    sent_at TIMESTAMP,
    completed_at TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Index for partitioning if needed
    command_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (DATE(created_at)) STORED
) PARTITION BY RANGE (created_at);

-- Create command_logs partitions
CREATE TABLE command_logs_default PARTITION OF command_logs DEFAULT;

-- ============================================
-- ALERT SYSTEM (File 12)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE alert_rules (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- overspeed, offline, ignition, geofence, fuel, tamper
    
    -- Rule definition
    condition JSONB NOT NULL, -- e.g., {"speed": {"operator": ">", "value": 120}}
    severity VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'WARNING', -- INFO, WARNING, CRITICAL
    
    -- Timing
    cooldown_minutes INTEGER DEFAULT 0, -- Prevent alert spam
    time_window_start TIME, -- Only trigger between these times
    time_window_end TIME,
    days_of_week INTEGER[], -- 0=Sunday, 6=Saturday, NULL=all
    
    -- Actions
    notify_in_app BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    notify_push BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    notify_email BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    notify_sms BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    notify_whatsapp BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    notify_webhook BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    webhook_url TEXT,
    
    -- Ownership
    client_id UUID REFERENCES clients(id),
    vehicle_id UUID REFERENCES vehicles(id),
    is_global BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    
    -- Metadata
    description TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id)
);

CREATE TABLE alert_events (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    rule_id UUID REFERENCES alert_rules(id),
    device_id UUID REFERENCES devices(id),
    vehicle_id UUID REFERENCES vehicles(id),
    client_id UUID REFERENCES clients(id),
    
    -- Alert data
    severity VARCHAR(20),
    message TEXT,
    details JSONB, -- Snapshot of data when alert triggered
    location GEOGRAPHY(POINT),
    
    -- Values at trigger
    trigger_value TEXT,
    trigger_unit VARCHAR(20),
    
    -- Status
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'ACTIVE', -- ACTIVE, ACKNOWLEDGED, RESOLVED, IGNORED
    acknowledged_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    resolved_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    resolved_at TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Timestamps
    triggered_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    acknowledged_at TIMESTAMP,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE notifications (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    alert_event_id UUID REFERENCES alert_events(id),
    
    channel VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, -- PUSH, EMAIL, SMS, WHATSAPP, IN_APP, WEBHOOK
    title TEXT,
    body TEXT,
    data JSONB,
    
    -- Delivery
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'PENDING', -- PENDING, SENT, DELIVERED, FAILED, READ
    provider_response JSONB,
    error_message TEXT,
    
    -- Receipt
    sent_at TIMESTAMP,
    delivered_at TIMESTAMP,
    read_at TIMESTAMP,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- ============================================
-- TRIPS & PLAYBACK (File 14)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE trips (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    device_id UUID REFERENCES devices(id) NOT NULL,
    vehicle_id UUID REFERENCES vehicles(id),
    driver_id UUID, -- Will reference drivers
    
    -- Timing
    start_time TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    end_time TIMESTAMP,
    duration_seconds INTEGER,
    
    -- Location
    start_latitude DECIMAL(10,8),
    start_longitude DECIMAL(11,8),
    end_latitude DECIMAL(10,8),
    end_longitude DECIMAL(11,8),
    start_address TEXT,
    end_address TEXT,
    
    -- Statistics
    distance_meters DECIMAL(10,2),
    max_speed DECIMAL(6,2),
    avg_speed DECIMAL(6,2),
    idle_seconds INTEGER,
    moving_seconds INTEGER,
    fuel_consumed DECIMAL(8,2),
    fuel_avg_kmpl DECIMAL(5,2),
    
    -- Events
    overspeed_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    harsh_braking_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    harsh_acceleration_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    sharp_turn_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Route
    polyline TEXT, -- Encoded polyline for map
    route_points JSONB, -- Compressed route points
    point_count INTEGER,
    
    -- Status
    is_completed BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    is_processed BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE trip_points (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    trip_id UUID REFERENCES trips(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    latitude DECIMAL(10,8) NOT NULL,
    longitude DECIMAL(11,8) NOT NULL,
    speed DECIMAL(6,2),
    heading DECIMAL(5,2),
    altitude DECIMAL(8,2),
    ignition BOOLEAN,
    distance_from_start DECIMAL(10,2),
    elapsed_seconds INTEGER,
    recorded_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- ============================================
-- FUEL & CAN BUS (File 12)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE fuel_data (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    device_id UUID REFERENCES devices(id),
    vehicle_id UUID REFERENCES vehicles(id),
    
    -- Fuel levels
    level_percent DECIMAL(5,2),
    level_liters DECIMAL(8,2),
    temperature DECIMAL(5,2),
    
    -- Status
    is_fueling BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    is_theft BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    fueling_amount DECIMAL(8,2),
    theft_amount DECIMAL(8,2),
    
    -- Raw
    raw_data JSONB,
    sensor_id VARCHAR(50),
    
    recorded_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE canbus_data (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    device_id UUID REFERENCES devices(id),
    vehicle_id UUID REFERENCES vehicles(id),
    
    -- Engine
    rpm INTEGER,
    engine_load DECIMAL(5,2),
    coolant_temp DECIMAL(5,2),
    intake_temp DECIMAL(5,2),
    throttle_position DECIMAL(5,2),
    
    -- Fuel
    instant_fuel_consumption DECIMAL(8,2),
    avg_fuel_consumption DECIMAL(8,2),
    fuel_pressure DECIMAL(8,2),
    
    -- Electrical
    battery_voltage DECIMAL(5,2),
    alternator_voltage DECIMAL(5,2),
    
    -- Diagnostics
    dtc_codes TEXT[], -- Diagnostic trouble codes
    check_engine BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    
    -- OBD
    obd_standards VARCHAR(20),
    
    recorded_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- ============================================
-- AI DRIVER SCORING (File 11, 14)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE driver_scores (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    driver_id UUID, -- Will reference drivers
    vehicle_id UUID REFERENCES vehicles(id),
    
    -- Score period
    period_start DATE NOT NULL,
    period_end DATE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Overall score (0-100)
    overall_score DECIMAL(5,2),
    
    -- Component scores
    speed_score DECIMAL(5,2),
    braking_score DECIMAL(5,2),
    acceleration_score DECIMAL(5,2),
    cornering_score DECIMAL(5,2),
    idle_score DECIMAL(5,2),
    night_driving_score DECIMAL(5,2),
    
    -- Statistics
    total_distance DECIMAL(10,2),
    total_driving_hours DECIMAL(8,2),
    trip_count INTEGER,
    
    -- Events
    overspeed_count INTEGER,
    harsh_braking_count INTEGER,
    harsh_acceleration_count INTEGER,
    sharp_turn_count INTEGER,
    idle_percent DECIMAL(5,2),
    night_driving_percent DECIMAL(5,2),
    
    -- Risk level
    risk_level VARCHAR(20), -- LOW, MEDIUM, HIGH, CRITICAL
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- ============================================
-- BILLING & SUBSCRIPTIONS (File 8, 14)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE plans (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    
    -- Pricing
    price_monthly DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL,
    price_yearly DECIMAL(10,2),
    setup_fee DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0,
    currency VARCHAR(3) DEFAULT 'USD',
    
    -- Features
    max_vehicles INTEGER,
    max_drivers INTEGER,
    features JSONB, -- List of included features
    
    -- Limits
    data_retention_days INTEGER DEFAULT 365,
    support_level VARCHAR(20),
    
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    is_public BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE subscriptions (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    client_id UUID REFERENCES clients(id),
    reseller_id UUID REFERENCES resellers(id),
    plan_id UUID REFERENCES plans(id),
    
    -- Subscription details
    start_date DATE NOT NULL,
    end_date DATE NOT NULL,
    grace_period_end DATE,
    auto_renew BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    
    -- Status
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'ACTIVE', -- ACTIVE, EXPIRED, CANCELLED, SUSPENDED, GRACE
    
    -- Pricing at time of subscription
    price_monthly DECIMAL(10,2),
    price_yearly DECIMAL(10,2),
    setup_fee DECIMAL(10,2),
    
    -- Billing
    billing_cycle VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'MONTHLY', -- MONTHLY, YEARLY
    next_billing_date DATE,
    last_invoice_id UUID,
    
    -- Device limits
    device_limit INTEGER,
    devices_used INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Metadata
    notes TEXT,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id)
);

CREATE TABLE invoices (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    subscription_id UUID REFERENCES subscriptions(id),
    client_id UUID REFERENCES clients(id),
    invoice_number VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE,
    
    -- Billing
    amount DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL,
    tax_amount DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0,
    total_amount DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL,
    currency VARCHAR(3) DEFAULT 'USD',
    
    -- Period
    period_start DATE,
    period_end DATE,
    due_date DATE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Status
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'PENDING', -- PENDING, PAID, OVERDUE, CANCELLED, REFUNDED
    paid_at TIMESTAMP,
    payment_method VARCHAR(50),
    transaction_id VARCHAR(255),
    
    -- Items
    items JSONB, -- Line items
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE payments (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    invoice_id UUID REFERENCES invoices(id),
    client_id UUID REFERENCES clients(id),
    
    amount DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL,
    payment_method VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- CARD, BANK_TRANSFER, CASH, CRYPTO
    payment_provider VARCHAR(50),
    transaction_id VARCHAR(255),
    
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'PENDING', -- PENDING, COMPLETED, FAILED, REFUNDED
    provider_response JSONB,
    error_message TEXT,
    
    paid_at TIMESTAMP,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- ============================================
-- AUDIT & SECURITY (File 15, 16)
-- ============================================

-- Comprehensive audit log (IMMUTABLE)
CREATE TABLE audit_logs (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    user_email VARCHAR(255),
    user_role VARCHAR(50),
    
    action VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    category VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- AUTH, DEVICE, COMMAND, ALERT, BILLING, USER
    
    -- Target
    entity_type VARCHAR(50),
    entity_id UUID,
    entity_name VARCHAR(255),
    
    -- Changes
    old_values JSONB,
    new_values JSONB,
    diff JSONB,
    
    -- Context
    ip_address INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    request_id VARCHAR(255),
    request_path TEXT,
    request_method VARCHAR(10),
    
    -- Result
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'SUCCESS', -- SUCCESS, FAILURE, DENIED
    error_message TEXT,
    response_time_ms INTEGER,
    
    -- Metadata
    location GEOGRAPHY(POINT),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
) PARTITION BY RANGE (created_at);

-- Create audit_logs partitions
CREATE TABLE audit_logs_default PARTITION OF audit_logs DEFAULT;

-- Login history
CREATE TABLE login_history (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    email VARCHAR(255),
    
    success BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    ip_address INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    
    -- 2FA
    two_factor_used BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    two_factor_success BOOLEAN,
    
    -- Failure reason
    failure_reason VARCHAR(100),
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE geofences (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    client_id UUID REFERENCES clients(id),

    type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, -- CIRCLE, POLYGON, ROUTE
    
    -- Shape data

    center_longitude DECIMAL(11,8), -- For circle
    radius_meters DECIMAL(10,2), -- For circle
    polygon_coordinates JSONB, -- For polygon
    route_coordinates JSONB, -- For route
    
    -- Geometry
    geometry GEOGRAPHY,

    alert_on_enter BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    alert_on_exit BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    alert_on_speed BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    
    -- Schedule
    active_24_7 BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    time_window_start TIME,
    time_window_end TIME,
    days_of_week INTEGER[],
    
    -- Metadata
    color VARCHAR(7) DEFAULT '#2563eb',
    description TEXT,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id)
);

);

📊 File 4: /tcp-server/protocols/gt06.js
javascript
/**
 * GT06 Protocol Handler
 * Based on File 5 and File 10 requirements
 */

class GT06Protocol {
    constructor() {
        this.protocolName = 'GT06';
        this.port = 5001;
    }

    /**
     * Parse GT06 packet
     * Format: Start Bit (0x78/0x79) + Length + Protocol Number + Data + CRC + Stop Bit
     */
    parse(buffer) {
        try {
            const data = {
                raw: buffer.toString('hex'),
                length: buffer.length
            };

            // Check start bits
            const startByte = buffer[0];
            if (startByte !== 0x78 && startByte !== 0x79) {
                throw new Error('Invalid start byte');
            }

            // Get protocol number
            const protocolNumber = buffer[2];
            
            // Parse based on protocol number
            switch(protocolNumber) {
                case 0x01: // Login message
                    return this.parseLogin(buffer);
                case 0x12: // GPS data
                    return this.parseGPSData(buffer);
                case 0x13: // GPS data (with additional info)
                    return this.parseGPSData(buffer);
                case 0x80: // Heartbeat
                    return this.parseHeartbeat(buffer);
                case 0x05: // Command response
                    return this.parseCommandResponse(buffer);
                default:
                    return this.parseGeneric(buffer);
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('GT06 Parse Error:', error);
            return null;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Parse login message (Protocol 0x01)
     */
    parseLogin(buffer) {
        // Extract IMEI (usually 15 or 17 digits)
        const imeiStart = 4;
        const imeiLength = 8; // 8 bytes BCD = 15/16 digits
        const imeiBytes = buffer.slice(imeiStart, imeiStart + imeiLength);
        const imei = this.bcdToString(imeiBytes);
        
        return {
            type: 'LOGIN',
            imei: imei,
            protocol: 0x01,
            timestamp: new Date()
        };
    }

    /**
     * Parse GPS data (Protocol 0x12, 0x13, 0x22)
     */
    parseGPSData(buffer) {
        const protocolNumber = buffer[2];
        let dataStart = 4;
        
        // Parse date/time
        const year = buffer[dataStart];
        const month = buffer[dataStart + 1];
        const day = buffer[dataStart + 2];
        const hour = buffer[dataStart + 3];
        const minute = buffer[dataStart + 4];
        const second = buffer[dataStart + 5];
        
        // Parse GPS info
        const satellites = buffer[dataStart + 6];
        const latitude = this.parseLatitude(buffer.slice(dataStart + 7, dataStart + 11));
        const longitude = this.parseLongitude(buffer.slice(dataStart + 11, dataStart + 15));
        const speed = buffer[dataStart + 15]; // km/h
        const course = buffer[dataStart + 16] * 2; // degrees
        const status = buffer[dataStart + 17];
        
        // Parse additional info for protocol 0x13
        let mcc, mnc, lac, cellId;
        if (protocolNumber === 0x13 || protocolNumber === 0x22) {
            mcc = buffer.readUInt16BE(dataStart + 18);
            mnc = buffer[dataStart + 20];
            lac = buffer.readUInt16BE(dataStart + 21);
            cellId = buffer.readUInt16BE(dataStart + 23);
        }
        
        return {
            type: 'GPS',
            protocol: protocolNumber,
            deviceTime: this.createDate(year, month, day, hour, minute, second),
            satellites: satellites,
            latitude: latitude,
            longitude: longitude,
            speed: speed,
            heading: course,
            ignition: (status & 0x01) === 0x01,
            acc: (status & 0x02) === 0x02,
            charging: (status & 0x04) === 0x04,
            gsmSignal: (status >> 2) & 0x03,
            ...(protocolNumber === 0x13 || protocolNumber === 0x22 ? {
                mcc, mnc, lac, cellId
            } : {})
        };
    }

    /**
     * Parse heartbeat (Protocol 0x80)
     */
    parseHeartbeat(buffer) {
        const terminalInfo = buffer[4];
        
        return {
            type: 'HEARTBEAT',
            protocol: 0x80,
            ignition: (terminalInfo & 0x01) === 0x01,
            charging: (terminalInfo & 0x02) === 0x02,
            gsmSignal: (terminalInfo >> 2) & 0x03,
            timestamp: new Date()
        };
    }

    /**
     * Parse command response
     */
    parseCommandResponse(buffer) {
        return {
            type: 'COMMAND_RESPONSE',
            protocol: buffer[2],
            data: buffer.slice(4, -2).toString(),
            timestamp: new Date()
        };
    }

    parseGeneric(buffer) {
        return {
            type: 'UNKNOWN',
            protocol: buffer[2],
            data: buffer.slice(4, -2).toString('hex'),
            timestamp: new Date()
        };
    }

    /**
     * Create ACK response
     */
    createAck(protocolNumber, serialNumber) {
        const buffer = Buffer.alloc(5);
        buffer[0] = 0x78; // Start bit
        buffer[1] = 0x78; // Start bit
        buffer[2] = protocolNumber; // Same protocol number
        buffer[3] = serialNumber; // Serial number
        buffer[4] = this.calculateCRC(buffer.slice(0, 4)); // CRC
        buffer[5] = 0x0D; // Stop bit (carriage return)
        
        return buffer;
    }

    /**
     * Create command to device
     */
    createCommand(command, serialNumber) {
        const commandBuffer = Buffer.from(command, 'ascii');
        const length = commandBuffer.length;
        
        const buffer = Buffer.alloc(7 + length);
        buffer[0] = 0x78; // Start bit
        buffer[1] = 0x78; // Start bit
        buffer[2] = 0x80; // Command protocol
        buffer[3] = length + 3; // Length
        buffer[4] = serialNumber; // Serial number
        buffer.writeUInt16BE(0x0001, 5); // Command type
        commandBuffer.copy(buffer, 7);
        
        // Add CRC
        const crc = this.calculateCRC(buffer.slice(2, 7 + length));
        buffer[7 + length] = crc;
        buffer[8 + length] = 0x0D; // Stop bit
        
        return buffer;
    }

    // Helper functions
    bcdToString(bytes) {
        return bytes.map(b => {
            const high = (b >> 4) & 0x0F;
            const low = b & 0x0F;
            return `${high}${low}`;
        }).join('');
    }

    parseLatitude(bytes) {
        const raw = bytes.readUInt32BE(0);
        const degrees = Math.floor(raw / 30000 / 60);
        const minutes = (raw / 30000) % 60;
        return degrees + (minutes / 60);
    }

    parseLongitude(bytes) {
        const raw = bytes.readUInt32BE(0);
        const degrees = Math.floor(raw / 30000 / 60);
        const minutes = (raw / 30000) % 60;
        return degrees + (minutes / 60);
    }

    createDate(year, month, day, hour, minute, second) {
        const fullYear = 2000 + year;
        return new Date(fullYear, month - 1, day, hour, minute, second);
    }

    calculateCRC(buffer) {
        let crc = 0;
        for (let i = 0; i < buffer.length; i++) {
            crc ^= buffer[i];
        }
        return crc;
    }
}

module.exports = new GT06Protocol();
🖥️ File 5: /tcp-server/server.js
javascript
/**
 * Main TCP Server for GPS Devices
 * Based on File 5 and File 10 requirements
 */

const net = require('net');
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const winston = require('winston');
const config = require('./config');
const gt06 = require('./protocols/gt06');
const sessionManager = require('./sessions');
const commandSender = require('./command_sender');

// Database connection pool
const db = new Pool({
    host: config.database.host,
    port: config.database.port,
    database: config.database.name,
    user: config.database.user,
    password: config.database.password,
    max: config.database.poolSize
});

// Redis client for sessions and queues
const redis = new Redis({
    host: config.redis.host,
    port: config.redis.port,
    password: config.redis.password,
    keyPrefix: config.redis.keyPrefix
});

// Logger setup
const logger = winston.createLogger({
    level: config.logging.level,
    format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.timestamp(),
        winston.format.json()
    ),
    transports: [
        new winston.transports.File({ filename: config.logging.file }),
        new winston.transports.Console({ format: winston.format.simple() })
    ]
});

// Track connected devices
const connectedDevices = new Map();

// Create TCP server
const server = net.createServer((socket) => {
    const clientAddress = `${socket.remoteAddress}:${socket.remotePort}`;
    logger.info(`Device connected from ${clientAddress}`);
    
    let deviceId = null;
    let imei = null;
    let heartbeatInterval = null;
    
    // Set socket timeout
    socket.setTimeout(60000); // 60 seconds
    socket.setKeepAlive(true, 30000);
    
    // Handle incoming data
    socket.on('data', async (data) => {
        try {
            logger.debug(`Received ${data.length} bytes from ${clientAddress}`);
            
            // Parse packet based on protocol
            const packet = gt06.parse(data);
            if (!packet) {
                logger.warn(`Failed to parse packet from ${clientAddress}`);
                return;
            }
            
            // Handle different packet types
            switch(packet.type) {
                case 'LOGIN':
                    await handleLogin(socket, packet);
                    break;
                    
                case 'GPS':
                    await handleGPSData(socket, packet);
                    break;
                    
                case 'HEARTBEAT':
                    await handleHeartbeat(socket, packet);
                    break;
                    
                case 'COMMAND_RESPONSE':
                    await handleCommandResponse(socket, packet);
                    break;
                    
                default:
                    logger.info(`Unknown packet type from ${imei || clientAddress}`);
            }
            
            // Reset heartbeat timeout
            if (heartbeatInterval) {
                clearTimeout(heartbeatInterval);
            }
            heartbeatInterval = setTimeout(() => {
                checkDeviceHeartbeat(imei);
            }, config.device.heartbeatTimeout * 1000);
            
        } catch (error) {
            logger.error(`Error processing data: ${error.message}`);
        }
    });
    
    // Handle socket errors
    socket.on('error', (error) => {
        logger.error(`Socket error for ${imei || clientAddress}: ${error.message}`);
    });
    
    // Handle socket close
    socket.on('close', async (hadError) => {
        logger.info(`Device disconnected: ${imei || clientAddress}`);
        
        if (heartbeatInterval) {
            clearTimeout(heartbeatInterval);
        }
        
        if (imei) {
            await handleDeviceDisconnect(imei);
        }
        
        connectedDevices.delete(socket);
    });
    
    // Handle timeout
    socket.on('timeout', () => {
        logger.warn(`Socket timeout for ${imei || clientAddress}`);
        socket.end();
    });
    
    /**
     * Handle device login
     */
    async function handleLogin(socket, packet) {
        try {
            imei = packet.imei;
            
            // Validate IMEI from database
            const device = await validateIMEI(imei);
            if (!device) {
                logger.warn(`Invalid IMEI: ${imei} from ${clientAddress}`);
                socket.write(gt06.createAck(0x01, 0x00)); // Login failed
                socket.end();
                return;
            }
            
            deviceId = device.id;
            
            // Check subscription
            if (!device.is_subscription_active || 
                (device.subscription_expiry && new Date(device.subscription_expiry) < new Date())) {
                logger.warn(`Expired subscription for device ${imei}`);
                socket.write(gt06.createAck(0x01, 0x02)); // Expired
                socket.end();
                return;
            }
            
            // Store session
            await sessionManager.createSession({
                deviceId: device.id,
                imei: imei,
                socket: socket,
                ip: socket.remoteAddress,
                modelId: device.model_id,
                protocol: 'GT06'
            });
            
            // Send login success
            socket.write(gt06.createAck(0x01, 0x01));
            
            // Update device status
            await updateDeviceStatus(device.id, 'online');
            
            logger.info(`Device ${imei} (${device.id}) logged in successfully`);
            
            // Check for pending commands
            await sendPendingCommands(device.id);
            
        } catch (error) {
            logger.error(`Login error for ${imei}: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Handle GPS data
     */
    async function handleGPSData(socket, packet) {
        try {
            if (!deviceId) {
                logger.warn(`GPS data before login from ${clientAddress}`);
                return;
            }
            
            // Store in live data
            await updateLiveData(deviceId, packet);
            
            // Store in history
            await insertHistory(deviceId, packet);
            
            // Check alerts
            await checkAlerts(deviceId, packet);
            
            // Send ACK
            socket.write(gt06.createAck(packet.protocol, 0x01));
            
            // Update last seen
            await updateLastSeen(deviceId);
            
            logger.debug(`GPS data processed for ${imei}: lat=${packet.latitude}, lng=${packet.longitude}`);
            
        } catch (error) {
            logger.error(`GPS data error for ${imei}: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Handle heartbeat
     */
    async function handleHeartbeat(socket, packet) {
        try {
            if (!deviceId) return;
            
            // Update last seen
            await updateLastSeen(deviceId);
            
            // Send ACK
            socket.write(gt06.createAck(0x80, 0x01));
            
            logger.debug(`Heartbeat from ${imei}`);
            
        } catch (error) {
            logger.error(`Heartbeat error for ${imei}: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Handle command response
     */
    async function handleCommandResponse(socket, packet) {
        try {
            if (!deviceId) return;
            
            logger.info(`Command response from ${imei}: ${packet.data}`);
            
            // Update command log
            await updateCommandLog(deviceId, packet);
            
        } catch (error) {
            logger.error(`Command response error: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }
});

/**
 * Validate IMEI from database
 */
async function validateIMEI(imei) {
    try {
        const result = await db.query(`
            SELECT d.id, d.imei, d.model_id, d.client_id, 
                   d.is_subscription_active, d.subscription_expiry,
                   dm.name as model_name, dm.protocol
            FROM devices d
            JOIN device_models dm ON d.model_id = dm.id
            WHERE d.imei = $1 AND d.is_active = true
        `, [imei]);
        
        return result.rows[0] || null;
    } catch (error) {
        logger.error(`Database error validating IMEI: ${error.message}`);
        return null;
    }
}

/**
 * Update device status
 */
async function updateDeviceStatus(deviceId, status) {
    try {
        await db.query(`
            UPDATE devices 
            SET status = $1, 
                last_seen = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
                updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
            WHERE id = $2
        `, [status, deviceId]);
        
        // Update Redis
        await redis.hset(`device:${deviceId}`, 'status', status);
        await redis.hset(`device:${deviceId}`, 'last_seen', new Date().toISOString());
        
    } catch (error) {
        logger.error(`Error updating device status: ${error.message}`);
    }
}

/**
 * Update live data
 */
async function updateLiveData(deviceId, packet) {
    try {
        const query = `
            INSERT INTO gps_live_data (
                device_id, latitude, longitude, speed, heading, 
                satellites, ignition, device_time, raw_data, updated_at
            ) VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8, $9, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
            ON CONFLICT (device_id) DO UPDATE SET
                latitude = EXCLUDED.latitude,
                longitude = EXCLUDED.longitude,
                speed = EXCLUDED.speed,
                heading = EXCLUDED.heading,
                satellites = EXCLUDED.satellites,
                ignition = EXCLUDED.ignition,
                device_time = EXCLUDED.device_time,
                raw_data = EXCLUDED.raw_data,
                updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
        `;
        
        await db.query(query, [
            deviceId,
            packet.latitude,
            packet.longitude,
            packet.speed,
            packet.heading,
            packet.satellites,
            packet.ignition,
            packet.deviceTime,
            JSON.stringify(packet)
        ]);
        
        // Update Redis cache
        await redis.hmset(`live:${deviceId}`, {
            lat: packet.latitude,
            lng: packet.longitude,
            speed: packet.speed,
            heading: packet.heading,
            ignition: packet.ignition ? '1' : '0',
            last_update: new Date().toISOString()
        });
        
    } catch (error) {
        logger.error(`Error updating live data: ${error.message}`);
    }
}

/**
 * Insert history
 */
async function insertHistory(deviceId, packet) {
    try {
        const query = `
            INSERT INTO gps_history (
                id, device_id, latitude, longitude, speed, heading,
                satellites, ignition, device_time, raw_data, created_at
            ) VALUES (uuid_generate_v4(), $1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8, $9, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
        `;
        
        await db.query(query, [
            deviceId,
            packet.latitude,
            packet.longitude,
            packet.speed,
            packet.heading,
            packet.satellites,
            packet.ignition,
            packet.deviceTime,
            JSON.stringify(packet)
        ]);
        
    } catch (error) {
        logger.error(`Error inserting history: ${error.message}`);
    }
}

/**
 * Update last seen
 */
async function updateLastSeen(deviceId) {
    try {
        await db.query(`
            UPDATE devices 
            SET last_seen = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
            WHERE id = $1
        `, [deviceId]);
        
        await redis.hset(`device:${deviceId}`, 'last_seen', new Date().toISOString());
        
    } catch (error) {
        logger.error(`Error updating last seen: ${error.message}`);
    }
}

/**
 * Check device heartbeat
 */
async function checkDeviceHeartbeat(imei) {
    try {
        const device = await validateIMEI(imei);
        if (!device) return;
        
        const lastSeen = await redis.hget(`device:${device.id}`, 'last_seen');
        
        if (lastSeen) {
            const diff = (new Date() - new Date(lastSeen)) / 1000;
            
            if (diff > config.device.offlineTimeout) {
                logger.warn(`Device ${imei} heartbeat timeout - marking offline`);
                await handleDeviceDisconnect(imei);
            }
        }
    } catch (error) {
        logger.error(`Heartbeat check error: ${error.message}`);
    }
}

/**
 * Handle device disconnect
 */
async function handleDeviceDisconnect(imei) {
    try {
        const device = await validateIMEI(imei);
        if (!device) return;
        
        await updateDeviceStatus(device.id, 'offline');
        await sessionManager.removeSession(imei);
        
        // Create offline alert
        await createOfflineAlert(device.id);
        
    } catch (error) {
        logger.error(`Disconnect handling error: ${error.message}`);
    }
}

/**
 * Create offline alert
 */
async function createOfflineAlert(deviceId) {
    try {
        const query = `
            INSERT INTO alert_events (
                id, rule_id, device_id, severity, message, status
            ) VALUES (
                uuid_generate_v4(),
                (SELECT id FROM alert_rules WHERE type = 'offline' AND is_global = true LIMIT 1),
                $1,
                'WARNING',
                'Device went offline',
                'ACTIVE'
            )
        `;
        
        await db.query(query, [deviceId]);
        
    } catch (error) {
        logger.error(`Error creating offline alert: ${error.message}`);
    }
}

/**
 * Send pending commands
 */
async function sendPendingCommands(deviceId) {
    try {
        const commands = await db.query(`
            SELECT cq.*, cl.command_text
            FROM command_queue cq
            JOIN command_logs cl ON cq.command_log_id = cl.id
            WHERE cq.device_id = $1 
            AND cq.status = 'QUEUED'
            AND (cq.execute_at <= CURRENT_TIMESTAMP OR cq.execute_at IS NULL)
            ORDER BY cq.priority DESC, cq.created_at ASC
            LIMIT 5
        `, [deviceId]);
        
        for (const cmd of commands.rows) {
            await commandSender.send(deviceId, cmd.command_text);
        }
        
    } catch (error) {
        logger.error(`Error sending pending commands: ${error.message}`);
    }
}

/**
 * Check alerts
 */
async function checkAlerts(deviceId, packet) {
    try {
        // Get active rules for this device
        const rules = await db.query(`
            SELECT ar.* 
            FROM alert_rules ar
            WHERE (ar.client_id = (SELECT client_id FROM devices WHERE id = $1) OR ar.is_global = true)
            AND ar.is_active = true
            AND ar.type IN ('overspeed', 'ignition')
        `, [deviceId]);
        
        for (const rule of rules.rows) {
            // Check overspeed
            if (rule.type === 'overspeed' && packet.speed > (rule.condition.speed || 120)) {
                await createAlert(deviceId, rule.id, {
                    speed: packet.speed,
                    limit: rule.condition.speed,
                    location: { lat: packet.latitude, lng: packet.longitude }
                });
            }
            
            // Check ignition change
            if (rule.type === 'ignition') {
                const lastIgnition = await redis.hget(`live:${deviceId}`, 'ignition');
                if (lastIgnition !== String(packet.ignition ? '1' : '0')) {
                    await createAlert(deviceId, rule.id, {
                        ignition: packet.ignition,
                        location: { lat: packet.latitude, lng: packet.longitude }
                    });
                }
            }
        }
        
    } catch (error) {
        logger.error(`Alert check error: ${error.message}`);
    }
}

/**
 * Create alert
 */
async function createAlert(deviceId, ruleId, details) {
    try {
        await db.query(`
            INSERT INTO alert_events (
                id, rule_id, device_id, severity, message, details, status
            ) VALUES (
                uuid_generate_v4(),
                $1,
                $2,
                'WARNING',
                $3,
                $4,
                'ACTIVE'
            )
        `, [ruleId, deviceId, `Alert triggered`, JSON.stringify(details)]);
        
    } catch (error) {
        logger.error(`Error creating alert: ${error.message}`);
    }
}

// Start server
server.listen(config.server.port, config.server.host, () => {
    logger.info(`TCP Server listening on ${config.server.host}:${config.server.port}`);
    logger.info('GT06 Protocol ready for connections');
});

// Handle server errors
server.on('error', (error) => {
    logger.error(`Server error: ${error.message}`);
    process.exit(1);
});

// Graceful shutdown
process.on('SIGTERM', gracefulShutdown);
process.on('SIGINT', gracefulShutdown);

async function gracefulShutdown() {
    logger.info('Received shutdown signal - closing connections...');
    
    // Close all device connections
    for (const [socket, info] of connectedDevices) {
        socket.end();
    }
    
    // Close server
    server.close(() => {
        logger.info('Server closed');
        
        // Close database connections
        db.end();
        
        // Close Redis
        redis.quit();
        
        process.exit(0);
    });
}

module.exports = { server, db, redis };
📁 File 6: /tcp-server/sessions/index.js
javascript
/**
 * Device Session Manager
 */

const Redis = require('ioredis');
const config = require('../config');

const redis = new Redis({
    host: config.redis.host,
    port: config.redis.port,
    password: config.redis.password,
    keyPrefix: 'session:'
});

class SessionManager {
    constructor() {
        this.sessions = new Map(); // imei -> session info
        this.socketMap = new Map(); // socket -> imei
    }

    /**
     * Create new session
     */
    async createSession({ deviceId, imei, socket, ip, modelId, protocol }) {
        const session = {
            deviceId,
            imei,
            ip,
            modelId,
            protocol,
            connectedAt: new Date(),
            lastActivity: new Date(),
            packetCount: 0
        };
        
        this.sessions.set(imei, session);
        this.socketMap.set(socket, imei);
        
        // Store in Redis
        await redis.hmset(imei, {
            deviceId,
            ip,
            modelId,
            protocol,
            connectedAt: session.connectedAt.toISOString()
        });
        
        return session;
    }

    /**
     * Get session by IMEI
     */
    getSession(imei) {
        return this.sessions.get(imei);
    }

    /**
     * Get IMEI by socket
     */
    getImeiBySocket(socket) {
        return this.socketMap.get(socket);
    }

    /**
     * Update session activity
     */
    async updateActivity(imei) {
        const session = this.sessions.get(imei);
        if (session) {
            session.lastActivity = new Date();
            session.packetCount++;
            
            await redis.hset(imei, 'lastActivity', session.lastActivity.toISOString());
            await redis.hset(imei, 'packetCount', session.packetCount);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Remove session
     */
    async removeSession(imei) {
        const session = this.sessions.get(imei);
        if (session) {
            this.sessions.delete(imei);
            
            // Find and remove socket mapping
            for (const [socket, sockImei] of this.socketMap) {
                if (sockImei === imei) {
                    this.socketMap.delete(socket);
                    break;
                }
            }
            
            // Remove from Redis
            await redis.del(imei);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get all online devices
     */
    getOnlineDevices() {
        return Array.from(this.sessions.keys());
    }

    /**
     * Get session count
     */
    getSessionCount() {
        return this.sessions.size;
    }

    /**
     * Get socket by IMEI
     */
    getSocketByImei(imei) {
        for (const [socket, sockImei] of this.socketMap) {
            if (sockImei === imei) {
                return socket;
            }
        }
        return null;
    }
}

module.exports = new SessionManager();
📁 File 7: /tcp-server/command_sender/index.js
javascript
/**
 * Command Sender
 */

const sessionManager = require('../sessions');
const gt06 = require('../protocols/gt06');
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const config = require('../config');

const db = new Pool({
    host: config.database.host,
    port: config.database.port,
    database: config.database.name,
    user: config.database.user,
    password: config.database.password
});

class CommandSender {
    constructor() {
        this.pendingCommands = new Map(); // commandId -> timeout
    }

    /**
     * Send command to device
     */
    async send(deviceId, command, commandLogId = null) {
        try {
            // Get device info
            const device = await this.getDeviceInfo(deviceId);
            if (!device) {
                throw new Error('Device not found');
            }
            
            // Get socket
            const socket = sessionManager.getSocketByImei(device.imei);
            if (!socket) {
                // Device offline - queue command
                await this.queueCommand(deviceId, command, commandLogId);
                return { queued: true };
            }
            
            // Create device-specific command
            const commandBuffer = this.createCommand(device.protocol, command);
            
            // Send to device
            socket.write(commandBuffer);
            
            // Update command log
            if (commandLogId) {
                await this.updateCommandLog(commandLogId, 'SENT');
            }
            
            // Set timeout for ACK
            const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
                this.handleTimeout(commandLogId, deviceId);
            }, config.device.ackTimeout * 1000);
            
            if (commandLogId) {
                this.pendingCommands.set(commandLogId, timeout);
            }
            
            return { sent: true };
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Command send error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Queue command for offline device
     */
    async queueCommand(deviceId, command, commandLogId) {
        try {
            await db.query(`
                UPDATE command_queue 
                SET status = 'QUEUED'
                WHERE command_log_id = $1
            `, [commandLogId]);
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Queue command error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Handle command timeout
     */
    async handleTimeout(commandLogId, deviceId) {
        try {
            this.pendingCommands.delete(commandLogId);
            
            // Update command log
            await db.query(`
                UPDATE command_logs 
                SET status = 'TIMEOUT', 
                    completed_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $1
            `, [commandLogId]);
            
            // Check if retry needed
            const retryCount = await this.getRetryCount(commandLogId);
            if (retryCount < config.device.maxRetries) {
                await this.retryCommand(commandLogId, deviceId);
            }
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Timeout handling error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Retry command
     */
    async retryCommand(commandLogId, deviceId) {
        try {
            await db.query(`
                INSERT INTO command_queue (device_id, command_log_id, priority, status)
                VALUES ($1, $2, 1, 'QUEUED')
            `, [deviceId, commandLogId]);
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Retry command error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get device info
     */
    async getDeviceInfo(deviceId) {
        try {
            const result = await db.query(`
                SELECT d.id, d.imei, dm.protocol
                FROM devices d
                JOIN device_models dm ON d.model_id = dm.id
                WHERE d.id = $1
            `, [deviceId]);
            
            return result.rows[0];
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get device info error:', error);
            return null;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Create device-specific command
     */
    createCommand(protocol, command) {
        switch(protocol) {
            case 'GT06':
                return gt06.createCommand(command, Math.floor(Math.random() * 65535));
            default:
                return Buffer.from(command, 'ascii');
        }
    }

    /**
     * Update command log
     */
    async updateCommandLog(commandLogId, status) {
        try {
            await db.query(`
                UPDATE command_logs 
                SET status = $1,
                    ${status === 'SENT' ? 'sent_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP' : ''}
                WHERE id = $2
            `, [status, commandLogId]);
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Update command log error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get retry count
     */
    async getRetryCount(commandLogId) {
        try {
            const result = await db.query(`
                SELECT attempt_count FROM command_logs WHERE id = $1
            `, [commandLogId]);
            
            return result.rows[0]?.attempt_count || 0;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get retry count error:', error);
            return 0;
        }
    }
}

module.exports = new CommandSender();
