📦 File 1: /backend/services/command-mapper.service.js
javascript
/**
 * Command Mapper Service
 * Maps logical commands to device-specific commands (File 11, Step 2)
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);

class CommandMapperService {
    /**
     * Get actual command for device model
     */
    async getActualCommand(deviceModelId, logicalCommand, parameters = {}) {
        try {
            // Try cache first
            const cacheKey = `cmd:map:${deviceModelId}:${logicalCommand}`;
            let cached = await redis.get(cacheKey);
            
            if (cached) {
                return JSON.parse(cached);
            }
            
            // Get from database
            const result = await pool.query(`
                SELECT dcm.*, lc.name as logical_name, lc.requires_otp, lc.safety_check_required
                FROM device_command_map dcm
                JOIN logical_commands lc ON dcm.logical_command_id = lc.id
                WHERE dcm.device_model_id = $1
                AND lc.name = $2
                AND dcm.is_active = true
            `, [deviceModelId, logicalCommand]);
            
            if (result.rows.length === 0) {
                throw new Error(`No command mapping found for ${logicalCommand}`);
            }
            
            const mapping = result.rows[0];
            
            // Format command with parameters
            let actualCommand = mapping.actual_command;
            if (parameters && Object.keys(parameters).length > 0) {
                Object.keys(parameters).forEach(key => {
                    actualCommand = actualCommand.replace(`{${key}}`, parameters[key]);
                });
            }
            
            const response = {
                command: actualCommand,
                requiresOtp: mapping.requires_otp,
                requiresSafetyCheck: mapping.safety_check_required,
                timeoutSeconds: mapping.timeout_seconds || 30,
                retryCount: mapping.retry_count || 3
            };
            
            // Cache for 1 hour
            await redis.setex(cacheKey, 3600, JSON.stringify(response));
            
            return response;
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Command mapping error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get all supported commands for device
     */
    async getDeviceCommands(deviceModelId) {
        try {
            const result = await pool.query(`
                SELECT lc.name, lc.category, lc.description, 
                       lc.requires_otp, lc.safety_check_required,
                       dcm.actual_command
                FROM logical_commands lc
                JOIN device_command_map dcm ON lc.id = dcm.logical_command_id
                WHERE dcm.device_model_id = $1
                AND dcm.is_active = true
                ORDER BY lc.category, lc.name
            `, [deviceModelId]);
            
            return result.rows;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get device commands error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }
}

module.exports = new CommandMapperService();
🛡️ File 2: /backend/services/safety.service.js
javascript
/**
 * Safety Rules Service (File 11, Step 4)
 * Enforces command safety rules
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);

class SafetyService {
    /**
     * Check if command is safe to execute
     */
    async checkSafety(deviceId, commandName, userId) {
        try {
            // Get device and vehicle state
            const device = await this.getDeviceState(deviceId);
            
            // Get user permissions
            const user = await this.getUserPermissions(userId, device.client_id);
            
            const checks = {
                passed: true,
                failures: []
            };

            // Check 1: Global kill switch (File 16)
            const globalKill = await redis.get('global:ignition_disabled');
            if (globalKill === 'true' && commandName.includes('IGNITION')) {
                checks.passed = false;
                checks.failures.push('Global ignition kill switch is active');
            }

            // Check 2: User permission
            if (!user.canSendCommands) {
                checks.passed = false;
                checks.failures.push('User does not have command permission');
            }

            // Check 3: Client permission for ignition commands
            if (commandName.includes('IGNITION')) {
                const clientAllowed = await this.checkClientIgnitionPermission(device.client_id);
                if (!clientAllowed) {
                    checks.passed = false;
                    checks.failures.push('Client not allowed to control ignition');
                }
            }

            // Check 4: Speed check for ignition off (File 11, Step 4)
            if (commandName === 'IGNITION_OFF') {
                const liveData = await this.getLiveData(deviceId);
                if (liveData.speed > 5) { // > 5 km/h
                    checks.passed = false;
                    checks.failures.push(`Cannot turn off ignition at speed ${liveData.speed} km/h`);
                }
                
                if (!liveData.ignition) {
                    checks.passed = false;
                    checks.failures.push('Ignition is already OFF');
                }
            }

            // Check 5: Speed check for ignition on
            if (commandName === 'IGNITION_ON') {
                const liveData = await this.getLiveData(deviceId);
                if (liveData.speed > 5) {
                    checks.passed = false;
                    checks.failures.push(`Cannot turn on ignition at speed ${liveData.speed} km/h`);
                }
                
                if (liveData.ignition) {
                    checks.passed = false;
                    checks.failures.push('Ignition is already ON');
                }
            }

            // Check 6: Device online
            if (device.status !== 'online') {
                checks.passed = false;
                checks.failures.push('Device is offline');
            }

            // Check 7: Subscription active
            if (!device.is_subscription_active) {
                checks.passed = false;
                checks.failures.push('Device subscription is inactive');
            }

            // Log safety check
            await this.logSafetyCheck(deviceId, commandName, userId, checks);

            return checks;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Safety check error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Verify OTP for command
     */
    async verifyOtp(deviceId, commandName, userId, otp) {
        try {
            // Get stored OTP from Redis
            const storedOtp = await redis.get(`otp:${deviceId}:${commandName}:${userId}`);
            
            if (!storedOtp || storedOtp !== otp) {
                return { valid: false, message: 'Invalid OTP' };
            }
            
            // Check expiry
            const ttl = await redis.ttl(`otp:${deviceId}:${commandName}:${userId}`);
            if (ttl < 0) {
                return { valid: false, message: 'OTP expired' };
            }
            
            // Delete used OTP
            await redis.del(`otp:${deviceId}:${commandName}:${userId}`);
            
            return { valid: true };
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('OTP verification error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Generate OTP for command
     */
    async generateOtp(deviceId, commandName, userId) {
        const otp = Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000).toString(); // 6-digit
        
        // Store in Redis with 5 minute expiry
        await redis.setex(`otp:${deviceId}:${commandName}:${userId}`, 300, otp);
        
        // Log OTP generation
        await pool.query(`
            INSERT INTO audit_logs (user_id, action, details)
            VALUES ($1, 'OTP_GENERATED', $2)
        `, [userId, JSON.stringify({ deviceId, commandName })]);
        
        return otp;
    }

    /**
     * Get device state
     */
    async getDeviceState(deviceId) {
        const result = await pool.query(`
            SELECT d.*, c.id as client_id
            FROM devices d
            LEFT JOIN clients c ON d.client_id = c.id
            WHERE d.id = $1
        `, [deviceId]);
        
        return result.rows[0];
    }

    /**
     * Get user permissions
     */
    async getUserPermissions(userId, clientId) {
        const result = await pool.query(`
            SELECT 
                u.*,
                bool_or(r.permissions->>'send_commands') as can_send_commands,
                bool_or(r.permissions->>'send_ignition_commands') as can_send_ignition
            FROM users u
            JOIN user_roles ur ON u.id = ur.user_id
            JOIN roles r ON ur.role_id = r.id
            WHERE u.id = $1
            GROUP BY u.id
        `, [userId]);
        
        const user = result.rows[0];
        
        return {
            canSendCommands: user.can_send_commands || false,
            canSendIgnition: user.can_send_ignition || false,
            isClient: user.id === clientId
        };
    }

    /**
     * Check if client allowed to control ignition
     */
    async checkClientIgnitionPermission(clientId) {
        const result = await pool.query(`
            SELECT settings->>'allow_client_ignition' as allow_ignition
            FROM clients
            WHERE id = $1
        `, [clientId]);
        
        return result.rows[0]?.allow_ignition === 'true';
    }

    /**
     * Get live data
     */
    async getLiveData(deviceId) {
        // Try Redis first
        const cached = await redis.hgetall(`live:${deviceId}`);
        if (cached && cached.lat) {
            return {
                speed: parseFloat(cached.speed) || 0,
                ignition: cached.ignition === '1'
            };
        }
        
        // Fallback to database
        const result = await pool.query(`
            SELECT speed, ignition
            FROM gps_live_data
            WHERE device_id = $1
        `, [deviceId]);
        
        return result.rows[0] || { speed: 0, ignition: false };
    }

    /**
     * Log safety check
     */
    async logSafetyCheck(deviceId, commandName, userId, checks) {
        await pool.query(`
            INSERT INTO audit_logs (user_id, action, entity_type, entity_id, details)
            VALUES ($1, 'SAFETY_CHECK', 'COMMAND', $2, $3)
        `, [userId, deviceId, JSON.stringify({
            command: commandName,
            passed: checks.passed,
            failures: checks.failures,
            timestamp: new Date()
        })]);
    }
}

module.exports = new SafetyService();
⚙️ File 3: /backend/services/command.service.js
javascript
/**
 * Main Command Service (File 11, Step 3)
 * Handles command execution flow
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

const commandMapper = require('./command-mapper.service');
const safetyService = require('./safety.service');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);

class CommandService {
    /**
     * Execute command (main entry point)
     */
    async executeCommand(deviceId, commandName, userId, options = {}) {
        const commandLogId = uuidv4();
        
        try {
            // Step 1: Get device info
            const device = await this.getDevice(deviceId);
            if (!device) {
                throw new Error('Device not found');
            }

            // Step 2: Get actual command from mapper
            const mapping = await commandMapper.getActualCommand(
                device.model_id, 
                commandName,
                options.parameters || {}
            );

            // Step 3: Safety checks
            if (mapping.requiresSafetyCheck) {
                const safety = await safetyService.checkSafety(deviceId, commandName, userId);
                if (!safety.passed) {
                    await this.logCommand({
                        id: commandLogId,
                        deviceId,
                        commandName,
                        actualCommand: mapping.command,
                        userId,
                        status: 'REJECTED',
                        error: safety.failures.join(', '),
                        metadata: options
                    });
                    
                    return {
                        success: false,
                        status: 'REJECTED',
                        errors: safety.failures
                    };
                }
            }

            // Step 4: OTP verification if required
            let otpVerified = false;
            if (mapping.requiresOtp) {
                if (!options.otp) {
                    // Generate and send OTP
                    const otp = await safetyService.generateOtp(deviceId, commandName, userId);
                    
                    // Store OTP in Redis
                    await redis.setex(`cmd:otp:${commandLogId}`, 300, otp);
                    
                    // Send OTP to user (via push, SMS, etc.)
                    await this.sendOtpToUser(userId, otp, deviceId);
                    
                    return {
                        success: true,
                        status: 'OTP_REQUIRED',
                        commandLogId,
                        message: 'OTP sent for verification'
                    };
                } else {
                    // Verify OTP
                    const otpCheck = await safetyService.verifyOtp(deviceId, commandName, userId, options.otp);
                    if (!otpCheck.valid) {
                        return {
                            success: false,
                            status: 'OTP_INVALID',
                            message: otpCheck.message
                        };
                    }
                    otpVerified = true;
                }
            }

            // Step 5: Create command log
            const commandLog = await this.createCommandLog({
                id: commandLogId,
                deviceId,
                commandName,
                actualCommand: mapping.command,
                userId,
                otpVerified,
                metadata: options,
                safetyChecks: mapping.requiresSafetyCheck ? true : null
            });

            // Step 6: Queue command
            await this.queueCommand({
                commandLogId,
                deviceId,
                command: mapping.command,
                timeoutSeconds: mapping.timeoutSeconds,
                maxRetries: mapping.retryCount
            });

            return {
                success: true,
                status: 'QUEUED',
                commandLogId,
                message: 'Command queued for execution'
            };

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Command execution error:', error);
            
            await this.logCommand({
                id: commandLogId,
                deviceId,
                commandName,
                userId,
                status: 'ERROR',
                error: error.message,
                metadata: options
            });
            
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get command status
     */
    async getCommandStatus(commandLogId) {
        const result = await pool.query(`
            SELECT 
                cl.*,
                d.imei,
                d.name as device_name
            FROM command_logs cl
            JOIN devices d ON cl.device_id = d.id
            WHERE cl.id = $1
        `, [commandLogId]);
        
        return result.rows[0];
    }

    /**
     * Get device
     */
    async getDevice(deviceId) {
        const result = await pool.query(`
            SELECT d.*, dm.protocol, dm.name as model_name
            FROM devices d
            JOIN device_models dm ON d.model_id = dm.id
            WHERE d.id = $1
        `, [deviceId]);
        
        return result.rows[0];
    }

    /**
     * Create command log
     */
    async createCommandLog({ id, deviceId, commandName, actualCommand, userId, otpVerified, metadata, safetyChecks }) {
        const query = `
            INSERT INTO command_logs (
                id, device_id, logical_command_id, command_text, 
                requested_by, otp_verified, safety_checks_passed,
                status, parameters, created_at
            ) VALUES (
                $1, $2, 
                (SELECT id FROM logical_commands WHERE name = $3),
                $4, $5, $6, $7, 'PENDING', $8, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
            )
            RETURNING id
        `;
        
        await pool.query(query, [
            id,
            deviceId,
            commandName,
            actualCommand,
            userId,
            otpVerified,
            safetyChecks,
            JSON.stringify(metadata)
        ]);
        
        return { id };
    }

    /**
     * Queue command
     */
    async queueCommand({ commandLogId, deviceId, command, timeoutSeconds, maxRetries }) {
        const query = `
            INSERT INTO command_queue (
                id, device_id, command_log_id, status, 
                execute_at, expires_at
            ) VALUES (
                uuid_generate_v4(), $1, $2, 'QUEUED',
                CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
                CURRENT_TIMESTAMP + interval '${timeoutSeconds} seconds'
            )
        `;
        
        await pool.query(query, [deviceId, commandLogId]);
        
        // Publish to Redis for real-time processing
        await redis.publish('command:queue', JSON.stringify({
            commandLogId,
            deviceId,
            command
        }));
    }

    /**
     * Send OTP to user
     */
    async sendOtpToUser(userId, otp, deviceId) {
        // Get user notification preferences
        const user = await pool.query(`
            SELECT email, phone, notification_preferences
            FROM users WHERE id = $1
        `, [userId]);
        
        const prefs = user.rows[0]?.notification_preferences || {};
        
        // Send via push (if app installed)
        if (prefs.push) {
            await redis.publish('notification:push', JSON.stringify({
                userId,
                title: 'Command OTP',
                body: `Your OTP for command is: ${otp}`,
                data: { deviceId, otp }
            }));
        }
        
        // Send via SMS (if phone available)
        if (prefs.sms && user.rows[0]?.phone) {
            await redis.publish('notification:sms', JSON.stringify({
                phone: user.rows[0].phone,
                message: `Your OTP for GPS command is: ${otp}`
            }));
        }
        
        // Send via email (if email available)
        if (prefs.email && user.rows[0]?.email) {
            await redis.publish('notification:email', JSON.stringify({
                email: user.rows[0].email,
                subject: 'Command OTP',
                body: `Your OTP for command is: ${otp}`
            }));
        }
    }

    /**
     * Log command (for error cases)
     */
    async logCommand({ id, deviceId, commandName, actualCommand, userId, status, error, metadata }) {
        try {
            const query = `
                INSERT INTO command_logs (
                    id, device_id, logical_command_id, command_text,
                    requested_by, status, error_message, parameters, created_at
                ) VALUES (
                    $1, $2, 
                    (SELECT id FROM logical_commands WHERE name = $3),
                    $4, $5, $6, $7, $8, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                )
            `;
            
            await pool.query(query, [
                id || uuidv4(),
                deviceId,
                commandName,
                actualCommand || '',
                userId,
                status,
                error,
                JSON.stringify(metadata || {})
            ]);
        } catch (err) {
            console.error('Error logging command:', err);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Handle command ACK from device
     */
    async handleCommandAck(deviceId, commandLogId, success, response = null) {
        try {
            const status = success ? 'SUCCESS' : 'FAILED';
            
            await pool.query(`
                UPDATE command_logs 
                SET status = $1,
                    ack_received = true,
                    ack_data = $2,
                    completed_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $3
            `, [status, response ? JSON.stringify(response) : null, commandLogId]);
            
            // Remove from queue
            await pool.query(`
                DELETE FROM command_queue 
                WHERE command_log_id = $1
            `, [commandLogId]);
            
            // Notify user
            await this.notifyCommandResult(commandLogId, status);
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error handling command ACK:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Notify user of command result
     */
    async notifyCommandResult(commandLogId, status) {
        const result = await pool.query(`
            SELECT cl.*, u.id as user_id
            FROM command_logs cl
            JOIN users u ON cl.requested_by = u.id
            WHERE cl.id = $1
        `, [commandLogId]);
        
        if (result.rows[0]) {
            await redis.publish('notification:push', JSON.stringify({
                userId: result.rows[0].user_id,
                title: 'Command Executed',
                body: `Command ${status}`,
                data: { commandLogId, status }
            }));
        }
    }
}

module.exports = new CommandService();
🔄 File 4: /backend/jobs/command-processor.js
javascript
/**
 * Command Queue Processor
 * Runs as background job to process queued commands
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const commandService = require('../services/command.service');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);

class CommandProcessor {
    constructor() {
        this.isRunning = false;
        this.processingInterval = null;
    }

    /**
     * Start the processor
     */
    start() {
        if (this.isRunning) return;
        
        this.isRunning = true;
        console.log('Command processor started');
        
        // Process every 5 seconds
        this.processingInterval = setInterval(() => {
            this.processQueue();
        }, 5000);
        
        // Also listen for real-time events
        this.listenForCommands();
    }

    /**
     * Stop the processor
     */
    stop() {
        this.isRunning = false;
        if (this.processingInterval) {
            clearInterval(this.processingInterval);
        }
        console.log('Command processor stopped');
    }

    /**
     * Process command queue
     */
    async processQueue() {
        try {
            // Get pending commands
            const commands = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    cq.id as queue_id,
                    cq.device_id,
                    cq.command_log_id,
                    cl.command_text,
                    cl.attempt_count,
                    d.imei,
                    d.status as device_status,
                    dm.protocol
                FROM command_queue cq
                JOIN command_logs cl ON cq.command_log_id = cl.id
                JOIN devices d ON cq.device_id = d.id
                JOIN device_models dm ON d.model_id = dm.id
                WHERE cq.status = 'QUEUED'
                AND (cq.execute_at <= CURRENT_TIMESTAMP OR cq.execute_at IS NULL)
                AND cq.expires_at > CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                ORDER BY cq.priority DESC, cq.created_at ASC
                LIMIT 50
            `);

            for (const cmd of commands.rows) {
                await this.sendCommand(cmd);
            }

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Queue processing error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Listen for real-time commands via Redis
     */
    listenForCommands() {
        redis.subscribe('command:queue', (err, count) => {
            if (err) {
                console.error('Failed to subscribe:', err);
                return;
            }
            console.log('Subscribed to command:queue');
        });

        redis.on('message', (channel, message) => {
            if (channel === 'command:queue') {
                const cmd = JSON.parse(message);
                this.processImmediate(cmd);
            }
        });
    }

    /**
     * Process immediate command
     */
    async processImmediate(cmd) {
        try {
            const commandData = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    cq.id as queue_id,
                    cq.device_id,
                    cq.command_log_id,
                    cl.command_text,
                    cl.attempt_count,
                    d.imei,
                    d.status as device_status,
                    dm.protocol
                FROM command_queue cq
                JOIN command_logs cl ON cq.command_log_id = cl.id
                JOIN devices d ON cq.device_id = d.id
                JOIN device_models dm ON d.model_id = dm.id
                WHERE cq.command_log_id = $1
            `, [cmd.commandLogId]);

            if (commandData.rows[0]) {
                await this.sendCommand(commandData.rows[0]);
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Immediate command error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send command to device via TCP server
     */
    async sendCommand(cmd) {
        try {
            // Check if device is online
            if (cmd.device_status !== 'online') {
                // Device offline - will retry later
                console.log(`Device ${cmd.imei} offline, command queued`);
                return;
            }

            // Update attempt count
            await pool.query(`
                UPDATE command_logs 
                SET attempt_count = attempt_count + 1,
                    last_attempt = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $1
            `, [cmd.command_log_id]);

            // Publish to TCP server via Redis
            await redis.publish('tcp:command:send', JSON.stringify({
                deviceId: cmd.device_id,
                imei: cmd.imei,
                command: cmd.command_text,
                protocol: cmd.protocol,
                commandLogId: cmd.command_log_id
            }));

            // Update queue status
            await pool.query(`
                UPDATE command_queue 
                SET status = 'SENT',
                    last_attempt = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $1
            `, [cmd.queue_id]);

            console.log(`Command sent to ${cmd.imei}: ${cmd.command_text}`);

        } catch (error) {
            console.error(`Error sending command to ${cmd.imei}:`, error);

            // Update status to failed
            await pool.query(`
                UPDATE command_logs 
                SET status = 'FAILED',
                    error_message = $1,
                    completed_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $2
            `, [error.message, cmd.command_log_id]);

            await pool.query(`
                UPDATE command_queue 
                SET status = 'FAILED'
                WHERE command_log_id = $1
            `, [cmd.command_log_id]);
        }
    }
}

module.exports = new CommandProcessor();
🌐 File 5: /backend/api/routes/commands.js

/**
 * Command API Routes
 */

const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const commandService = require('../../services/command.service');
const auth = require('../../middlewares/auth');
const rateLimit = require('../../middlewares/rate-limit');

// Rate limiting for commands (sensitive operations)
const commandLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 10 // 10 commands per 15 minutes
});

/**
 * Send command to device
 * POST /api/v1/commands/send
 */
router.post('/send', auth, commandLimiter, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { deviceId, command, parameters, otp } = req.body;
        
        // Validate required fields
        if (!deviceId || !command) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                error: 'deviceId and command are required'
            });
        }

        // Execute command
        const result = await commandService.executeCommand(
            deviceId,
            command,
            req.user.id,
            { parameters, otp, ip: req.ip, userAgent: req.headers['user-agent'] }
        );

        res.json(result);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Command API error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            error: error.message || 'Failed to send command'
        });
    }
});

/**
 * Get command status
 * GET /api/v1/commands/:commandLogId
 */
router.get('/:commandLogId', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const status = await commandService.getCommandStatus(req.params.commandLogId);
        
        if (!status) {
            return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Command not found' });
        }

        res.json(status);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Get command status error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get command status' });
    }
});

/**
 * Get device commands (supported commands for device)
 * GET /api/v1/commands/device/:deviceId
 */
router.get('/device/:deviceId', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        // Get device model
        const device = await commandService.getDevice(req.params.deviceId);
        
        if (!device) {
            return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Device not found' });
        }

        // Get supported commands
        const commands = await commandMapper.getDeviceCommands(device.model_id);

        res.json(commands);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Get device commands error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get device commands' });
    }
});

/**
 * Get command history for device
 * GET /api/v1/commands/history/:deviceId
 */
router.get('/history/:deviceId', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { limit = 50, offset = 0 } = req.query;
        
        const result = await pool.query(`
            SELECT 
                cl.*,
                lc.name as command_name,
                u.email as requested_by_email
            FROM command_logs cl
            JOIN logical_commands lc ON cl.logical_command_id = lc.id
            LEFT JOIN users u ON cl.requested_by = u.id
            WHERE cl.device_id = $1
            ORDER BY cl.created_at DESC
            LIMIT $2 OFFSET $3
        `, [req.params.deviceId, limit, offset]);

        res.json(result.rows);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Command history error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get command history' });
    }
});

module.exports = router;
📝 File 6: /tcp-server/ack_handler/index.js (Update TCP Server)
Add this to your TCP server to handle command ACKs:

javascript
/**
 * Command ACK Handler
 * Add to your TCP server
 */

const Redis = require('ioredis');
const { Pool } = require('pg');

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);
const pool = new Pool({ connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL });

class AckHandler {
    /**
     * Handle command response from device
     */
    async handle(imei, response) {
        try {
            // Find pending command for this device
            const pendingCmd = await pool.query(`
                SELECT cq.*, cl.id as command_log_id
                FROM command_queue cq
                JOIN command_logs cl ON cq.command_log_id = cl.id
                JOIN devices d ON cq.device_id = d.id
                WHERE d.imei = $1 
                AND cq.status = 'SENT'
                ORDER BY cq.created_at DESC
                LIMIT 1
            `, [imei]);

            if (pendingCmd.rows.length === 0) {
                console.log(`No pending command for ${imei}`);
                return;
            }

            const cmd = pendingCmd.rows[0];

            // Check if response indicates success
            const success = this.isSuccessResponse(response);

            // Update command log
            await pool.query(`
                UPDATE command_logs 
                SET status = $1,
                    ack_received = true,
                    ack_data = $2,
                    completed_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $3
            `, [success ? 'SUCCESS' : 'FAILED', JSON.stringify(response), cmd.command_log_id]);

            // Remove from queue
            await pool.query(`
                DELETE FROM command_queue 
                WHERE command_log_id = $1
            `, [cmd.command_log_id]);

            // Publish result
            await redis.publish('command:result', JSON.stringify({
                commandLogId: cmd.command_log_id,
                success,
                response
            }));

            console.log(`Command ${cmd.command_log_id} completed with ${success ? 'SUCCESS' : 'FAILURE'}`);

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('ACK handling error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Check if response indicates success
     */
    isSuccessResponse(response) {
        // GT06 success patterns
        if (response.type === 'COMMAND_RESPONSE') {
            const data = response.data?.toLowerCase() || '';
            return data.includes('ok') || data.includes('success') || data === '1';
        }
        return false;
    }
}

module.exports = new AckHandler();

const axios = require('axios');

async function testIgnitionOff() {

            {
                deviceId: 'your-device-uuid',
                command: 'IGNITION_OFF',
                otp: '123456' // if required
            },

        );

        console.error('Test failed:', error.response?.data || error.message);
    }
}

/**
 * Alert Evaluator Service
 * Evaluates rules against GPS data (File 12)
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);

class AlertEvaluatorService {
    /**
     * Evaluate all rules for a device
     */
    async evaluate(deviceId, gpsData) {
        try {
            // Get active rules for this device
            const rules = await this.getDeviceRules(deviceId);
            
            const triggeredAlerts = [];

            for (const rule of rules) {
                // Check cooldown
                if (await this.inCooldown(deviceId, rule.id)) {
                    continue;
                }

                // Check time window
                if (!this.isInTimeWindow(rule)) {
                    continue;
                }

                // Evaluate rule condition
                const triggered = await this.evaluateRule(rule, gpsData, deviceId);
                
                if (triggered) {
                    triggeredAlerts.push({
                        ruleId: rule.id,
                        deviceId,
                        severity: rule.severity,
                        details: triggered.details,
                        value: triggered.value
                    });
                    
                    // Set cooldown
                    await this.setCooldown(deviceId, rule.id, rule.cooldown_minutes);
                }
            }

            return triggeredAlerts;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Alert evaluation error:', error);
            return [];
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get active rules for device
     */
    async getDeviceRules(deviceId) {
        try {
            // Get device's client and vehicle
            const device = await pool.query(`
                SELECT client_id, vehicle_id 
                FROM devices 
                WHERE id = $1
            `, [deviceId]);

            const clientId = device.rows[0]?.client_id;
            const vehicleId = device.rows[0]?.vehicle_id;

            // Get all applicable rules
            const rules = await pool.query(`
                SELECT * FROM alert_rules 
                WHERE is_active = true 
                AND (
                    client_id = $1 
                    OR vehicle_id = $2 
                    OR (is_global = true AND client_id IS NULL)
                )
            `, [clientId, vehicleId]);

            return rules.rows;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get device rules error:', error);
            return [];
        }
    }

    /**
     * Evaluate single rule
     */
    async evaluateRule(rule, gpsData, deviceId) {
        const condition = rule.condition;
        const type = rule.type;

        switch(type) {
            case 'overspeed':
                return this.evaluateOverspeed(condition, gpsData);
                
            case 'offline':
                return this.evaluateOffline(condition, deviceId);
                
            case 'ignition':
                return this.evaluateIgnition(condition, gpsData, deviceId);
                
            case 'geofence':
                return this.evaluateGeofence(condition, gpsData, deviceId);
                
            case 'fuel_drop':
                return this.evaluateFuelDrop(condition, gpsData, deviceId);
                
            case 'battery':
                return this.evaluateBattery(condition, gpsData);
                
            case 'tamper':
                return this.evaluateTamper(condition, gpsData, deviceId);
                
            case 'maintenance':
                return this.evaluateMaintenance(condition, deviceId);
                
            default:
                return null;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Overspeed alert
     */
    async evaluateOverspeed(condition, gpsData) {
        const speedLimit = condition.speed || 120;
        
        if (gpsData.speed > speedLimit) {
            return {
                triggered: true,
                details: {
                    speed: gpsData.speed,
                    limit: speedLimit,
                    location: { lat: gpsData.latitude, lng: gpsData.longitude }
                },
                value: gpsData.speed
            };
        }
        return null;
    }

    /**
     * Offline alert
     */
    async evaluateOffline(condition, deviceId) {
        const timeoutMinutes = condition.timeout_minutes || 10;
        
        // Get last seen from Redis
        const lastSeen = await redis.hget(`device:${deviceId}`, 'last_seen');
        
        if (lastSeen) {
            const minutesSinceLastSeen = (Date.now() - new Date(lastSeen)) / (1000 * 60);
            
            if (minutesSinceLastSeen > timeoutMinutes) {
                return {
                    triggered: true,
                    details: {
                        minutes_offline: Math.round(minutesSinceLastSeen),
                        timeout: timeoutMinutes
                    },
                    value: minutesSinceLastSeen
                };
            }
        }
        return null;
    }

    /**
     * Ignition alert
     */
    async evaluateIgnition(condition, gpsData, deviceId) {
        // Get previous ignition state
        const prevState = await redis.hget(`live:${deviceId}`, 'ignition');
        const currentIgnition = gpsData.ignition ? '1' : '0';
        
        if (condition.on_change && prevState !== currentIgnition) {
            return {
                triggered: true,
                details: {
                    previous: prevState === '1',
                    current: gpsData.ignition,
                    location: { lat: gpsData.latitude, lng: gpsData.longitude }
                },
                value: gpsData.ignition ? 'ON' : 'OFF'
            };
        }
        
        if (condition.status !== undefined && gpsData.ignition === condition.status) {
            return {
                triggered: true,
                details: {
                    status: gpsData.ignition ? 'ON' : 'OFF',
                    location: { lat: gpsData.latitude, lng: gpsData.longitude }
                },
                value: gpsData.ignition ? 'ON' : 'OFF'
            };
        }
        
        return null;
    }

    /**
     * Geofence alert
     */
    async evaluateGeofence(condition, gpsData, deviceId) {
        // Get geofences for this device
        const geofences = await pool.query(`
            SELECT g.* 
            FROM geofences g
            JOIN devices d ON d.client_id = g.client_id
            WHERE d.id = $1 AND g.is_active = true
        `, [deviceId]);

        for (const geofence of geofences.rows) {
            const inside = this.pointInGeofence(
                { lat: gpsData.latitude, lng: gpsData.longitude },
                geofence
            );

            // Get previous state
            const wasInside = await redis.get(`geofence:${deviceId}:${geofence.id}`);

            if (inside && wasInside === 'false' && geofence.alert_on_enter) {
                await redis.set(`geofence:${deviceId}:${geofence.id}`, 'true');
                return {
                    triggered: true,
                    details: {
                        geofence: geofence.name,
                        action: 'ENTER',
                        location: { lat: gpsData.latitude, lng: gpsData.longitude }
                    },
                    value: 'ENTER'
                };
            }

            if (!inside && wasInside === 'true' && geofence.alert_on_exit) {
                await redis.set(`geofence:${deviceId}:${geofence.id}`, 'false');
                return {
                    triggered: true,
                    details: {
                        geofence: geofence.name,
                        action: 'EXIT',
                        location: { lat: gpsData.latitude, lng: gpsData.longitude }
                    },
                    value: 'EXIT'
                };
            }
        }

        return null;
    }

    /**
     * Fuel drop alert (potential theft)
     */
    async evaluateFuelDrop(condition, gpsData, deviceId) {
        const dropThreshold = condition.drop_percent || 15; // 15% drop
        
        // Get current fuel level
        const currentFuel = gpsData.fuel_level || 0;
        
        // Get previous fuel level from Redis
        const prevFuel = await redis.get(`fuel:${deviceId}`);
        
        if (prevFuel) {
            const dropPercent = ((prevFuel - currentFuel) / prevFuel) * 100;
            
            // Check if drop is sudden (within 5 minutes) and significant
            if (dropPercent > dropThreshold && gpsData.ignition === false) {
                return {
                    triggered: true,
                    details: {
                        previous: prevFuel,
                        current: currentFuel,
                        drop_percent: dropPercent,
                        location: { lat: gpsData.latitude, lng: gpsData.longitude }
                    },
                    value: dropPercent
                };
            }
        }
        
        // Update current fuel
        await redis.setex(`fuel:${deviceId}`, 300, currentFuel);
        
        return null;
    }

    /**
     * Battery low alert
     */
    evaluateBattery(condition, gpsData) {
        const minBattery = condition.min_battery || 20; // 20%
        
        if (gpsData.battery_level && gpsData.battery_level < minBattery && !gpsData.charging) {
            return {
                triggered: true,
                details: {
                    battery: gpsData.battery_level,
                    min: minBattery,
                    charging: gpsData.charging
                },
                value: gpsData.battery_level
            };
        }
        return null;
    }

    /**
     * Tamper alert (power cut)
     */
    async evaluateTamper(condition, gpsData, deviceId) {
        // Check if external power was lost
        if (gpsData.external_power === false) {
            // Check if battery is also discharging
            if (gpsData.battery_level && gpsData.battery_level < condition.min_battery || 50) {
                return {
                    triggered: true,
                    details: {
                        battery: gpsData.battery_level,
                        external_power: false,
                        location: { lat: gpsData.latitude, lng: gpsData.longitude }
                    },
                    value: 'POWER_CUT'
                };
            }
        }
        return null;
    }

    /**
     * Maintenance due alert
     */
    async evaluateMaintenance(condition, deviceId) {
        const daysBefore = condition.days_before || 7;
        
        const device = await pool.query(`
            SELECT next_maintenance_due, odometer_reading
            FROM devices WHERE id = $1
        `, [deviceId]);

        if (device.rows[0]?.next_maintenance_due) {
            const dueDate = new Date(device.rows[0].next_maintenance_due);
            const daysUntilDue = Math.ceil((dueDate - Date.now()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
            
            if (daysUntilDue <= daysBefore && daysUntilDue > 0) {
                return {
                    triggered: true,
                    details: {
                        days_remaining: daysUntilDue,
                        due_date: dueDate
                    },
                    value: daysUntilDue
                };
            }
        }
        
        return null;
    }

    /**
     * Check if point is inside geofence
     */
    pointInGeofence(point, geofence) {
        if (geofence.type === 'CIRCLE') {
            const distance = this.calculateDistance(
                point.lat, point.lng,
                geofence.center_latitude, geofence.center_longitude
            );
            return distance <= geofence.radius_meters;
        }
        
        // For polygon, use ray casting algorithm
        if (geofence.type === 'POLYGON' && geofence.polygon_coordinates) {
            return this.pointInPolygon(point, geofence.polygon_coordinates);
        }
        
        return false;
    }

    /**
     * Calculate distance between two points (Haversine formula)
     */
    calculateDistance(lat1, lon1, lat2, lon2) {
        const R = 6371e3; // Earth's radius in meters
        const φ1 = lat1 * Math.PI / 180;
        const φ2 = lat2 * Math.PI / 180;
        const Δφ = (lat2 - lat1) * Math.PI / 180;
        const Δλ = (lon2 - lon1) * Math.PI / 180;

        const a = Math.sin(Δφ / 2) * Math.sin(Δφ / 2) +
                Math.cos(φ1) * Math.cos(φ2) *
                Math.sin(Δλ / 2) * Math.sin(Δλ / 2);
        const c = 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1 - a));

        return R * c;
    }

    /**
     * Point in polygon test
     */
    pointInPolygon(point, polygon) {
        // Ray casting algorithm
        let inside = false;
        for (let i = 0, j = polygon.length - 1; i < polygon.length; j = i++) {
            const xi = polygon[i][0], yi = polygon[i][1];
            const xj = polygon[j][0], yj = polygon[j][1];
            
            const intersect = ((yi > point.lat) !== (yj > point.lat)) &&
                (point.lng < (xj - xi) * (point.lat - yi) / (yj - yi) + xi);
            if (intersect) inside = !inside;
        }
        return inside;
    }

    /**
     * Check cooldown
     */
    async inCooldown(deviceId, ruleId) {
        const key = `cooldown:${deviceId}:${ruleId}`;
        const exists = await redis.exists(key);
        return exists === 1;
    }

    /**
     * Set cooldown
     */
    async setCooldown(deviceId, ruleId, minutes) {
        if (minutes > 0) {
            const key = `cooldown:${deviceId}:${ruleId}`;
            await redis.setex(key, minutes * 60, '1');
        }
    }

    /**
     * Check if current time is in rule's time window
     */
    isInTimeWindow(rule) {
        if (!rule.time_window_start || !rule.time_window_end) {
            return true;
        }

        const now = new Date();
        const currentHour = now.getHours();
        const currentMinute = now.getMinutes();
        const currentTime = currentHour * 60 + currentMinute;

        const [startHour, startMinute] = rule.time_window_start.split(':').map(Number);
        const [endHour, endMinute] = rule.time_window_end.split(':').map(Number);
        
        const startTime = startHour * 60 + startMinute;
        const endTime = endHour * 60 + endMinute;

        // Check day of week
        if (rule.days_of_week && rule.days_of_week.length > 0) {
            const today = now.getDay(); // 0 = Sunday
            if (!rule.days_of_week.includes(today)) {
                return false;
            }
        }

        if (startTime <= endTime) {
            return currentTime >= startTime && currentTime <= endTime;
        } else {
            // Overnight window
            return currentTime >= startTime || currentTime <= endTime;
        }
    }
}

module.exports = new AlertEvaluatorService();

javascript
/**
 * Main Alert Service
 * Creates and manages alerts
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const evaluator = require('./alert-evaluator.service');
const notificationService = require('./notification.service');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);

class AlertService {
    /**
     * Process GPS data and generate alerts
     */
    async processGpsData(deviceId, gpsData) {
        try {
            // Evaluate rules
            const triggeredAlerts = await evaluator.evaluate(deviceId, gpsData);
            
            for (const alert of triggeredAlerts) {
                await this.createAlert(alert);
            }

            return triggeredAlerts;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Alert processing error:', error);
            return [];
        }
    }

    /**
     * Create alert
     */
    async createAlert({ ruleId, deviceId, severity, details, value }) {
        const alertId = uuidv4();

        try {
            // Get device and client info
            const device = await pool.query(`
                SELECT d.client_id, d.vehicle_id, d.imei, 
                       c.user_id as client_user_id
                FROM devices d
                LEFT JOIN clients c ON d.client_id = c.id
                WHERE d.id = $1
            `, [deviceId]);

            const clientUserId = device.rows[0]?.client_user_id;

            // Insert alert
            await pool.query(`
                INSERT INTO alert_events (
                    id, rule_id, device_id, vehicle_id, client_id,
                    severity, message, details, trigger_value, status
                ) VALUES (
                    $1, $2, $3, $4, $5,
                    $6, $7, $8, $9, 'ACTIVE'
                )
            `, [
                alertId,
                ruleId,
                deviceId,
                device.rows[0]?.vehicle_id,
                device.rows[0]?.client_id,
                severity,
                this.generateMessage(severity, details),
                JSON.stringify(details),
                value
            ]);

            // Get rule to check notification settings
            const rule = await pool.query(`
                SELECT * FROM alert_rules WHERE id = $1
            `, [ruleId]);

            // Send notifications
            await notificationService.sendNotifications({
                userId: clientUserId,
                alertId,
                rule: rule.rows[0],
                details,
                severity
            });

            // Store in Redis for real-time
            await redis.publish('alert:new', JSON.stringify({
                id: alertId,
                deviceId,
                severity,
                details,
                timestamp: new Date()
            }));

            console.log(`Alert created: ${alertId} for device ${deviceId}`);

            return alertId;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Create alert error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Acknowledge alert
     */
    async acknowledgeAlert(alertId, userId) {
        try {
            await pool.query(`
                UPDATE alert_events 
                SET status = 'ACKNOWLEDGED',
                    acknowledged_by = $1,
                    acknowledged_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $2 AND status = 'ACTIVE'
            `, [userId, alertId]);

            // Publish update
            await redis.publish('alert:update', JSON.stringify({
                id: alertId,
                status: 'ACKNOWLEDGED'
            }));

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Acknowledge alert error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Resolve alert
     */
    async resolveAlert(alertId, userId) {
        try {
            await pool.query(`
                UPDATE alert_events 
                SET status = 'RESOLVED',
                    resolved_by = $1,
                    resolved_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $2
            `, [userId, alertId]);

            // Publish update
            await redis.publish('alert:update', JSON.stringify({
                id: alertId,
                status: 'RESOLVED'
            }));

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Resolve alert error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get active alerts for device
     */
    async getDeviceAlerts(deviceId, limit = 50) {
        try {
            const alerts = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    ae.*,
                    ar.name as rule_name,
                    ar.type as rule_type
                FROM alert_events ae
                JOIN alert_rules ar ON ae.rule_id = ar.id
                WHERE ae.device_id = $1
                ORDER BY ae.triggered_at DESC
                LIMIT $2
            `, [deviceId, limit]);

            return alerts.rows;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get device alerts error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get alerts for client
     */
    async getClientAlerts(clientId, status = null, limit = 100) {
        try {
            let query = `
                SELECT 
                    ae.*,
                    ar.name as rule_name,
                    ar.type as rule_type,
                    d.imei,
                    d.name as device_name
                FROM alert_events ae
                JOIN alert_rules ar ON ae.rule_id = ar.id
                JOIN devices d ON ae.device_id = d.id
                WHERE ae.client_id = $1
            `;
            
            const params = [clientId];
            
            if (status) {
                query += ` AND ae.status = $2`;
                params.push(status);
            }
            
            query += ` ORDER BY ae.triggered_at DESC LIMIT $${params.length + 1}`;
            params.push(limit);

            const alerts = await pool.query(query, params);
            return alerts.rows;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get client alerts error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get alert statistics
     */
    async getAlertStats(clientId, days = 7) {
        try {
            const stats = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    ar.type,
                    ar.severity,
                    COUNT(*) as count,
                    MIN(ae.triggered_at) as first_occurrence,
                    MAX(ae.triggered_at) as last_occurrence
                FROM alert_events ae
                JOIN alert_rules ar ON ae.rule_id = ar.id
                WHERE ae.client_id = $1
                AND ae.triggered_at > CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '$2 days'
                GROUP BY ar.type, ar.severity
                ORDER BY count DESC
            `, [clientId, days]);

            return stats.rows;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get alert stats error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Generate human-readable message
     */
    generateMessage(severity, details) {
        const prefix = severity === 'CRITICAL' ? '🚨' :
                      severity === 'WARNING' ? '⚠️' : 'ℹ️';
        
        if (details.speed) {
            return `${prefix} Overspeed: ${details.speed} km/h (Limit: ${details.limit} km/h)`;
        }
        if (details.minutes_offline) {
            return `${prefix} Device offline for ${details.minutes_offline} minutes`;
        }
        if (details.action === 'ENTER') {
            return `${prefix} Entered geofence: ${details.geofence}`;
        }
        if (details.action === 'EXIT') {
            return `${prefix} Exited geofence: ${details.geofence}`;
        }
        if (details.drop_percent) {
            return `${prefix} Possible fuel theft: ${details.drop_percent.toFixed(1)}% drop`;
        }
        if (details.battery) {
            return `${prefix} Battery low: ${details.battery}%`;
        }
        if (details.value === 'POWER_CUT') {
            return `${prefix} Device tamper detected - power cut`;
        }
        
        return `${prefix} Alert triggered`;
    }
}

module.exports = new AlertService();
📦 File 3: /backend/services/notification.service.js
javascript
/**
 * Multi-channel Notification Service
 * Handles push, SMS, email, WhatsApp notifications
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const axios = require('axios');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);

class NotificationService {
    /**
     * Send notifications for alert
     */
    async sendNotifications({ userId, alertId, rule, details, severity }) {
        try {
            // Get user notification preferences
            const user = await pool.query(`
                SELECT email, phone, notification_preferences
                FROM users WHERE id = $1
            `, [userId]);

            if (!user.rows[0]) return;

            const prefs = user.rows[0].notification_preferences || {};

            // Create notification records
            const notifications = [];

            // In-app notification (always)
            notifications.push(await this.createInAppNotification(
                userId, alertId, rule, details, severity
            ));

            // Push notification
            if (prefs.push && rule.notify_push) {
                notifications.push(await this.sendPushNotification(
                    userId, alertId, rule, details, severity
                ));
            }

            // Email notification
            if (prefs.email && rule.notify_email && user.rows[0].email) {
                notifications.push(await this.sendEmail(
                    user.rows[0].email, alertId, rule, details, severity
                ));
            }

            // SMS notification
            if (prefs.sms && rule.notify_sms && user.rows[0].phone) {
                notifications.push(await this.sendSMS(
                    user.rows[0].phone, alertId, rule, details, severity
                ));
            }

            // WhatsApp notification
            if (prefs.whatsapp && rule.notify_whatsapp && user.rows[0].phone) {
                notifications.push(await this.sendWhatsApp(
                    user.rows[0].phone, alertId, rule, details, severity
                ));
            }

            // Webhook notification
            if (rule.notify_webhook && rule.webhook_url) {
                notifications.push(await this.sendWebhook(
                    rule.webhook_url, alertId, rule, details, severity
                ));
            }

            return notifications;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Send notifications error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Create in-app notification
     */
    async createInAppNotification(userId, alertId, rule, details, severity) {
        try {
            const notificationId = await pool.query(`
                INSERT INTO notifications (
                    id, user_id, alert_event_id, channel,
                    title, body, data, status
                ) VALUES (
                    uuid_generate_v4(), $1, $2, 'IN_APP',
                    $3, $4, $5, 'PENDING'
                ) RETURNING id
            `, [
                userId,
                alertId,
                this.getTitle(rule, severity),
                this.getBody(rule, details),
                JSON.stringify({ rule, details, severity })
            ]);

            // Publish for real-time delivery
            await redis.publish('notification:inapp', JSON.stringify({
                userId,
                notificationId: notificationId.rows[0].id,
                title: this.getTitle(rule, severity),
                body: this.getBody(rule, details),
                severity,
                timestamp: new Date()
            }));

            return notificationId.rows[0].id;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('In-app notification error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send push notification via Firebase
     */
    async sendPushNotification(userId, alertId, rule, details, severity) {
        try {
            // Get user's FCM tokens
            const tokens = await pool.query(`
                SELECT fcm_token FROM user_devices 
                WHERE user_id = $1 AND fcm_token IS NOT NULL
            `, [userId]);

            if (tokens.rows.length === 0) return null;

            const notification = {
                title: this.getTitle(rule, severity),
                body: this.getBody(rule, details),
                data: {
                    alertId,
                    type: rule.type,
                    severity,
                    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
                }
            };

            // Send to Firebase Cloud Messaging
            const response = await axios.post('https://fcm.googleapis.com/fcm/send', {
                registration_ids: tokens.rows.map(t => t.fcm_token),
                notification: {
                    title: notification.title,
                    body: notification.body,
                    sound: 'default'
                },
                data: notification.data,
                android: {
                    priority: 'high'
                },
                apns: {
                    payload: {
                        aps: {
                            sound: 'default'
                        }
                    }
                }
            }, {
                headers: {
                    'Authorization': `key=${process.env.FCM_SERVER_KEY}`,
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                }
            });

            // Log notification
            const notificationId = await pool.query(`
                INSERT INTO notifications (
                    id, user_id, alert_event_id, channel,
                    title, body, data, status, provider_response
                ) VALUES (
                    uuid_generate_v4(), $1, $2, 'PUSH',
                    $3, $4, $5, $6, $7
                ) RETURNING id
            `, [
                userId,
                alertId,
                notification.title,
                notification.body,
                JSON.stringify(notification.data),
                response.data.success ? 'SENT' : 'FAILED',
                JSON.stringify(response.data)
            ]);

            return notificationId.rows[0].id;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Push notification error:', error);
            
            // Log failed notification
            await pool.query(`
                INSERT INTO notifications (
                    user_id, alert_event_id, channel,
                    title, body, status, error_message
                ) VALUES (
                    $1, $2, 'PUSH',
                    $3, $4, 'FAILED', $5
                )
            `, [
                userId,
                alertId,
                this.getTitle(rule, severity),
                this.getBody(rule, details),
                error.message
            ]);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send email notification
     */
    async sendEmail(email, alertId, rule, details, severity) {
        try {
            // Queue email for processing
            await redis.lpush('email:queue', JSON.stringify({
                to: email,
                subject: this.getTitle(rule, severity),
                html: this.getEmailBody(rule, details),
                alertId
            }));

            // Log notification
            const notificationId = await pool.query(`
                INSERT INTO notifications (
                    id, user_id, alert_event_id, channel,
                    title, body, data, status
                ) VALUES (
                    uuid_generate_v4(), 
                    (SELECT id FROM users WHERE email = $1),
                    $2, 'EMAIL', $3, $4, $5, 'QUEUED'
                ) RETURNING id
            `, [
                email,
                alertId,
                this.getTitle(rule, severity),
                this.getBody(rule, details),
                JSON.stringify({ rule, details, severity })
            ]);

            return notificationId.rows[0].id;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Email notification error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send SMS notification
     */
    async sendSMS(phone, alertId, rule, details, severity) {
        try {
            // Queue SMS for processing
            await redis.lpush('sms:queue', JSON.stringify({
                to: phone,
                message: `${this.getTitle(rule, severity)}: ${this.getBody(rule, details)}`,
                alertId
            }));

            // Log notification
            const notificationId = await pool.query(`
                INSERT INTO notifications (
                    id, user_id, alert_event_id, channel,
                    title, body, status
                ) VALUES (
                    uuid_generate_v4(),
                    (SELECT id FROM users WHERE phone = $1),
                    $2, 'SMS', $3, $4, 'QUEUED'
                ) RETURNING id
            `, [
                phone,
                alertId,
                this.getTitle(rule, severity),
                this.getBody(rule, details)
            ]);

            return notificationId.rows[0].id;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('SMS notification error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send WhatsApp notification
     */
    async sendWhatsApp(phone, alertId, rule, details, severity) {
        try {
            // Queue WhatsApp for processing
            await redis.lpush('whatsapp:queue', JSON.stringify({
                to: phone,
                message: `${this.getTitle(rule, severity)}: ${this.getBody(rule, details)}`,
                alertId
            }));

            // Log notification
            const notificationId = await pool.query(`
                INSERT INTO notifications (
                    id, user_id, alert_event_id, channel,
                    title, body, status
                ) VALUES (
                    uuid_generate_v4(),
                    (SELECT id FROM users WHERE phone = $1),
                    $2, 'WHATSAPP', $3, $4, 'QUEUED'
                ) RETURNING id
            `, [
                phone,
                alertId,
                this.getTitle(rule, severity),
                this.getBody(rule, details)
            ]);

            return notificationId.rows[0].id;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('WhatsApp notification error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send webhook notification
     */
    async sendWebhook(url, alertId, rule, details, severity) {
        try {
            const payload = {
                alertId,
                type: rule.type,
                severity,
                details,
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
            };

            // Queue webhook
            await redis.lpush('webhook:queue', JSON.stringify({
                url,
                payload,
                alertId
            }));

            // Log notification
            await pool.query(`
                INSERT INTO notifications (
                    user_id, alert_event_id, channel,
                    title, body, data, status
                ) VALUES (
                    NULL, $1, 'WEBHOOK',
                    $2, $3, $4, 'QUEUED'
                )
            `, [
                alertId,
                this.getTitle(rule, severity),
                this.getBody(rule, details),
                JSON.stringify(payload)
            ]);

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Webhook notification error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get notification title
     */
    getTitle(rule, severity) {
        const prefix = severity === 'CRITICAL' ? '🚨 CRITICAL' :
                      severity === 'WARNING' ? '⚠️ Warning' : 'ℹ️ Info';
        
        return `${prefix}: ${rule.name}`;
    }

    /**
     * Get notification body
     */
    getBody(rule, details) {
        if (details.speed) {
            return `Vehicle speeding at ${details.speed} km/h`;
        }
        if (details.minutes_offline) {
            return `Device offline for ${details.minutes_offline} minutes`;
        }
        if (details.geofence) {
            return `${details.action} geofence: ${details.geofence}`;
        }
        if (details.drop_percent) {
            return `Fuel level dropped by ${details.drop_percent.toFixed(1)}%`;
        }
        if (details.battery) {
            return `Battery at ${details.battery}%`;
        }
        return rule.description || 'Alert triggered';
    }

    /**
     * Get email HTML body
     */
    getEmailBody(rule, details) {
        return `
            <div style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif; max-width: 600px; margin: 0 auto;">
                <h2 style="color: ${details.severity === 'CRITICAL' ? '#dc2626' : '#f59e0b'};">
                    ${this.getTitle(rule, details.severity)}
                </h2>
                
                <div style="background: #f3f4f6; padding: 20px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 20px 0;">
                    <p><strong>Time:</strong> ${new Date().toLocaleString()}</p>
                    ${details.location ? `
                        <p><strong>Location:</strong> ${details.location.lat}, ${details.location.lng}</p>
                    ` : ''}
                    ${details.speed ? `<p><strong>Speed:</strong> ${details.speed} km/h</p>` : ''}
                    ${details.limit ? `<p><strong>Limit:</strong> ${details.limit} km/h</p>` : ''}
                </div>
                
                <p style="color: #6b7280; font-size: 14px;">
                    View details in your GPS Tracking dashboard
                </p>
            </div>
        `;
    }
}

module.exports = new NotificationService();
⚙️ File 4: /backend/jobs/alert-processor.js
javascript
/**
 * Alert Processor Job
 * Runs continuously to process GPS data and generate alerts
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const alertService = require('../services/alert.service');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);

class AlertProcessor {
    constructor() {
        this.isRunning = false;
    }

    /**
     * Start the processor
     */
    start() {
        if (this.isRunning) return;
        
        this.isRunning = true;
        console.log('Alert processor started');
        
        // Listen for new GPS data
        this.listenForGPSData();
        
        // Run offline check every minute
        setInterval(() => this.checkOfflineDevices(), 60000);
        
        // Run maintenance checks daily at 2 AM
        setInterval(() => this.checkMaintenance(), 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
    }

    /**
     * Listen for real-time GPS data
     */
    listenForGPSData() {
        redis.subscribe('gps:data', (err) => {
            if (err) {
                console.error('Failed to subscribe to gps:data:', err);
                return;
            }
            console.log('Listening for GPS data');
        });

        redis.on('message', async (channel, message) => {
            if (channel === 'gps:data') {
                const data = JSON.parse(message);
                await this.processGPSData(data.deviceId, data.gpsData);
            }
        });
    }

    /**
     * Process GPS data
     */
    async processGPSData(deviceId, gpsData) {
        try {
            await alertService.processGpsData(deviceId, gpsData);
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Process GPS data error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Check for offline devices
     */
    async checkOfflineDevices() {
        try {
            // Get devices that haven't sent data in last 10 minutes
            const devices = await pool.query(`
                SELECT d.id, d.imei, d.last_seen
                FROM devices d
                WHERE d.status = 'online'
                AND d.last_seen < NOW() - INTERVAL '10 minutes'
            `);

            for (const device of devices.rows) {
                // Create offline alert
                await alertService.processGpsData(device.id, {
                    type: 'offline_check',
                    last_seen: device.last_seen
                });
            }

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Offline check error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Check maintenance due
     */
    async checkMaintenance() {
        try {
            const devices = await pool.query(`
                SELECT d.id, d.next_maintenance_due
                FROM devices d
                WHERE d.next_maintenance_due IS NOT NULL
                AND d.next_maintenance_due <= NOW() + INTERVAL '7 days'
            `);

            for (const device of devices.rows) {
                await alertService.processGpsData(device.id, {
                    type: 'maintenance_check'
                });
            }

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Maintenance check error:', error);
        }
    }
}

module.exports = new AlertProcessor();
