🖥️ BACKEND IMPLEMENTATION
📦 File 1: /backend/services/kpi.service.js
javascript
/**
 * KPI Service
 * Calculates all Key Performance Indicators
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);

class KPIService {
    /**
     * Get dashboard KPIs for client
     */
    async getClientKPIs(clientId, dateRange = 'today') {
        try {
            // Try cache first
            const cacheKey = `kpi:client:${clientId}:${dateRange}`;
            const cached = await redis.get(cacheKey);
            
            if (cached) {
                return JSON.parse(cached);
            }

            const { startDate, endDate } = this.getDateRange(dateRange);

            // Get all vehicles for client
            const vehicles = await pool.query(`
                SELECT id FROM vehicles WHERE client_id = $1
            `, [clientId]);

            const vehicleIds = vehicles.rows.map(v => v.id);

            if (vehicleIds.length === 0) {
                return this.getEmptyKPIs();
            }

            // Parallel KPI calculations
            const [
                fleetStats,
                tripStats,
                alertStats,
                commandStats,
                fuelStats,
                driverStats
            ] = await Promise.all([
                this.getFleetStats(vehicleIds),
                this.getTripStats(vehicleIds, startDate, endDate),
                this.getAlertStats(clientId, startDate, endDate),
                this.getCommandStats(vehicleIds, startDate, endDate),
                this.getFuelStats(vehicleIds, startDate, endDate),
                this.getDriverStats(vehicleIds, startDate, endDate)
            ]);

            const kpis = {
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                dateRange: { startDate, endDate },
                
                // Fleet Overview
                fleet: fleetStats,
                
                // Trip Summary
                trips: tripStats,
                
                // Alerts
                alerts: alertStats,
                
                // Commands
                commands: commandStats,
                
                // Fuel & Efficiency
                fuel: fuelStats,
                
                // Driver Performance
                drivers: driverStats,
                
                // Utilization
                utilization: this.calculateUtilization(fleetStats, tripStats),
                
                // Cost Analysis
                costs: await this.getCostStats(vehicleIds, tripStats)
            };

            // Cache for 5 minutes
            await redis.setex(cacheKey, 300, JSON.stringify(kpis));

            return kpis;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get client KPIs error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get admin KPIs (all clients)
     */
    async getAdminKPIs(dateRange = 'today') {
        try {
            const cacheKey = `kpi:admin:${dateRange}`;
            const cached = await redis.get(cacheKey);
            
            if (cached) {
                return JSON.parse(cached);
            }

            const { startDate, endDate } = this.getDateRange(dateRange);

            // Get all clients
            const clients = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    c.id,
                    c.company_name,
                    COUNT(DISTINCT v.id) as vehicle_count,
                    COUNT(DISTINCT d.id) as device_count
                FROM clients c
                LEFT JOIN vehicles v ON c.id = v.client_id
                LEFT JOIN devices d ON v.current_device_id = d.id
                GROUP BY c.id
            `);

            // Calculate totals
            let totalVehicles = 0;
            let totalDevices = 0;
            let totalDistance = 0;
            let totalAlerts = 0;
            let totalRevenue = 0;

            for (const client of clients.rows) {
                totalVehicles += parseInt(client.vehicle_count);
                totalDevices += parseInt(client.device_count);

                // Get client KPIs
                const clientKpis = await this.getClientKPIs(client.id, dateRange);
                
                totalDistance += clientKpis.trips.totalDistance || 0;
                totalAlerts += clientKpis.alerts.total || 0;
                
                // Get revenue
                const revenue = await this.getClientRevenue(client.id, startDate, endDate);
                totalRevenue += revenue;
            }

            // Get system health
            const systemHealth = await this.getSystemHealth();

            // Get online/offline stats
            const onlineStats = await this.getOnlineStats();

            const kpis = {
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                dateRange: { startDate, endDate },
                
                // Summary
                summary: {
                    totalClients: clients.rows.length,
                    totalVehicles,
                    totalDevices,
                    totalDistance: (totalDistance / 1000).toFixed(2), // km
                    totalAlerts,
                    totalRevenue,
                    averageVehiclesPerClient: (totalVehicles / clients.rows.length).toFixed(1)
                },
                
                // Real-time
                realtime: onlineStats,
                
                // System
                system: systemHealth,
                
                // Client breakdown
                clients: clients.rows.map(c => ({
                    id: c.id,
                    name: c.company_name,
                    vehicles: parseInt(c.vehicle_count),
                    devices: parseInt(c.device_count)
                }))
            };

            // Cache for 2 minutes
            await redis.setex(cacheKey, 120, JSON.stringify(kpis));

            return kpis;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get admin KPIs error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get fleet statistics
     */
    async getFleetStats(vehicleIds) {
        try {
            const stats = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    COUNT(*) as total_vehicles,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN d.status = 'online' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as online,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN d.status = 'offline' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as offline,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN g.ignition = true AND g.speed > 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as moving,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN g.ignition = true AND g.speed = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as idle,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN g.ignition = false THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as stopped,
                    AVG(EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (NOW() - d.last_seen))) as avg_last_seen
                FROM vehicles v
                JOIN devices d ON v.current_device_id = d.id
                LEFT JOIN gps_live_data g ON d.id = g.device_id
                WHERE v.id = ANY($1::uuid[])
            `, [vehicleIds]);

            return {
                total: parseInt(stats.rows[0].total_vehicles) || 0,
                online: parseInt(stats.rows[0].online) || 0,
                offline: parseInt(stats.rows[0].offline) || 0,
                moving: parseInt(stats.rows[0].moving) || 0,
                idle: parseInt(stats.rows[0].idle) || 0,
                stopped: parseInt(stats.rows[0].stopped) || 0,
                onlinePercentage: this.calculatePercentage(
                    stats.rows[0].online,
                    stats.rows[0].total_vehicles
                ),
                avgLastSeen: Math.round(stats.rows[0].avg_last_seen || 0)
            };

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get fleet stats error:', error);
            return this.getEmptyFleetStats();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get trip statistics
     */
    async getTripStats(vehicleIds, startDate, endDate) {
        try {
            const stats = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    COUNT(*) as trip_count,
                    COALESCE(SUM(distance_meters), 0) as total_distance,
                    COALESCE(SUM(duration_seconds), 0) as total_duration,
                    COALESCE(AVG(avg_speed), 0) as average_speed,
                    COALESCE(MAX(max_speed), 0) as max_speed,
                    COALESCE(SUM(idle_seconds), 0) as total_idle,
                    COALESCE(AVG(idle_seconds), 0) as avg_idle_per_trip,
                    COALESCE(SUM(overspeed_count), 0) as total_overspeed,
                    COALESCE(SUM(harsh_braking_count), 0) as total_harsh_braking,
                    COALESCE(SUM(harsh_acceleration_count), 0) as total_harsh_acceleration
                FROM trips
                WHERE vehicle_id = ANY($1::uuid[])
                AND start_time >= $2
                AND end_time <= $3
                AND is_completed = true
            `, [vehicleIds, startDate, endDate]);

            const row = stats.rows[0];

            return {
                count: parseInt(row.trip_count) || 0,
                totalDistance: parseFloat(row.total_distance) || 0,
                totalDuration: parseInt(row.total_duration) || 0,
                averageSpeed: parseFloat(row.average_speed) || 0,
                maxSpeed: parseFloat(row.max_speed) || 0,
                totalIdle: parseInt(row.total_idle) || 0,
                avgIdlePerTrip: parseInt(row.avg_idle_per_trip) || 0,
                overspeed: parseInt(row.total_overspeed) || 0,
                harshBraking: parseInt(row.total_harsh_braking) || 0,
                harshAcceleration: parseInt(row.total_harsh_acceleration) || 0,
                
                // Calculated fields
                averageDistancePerTrip: row.trip_count > 0 
                    ? (row.total_distance / row.trip_count).toFixed(2)
                    : 0,
                averageDurationPerTrip: row.trip_count > 0
                    ? Math.round(row.total_duration / row.trip_count / 60) // minutes
                    : 0,
                movingTime: (row.total_duration - row.total_idle) || 0,
                utilizationRate: row.total_duration > 0
                    ? ((row.total_duration - row.total_idle) / row.total_duration * 100).toFixed(1)
                    : 0
            };

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get trip stats error:', error);
            return this.getEmptyTripStats();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get alert statistics
     */
    async getAlertStats(clientId, startDate, endDate) {
        try {
            const stats = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    COUNT(*) as total_alerts,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN severity = 'CRITICAL' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as critical,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN severity = 'WARNING' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as warning,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN severity = 'INFO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as info,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'ACTIVE' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as active,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'ACKNOWLEDGED' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as acknowledged,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'RESOLVED' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as resolved,
                    ar.type,
                    COUNT(*) as type_count
                FROM alert_events ae
                JOIN alert_rules ar ON ae.rule_id = ar.id
                WHERE ae.client_id = $1
                AND ae.triggered_at >= $2
                AND ae.triggered_at <= $3
                GROUP BY GROUPING SETS (
                    (),
                    (ar.type)
                )
            `, [clientId, startDate, endDate]);

            const row = stats.rows[0] || {};

            // Get top alert types
            const typeBreakdown = stats.rows
                .filter(r => r.type)
                .map(r => ({
                    type: r.type,
                    count: parseInt(r.type_count)
                }))
                .sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count)
                .slice(0, 5);

            return {
                total: parseInt(row.total_alerts) || 0,
                critical: parseInt(row.critical) || 0,
                warning: parseInt(row.warning) || 0,
                info: parseInt(row.info) || 0,
                active: parseInt(row.active) || 0,
                acknowledged: parseInt(row.acknowledged) || 0,
                resolved: parseInt(row.resolved) || 0,
                resolutionRate: row.total_alerts > 0
                    ? ((row.resolved / row.total_alerts) * 100).toFixed(1)
                    : 0,
                topTypes: typeBreakdown,
                averagePerDay: this.calculateAveragePerDay(
                    row.total_alerts,
                    startDate,
                    endDate
                )
            };

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get alert stats error:', error);
            return this.getEmptyAlertStats();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get command statistics
     */
    async getCommandStats(vehicleIds, startDate, endDate) {
        try {
            const stats = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    COUNT(*) as total_commands,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'SUCCESS' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as successful,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'FAILED' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as failed,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'TIMEOUT' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as timeout,
                    AVG(CASE 
                        WHEN status = 'SUCCESS' 
                        THEN EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (completed_at - sent_at))
                        ELSE NULL 
                    END) as avg_response_time
                FROM command_logs cl
                JOIN devices d ON cl.device_id = d.id
                WHERE d.id = ANY(
                    SELECT current_device_id 
                    FROM vehicles 
                    WHERE id = ANY($1::uuid[])
                )
                AND cl.created_at >= $2
                AND cl.created_at <= $3
            `, [vehicleIds, startDate, endDate]);

            const row = stats.rows[0];

            return {
                total: parseInt(row.total_commands) || 0,
                successful: parseInt(row.successful) || 0,
                failed: parseInt(row.failed) || 0,
                timeout: parseInt(row.timeout) || 0,
                successRate: row.total_commands > 0
                    ? ((row.successful / row.total_commands) * 100).toFixed(1)
                    : 0,
                avgResponseTime: parseFloat(row.avg_response_time)?.toFixed(2) || 0,
                averagePerDay: this.calculateAveragePerDay(
                    row.total_commands,
                    startDate,
                    endDate
                )
            };

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get command stats error:', error);
            return this.getEmptyCommandStats();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get fuel statistics
     */
    async getFuelStats(vehicleIds, startDate, endDate) {
        try {
            const stats = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    COALESCE(SUM(fuel_consumed), 0) as total_fuel,
                    COALESCE(AVG(fuel_avg_kmpl), 0) as average_mileage,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN fuel_theft_detected THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as theft_events,
                    COALESCE(SUM(fuel_theft_amount), 0) as total_theft
                FROM trips
                WHERE vehicle_id = ANY($1::uuid[])
                AND start_time >= $2
                AND end_time <= $3
                AND fuel_consumed > 0
            `, [vehicleIds, startDate, endDate]);

            // Get current fuel levels
            const current = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    AVG(fuel_level) as avg_fuel_level,
                    COUNT(*) as vehicles_with_fuel
                FROM fuel_data f
                WHERE f.vehicle_id = ANY($1::uuid[])
                AND f.recorded_at = (
                    SELECT MAX(recorded_at)
                    FROM fuel_data f2
                    WHERE f2.vehicle_id = f.vehicle_id
                )
            `, [vehicleIds]);

            const row = stats.rows[0];
            const currentRow = current.rows[0];

            return {
                totalFuel: parseFloat(row.total_fuel)?.toFixed(2) || 0,
                averageMileage: parseFloat(row.average_mileage)?.toFixed(2) || 0,
                theftEvents: parseInt(row.theft_events) || 0,
                totalTheft: parseFloat(row.total_theft)?.toFixed(2) || 0,
                avgFuelLevel: parseFloat(currentRow.avg_fuel_level)?.toFixed(1) || 0,
                vehiclesWithFuel: parseInt(currentRow.vehicles_with_fuel) || 0,
                costEstimate: this.estimateFuelCost(row.total_fuel)
            };

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get fuel stats error:', error);
            return this.getEmptyFuelStats();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get driver performance statistics
     */
    async getDriverStats(vehicleIds, startDate, endDate) {
        try {
            const stats = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    COALESCE(AVG(overall_score), 0) as avg_score,
                    MIN(overall_score) as min_score,
                    MAX(overall_score) as max_score,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN risk_level = 'LOW' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as low_risk,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN risk_level = 'MEDIUM' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as medium_risk,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN risk_level = 'HIGH' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as high_risk,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN risk_level = 'CRITICAL' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as critical_risk
                FROM driver_scores
                WHERE vehicle_id = ANY($1::uuid[])
                AND period_start >= $2
                AND period_end <= $3
            `, [vehicleIds, startDate, endDate]);

            const row = stats.rows[0];

            return {
                averageScore: parseFloat(row.avg_score)?.toFixed(1) || 0,
                minScore: parseFloat(row.min_score)?.toFixed(1) || 0,
                maxScore: parseFloat(row.max_score)?.toFixed(1) || 0,
                riskDistribution: {
                    low: parseInt(row.low_risk) || 0,
                    medium: parseInt(row.medium_risk) || 0,
                    high: parseInt(row.high_risk) || 0,
                    critical: parseInt(row.critical_risk) || 0
                },
                topDrivers: await this.getTopDrivers(vehicleIds, startDate, endDate, 5),
                improvementNeeded: await this.getWorstDrivers(vehicleIds, startDate, endDate, 5)
            };

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get driver stats error:', error);
            return this.getEmptyDriverStats();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get online/offline statistics
     */
    async getOnlineStats() {
        try {
            const stats = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    COUNT(*) as total,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'online' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as online,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'offline' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as offline,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN last_seen < NOW() - INTERVAL '1 hour' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as stale
                FROM devices
                WHERE is_active = true
            `);

            const row = stats.rows[0];

            return {
                total: parseInt(row.total) || 0,
                online: parseInt(row.online) || 0,
                offline: parseInt(row.offline) || 0,
                stale: parseInt(row.stale) || 0,
                onlinePercentage: row.total > 0
                    ? ((row.online / row.total) * 100).toFixed(1)
                    : 0,
                lastUpdated: new Date().toISOString()
            };

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get online stats error:', error);
            return {
                total: 0, online: 0, offline: 0, stale: 0, onlinePercentage: 0
            };
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get system health
     */
    async getSystemHealth() {
        try {
            // Database health
            const dbHealth = await pool.query('SELECT 1 as health');
            
            // Redis health
            const redisHealth = await redis.ping();
            
            // Recent errors
            const errors = await pool.query(`
                SELECT COUNT(*) as error_count
                FROM audit_logs
                WHERE category = 'ERROR'
                AND created_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '1 hour'
            `);

            // Command success rate (last hour)
            const commands = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    COUNT(*) as total,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'SUCCESS' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as success
                FROM command_logs
                WHERE created_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '1 hour'
            `);

            return {
                database: dbHealth.rows[0] ? 'healthy' : 'unhealthy',
                redis: redisHealth === 'PONG' ? 'healthy' : 'unhealthy',
                errorCount: parseInt(errors.rows[0].error_count) || 0,
                commandSuccessRate: commands.rows[0].total > 0
                    ? ((commands.rows[0].success / commands.rows[0].total) * 100).toFixed(1)
                    : 100,
                uptime: process.uptime(),
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
            };

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get system health error:', error);
            return {
                database: 'unknown',
                redis: 'unknown',
                errorCount: -1,
                commandSuccessRate: 0,
                uptime: 0
            };
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get revenue statistics
     */
    async getClientRevenue(clientId, startDate, endDate) {
        try {
            const revenue = await pool.query(`
                SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount), 0) as total
                FROM payments p
                JOIN invoices i ON p.invoice_id = i.id
                WHERE i.client_id = $1
                AND p.paid_at >= $2
                AND p.paid_at <= $3
                AND p.status = 'COMPLETED'
            `, [clientId, startDate, endDate]);

            return parseFloat(revenue.rows[0].total) || 0;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get client revenue error:', error);
            return 0;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get cost statistics
     */
    async getCostStats(vehicleIds, tripStats) {
        // Estimate costs based on distance and fuel
        const fuelPricePerLiter = 1.5; // USD
        const maintenanceCostPerKm = 0.1; // USD
        
        const distanceKm = tripStats.totalDistance / 1000;
        const fuelCost = tripStats.totalFuel * fuelPricePerLiter || 0;
        const maintenanceCost = distanceKm * maintenanceCostPerKm;
        
        return {
            estimatedFuelCost: fuelCost.toFixed(2),
            estimatedMaintenanceCost: maintenanceCost.toFixed(2),
            totalEstimatedCost: (fuelCost + maintenanceCost).toFixed(2),
            costPerKm: distanceKm > 0 
                ? ((fuelCost + maintenanceCost) / distanceKm).toFixed(2)
                : 0,
            currency: 'USD'
        };
    }

    /**
     * Calculate utilization rate
     */
    calculateUtilization(fleetStats, tripStats) {
        const totalVehicles = fleetStats.total;
        if (totalVehicles === 0) return 0;

        const movingVehicles = fleetStats.moving;
        const totalHours = 24; // 24 hours
        const movingHours = (tripStats.movingTime || 0) / 3600; // Convert to hours
        
        return {
            currentUtilization: (movingVehicles / totalVehicles * 100).toFixed(1),
            dailyAverageUtilization: totalVehicles > 0
                ? ((movingHours / (totalVehicles * totalHours)) * 100).toFixed(1)
                : 0,
            peakUtilization: Math.min(
                ((fleetStats.moving + fleetStats.idle) / totalVehicles * 100),
                100
            ).toFixed(1)
        };
    }

    /**
     * Get top drivers
     */
    async getTopDrivers(vehicleIds, startDate, endDate, limit = 5) {
        try {
            const drivers = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    ds.driver_id,
                    u.full_name as driver_name,
                    ds.overall_score,
                    ds.risk_level,
                    v.registration_number
                FROM driver_scores ds
                JOIN drivers d ON ds.driver_id = d.id
                JOIN users u ON d.user_id = u.id
                JOIN vehicles v ON ds.vehicle_id = v.id
                WHERE ds.vehicle_id = ANY($1::uuid[])
                AND ds.period_start >= $2
                AND ds.period_end <= $3
                ORDER BY ds.overall_score DESC
                LIMIT $4
            `, [vehicleIds, startDate, endDate, limit]);

            return drivers.rows;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get top drivers error:', error);
            return [];
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get worst drivers
     */
    async getWorstDrivers(vehicleIds, startDate, endDate, limit = 5) {
        try {
            const drivers = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    ds.driver_id,
                    u.full_name as driver_name,
                    ds.overall_score,
                    ds.risk_level,
                    v.registration_number
                FROM driver_scores ds
                JOIN drivers d ON ds.driver_id = d.id
                JOIN users u ON d.user_id = u.id
                JOIN vehicles v ON ds.vehicle_id = v.id
                WHERE ds.vehicle_id = ANY($1::uuid[])
                AND ds.period_start >= $2
                AND ds.period_end <= $3
                ORDER BY ds.overall_score ASC
                LIMIT $4
            `, [vehicleIds, startDate, endDate, limit]);

            return drivers.rows;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get worst drivers error:', error);
            return [];
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get date range from string
     */
    getDateRange(range) {
        const now = new Date();
        let startDate = new Date();
        let endDate = new Date();

        switch(range) {
            case 'today':
                startDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
                endDate.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
                break;
                
            case 'yesterday':
                startDate.setDate(startDate.getDate() - 1);
                startDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
                endDate.setDate(endDate.getDate() - 1);
                endDate.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
                break;
                
            case 'week':
                startDate.setDate(startDate.getDate() - 7);
                startDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
                break;
                
            case 'month':
                startDate.setMonth(startDate.getMonth() - 1);
                startDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
                break;
                
            case 'quarter':
                startDate.setMonth(startDate.getMonth() - 3);
                startDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
                break;
                
            case 'year':
                startDate.setFullYear(startDate.getFullYear() - 1);
                startDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
                break;
                
            default:
                // Custom range - parse from string
                if (range.includes('to')) {
                    const [start, end] = range.split('to');
                    startDate = new Date(start);
                    endDate = new Date(end);
                }
        }

        return {
            startDate: startDate.toISOString(),
            endDate: endDate.toISOString()
        };
    }

    /**
     * Calculate percentage
     */
    calculatePercentage(part, total) {
        if (!total || total === 0) return 0;
        return ((part / total) * 100).toFixed(1);
    }

    /**
     * Calculate average per day
     */
    calculateAveragePerDay(total, startDate, endDate) {
        const start = new Date(startDate);
        const end = new Date(endDate);
        const days = Math.max(1, Math.ceil((end - start) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)));
        
        return (total / days).toFixed(1);
    }

    /**
     * Estimate fuel cost
     */
    estimateFuelCost(fuelLiters) {
        const pricePerLiter = 1.5; // USD
        return (fuelLiters * pricePerLiter).toFixed(2);
    }

    /**
     * Empty KPI templates
     */
    getEmptyKPIs() {
        return {
            fleet: this.getEmptyFleetStats(),
            trips: this.getEmptyTripStats(),
            alerts: this.getEmptyAlertStats(),
            commands: this.getEmptyCommandStats(),
            fuel: this.getEmptyFuelStats(),
            drivers: this.getEmptyDriverStats()
        };
    }

    getEmptyFleetStats() {
        return {
            total: 0, online: 0, offline: 0,
            moving: 0, idle: 0, stopped: 0,
            onlinePercentage: 0, avgLastSeen: 0
        };
    }

    getEmptyTripStats() {
        return {
            count: 0, totalDistance: 0, totalDuration: 0,
            averageSpeed: 0, maxSpeed: 0, totalIdle: 0,
            avgIdlePerTrip: 0, overspeed: 0,
            harshBraking: 0, harshAcceleration: 0,
            averageDistancePerTrip: 0, averageDurationPerTrip: 0,
            movingTime: 0, utilizationRate: 0
        };
    }

    getEmptyAlertStats() {
        return {
            total: 0, critical: 0, warning: 0, info: 0,
            active: 0, acknowledged: 0, resolved: 0,
            resolutionRate: 0, topTypes: [], averagePerDay: 0
        };
    }

    getEmptyCommandStats() {
        return {
            total: 0, successful: 0, failed: 0, timeout: 0,
            successRate: 0, avgResponseTime: 0, averagePerDay: 0
        };
    }

    getEmptyFuelStats() {
        return {
            totalFuel: 0, averageMileage: 0,
            theftEvents: 0, totalTheft: 0,
            avgFuelLevel: 0, vehiclesWithFuel: 0,
            costEstimate: 0
        };
    }

    getEmptyDriverStats() {
        return {
            averageScore: 0, minScore: 0, maxScore: 0,
            riskDistribution: { low: 0, medium: 0, high: 0, critical: 0 },
            topDrivers: [], improvementNeeded: []
        };
    }
}

module.exports = new KPIService();
📦 File 2: /backend/services/report.service.js
javascript
/**
 * Report Service
 * Generates various reports and exports
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const ExcelJS = require('exceljs');
const PDFDocument = require('pdfkit');
const kpiService = require('./kpi.service');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

class ReportService {
    /**
     * Generate daily activity report
     */
    async generateDailyReport(clientId, date) {
        try {
            const reportDate = new Date(date);
            const nextDay = new Date(date);
            nextDay.setDate(nextDay.getDate() + 1);

            // Get KPIs for the day
            const kpis = await kpiService.getClientKPIs(
                clientId,
                `${date}to${nextDay.toISOString()}`
            );

            // Get detailed trip data
            const trips = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    t.*,
                    v.registration_number,
                    v.make,
                    v.model
                FROM trips t
                JOIN vehicles v ON t.vehicle_id = v.id
                WHERE v.client_id = $1
                AND DATE(t.start_time) = $2
                ORDER BY t.start_time DESC
            `, [clientId, date]);

            // Get alert summary
            const alerts = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    ae.*,
                    ar.name as rule_name,
                    v.registration_number
                FROM alert_events ae
                JOIN alert_rules ar ON ae.rule_id = ar.id
                JOIN vehicles v ON ae.vehicle_id = v.id
                WHERE v.client_id = $1
                AND DATE(ae.triggered_at) = $2
                ORDER BY ae.triggered_at DESC
            `, [clientId, date]);

            return {
                reportId: `daily-${clientId}-${date}`,
                generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
                date: date,
                summary: kpis,
                trips: trips.rows,
                alerts: alerts.rows,
                vehicleCount: kpis.fleet.total,
                activeVehicles: kpis.fleet.moving + kpis.fleet.idle
            };

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Generate daily report error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Generate fleet utilization report
     */
    async generateFleetReport(clientId, startDate, endDate) {
        try {
            const vehicles = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    v.id,
                    v.registration_number,
                    v.make,
                    v.model,
                    v.year,
                    COUNT(t.id) as trip_count,
                    COALESCE(SUM(t.distance_meters), 0) as total_distance,
                    COALESCE(SUM(t.duration_seconds), 0) as total_duration,
                    COALESCE(SUM(t.idle_seconds), 0) as total_idle,
                    COALESCE(MAX(t.max_speed), 0) as max_speed,
                    COALESCE(AVG(t.avg_speed), 0) as avg_speed,
                    COALESCE(SUM(t.overspeed_count), 0) as overspeed_count,
                    d.status as current_status
                FROM vehicles v
                LEFT JOIN trips t ON v.id = t.vehicle_id
                    AND t.start_time >= $2
                    AND t.end_time <= $3
                LEFT JOIN devices d ON v.current_device_id = d.id
                WHERE v.client_id = $1
                GROUP BY v.id, v.registration_number, v.make, v.model, v.year, d.status
                ORDER BY total_distance DESC
            `, [clientId, startDate, endDate]);

            // Calculate utilization metrics
            const totalDays = Math.ceil(
                (new Date(endDate) - new Date(startDate)) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)
            );

            const report = {
                reportId: `fleet-${clientId}-${startDate}-${endDate}`,
                generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
                period: { startDate, endDate, days: totalDays },
                vehicles: vehicles.rows.map(v => ({
                    ...v,
                    distanceKm: (v.total_distance / 1000).toFixed(2),
                    hoursUsed: (v.total_duration / 3600).toFixed(1),
                    idleHours: (v.total_idle / 3600).toFixed(1),
                    utilizationRate: totalDays > 0
                        ? ((v.total_duration / 3600) / (totalDays * 24) * 100).toFixed(1)
                        : 0,
                    avgSpeedPerTrip: v.avg_speed?.toFixed(1) || 0
                })),
                summary: {
                    totalVehicles: vehicles.rows.length,
                    activeVehicles: vehicles.rows.filter(v => v.trip_count > 0).length,
                    totalDistance: vehicles.rows.reduce((sum, v) => sum + v.total_distance, 0) / 1000,
                    totalTrips: vehicles.rows.reduce((sum, v) => sum + parseInt(v.trip_count), 0),
                    averageUtilization: vehicles.rows.reduce((sum, v) => {
                        const util = totalDays > 0
                            ? (v.total_duration / 3600) / (totalDays * 24) * 100
                            : 0;
                        return sum + util;
                    }, 0) / vehicles.rows.length
                }
            };

            return report;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Generate fleet report error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Generate driver performance report
     */
    async generateDriverReport(clientId, startDate, endDate) {
        try {
            const drivers = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    u.id,
                    u.full_name,
                    u.email,
                    COUNT(DISTINCT t.id) as trip_count,
                    COALESCE(SUM(t.distance_meters), 0) as total_distance,
                    COALESCE(SUM(t.duration_seconds), 0) as total_duration,
                    COALESCE(AVG(ds.overall_score), 0) as avg_score,
                    COALESCE(SUM(t.overspeed_count), 0) as total_overspeed,
                    COALESCE(SUM(t.harsh_braking_count), 0) as total_harsh_braking,
                    COALESCE(SUM(t.harsh_acceleration_count), 0) as total_harsh_acceleration,
                    MAX(ds.risk_level) as risk_level
                FROM drivers d
                JOIN users u ON d.user_id = u.id
                LEFT JOIN trips t ON d.id = t.driver_id
                    AND t.start_time >= $2
                    AND t.end_time <= $3
                LEFT JOIN driver_scores ds ON d.id = ds.driver_id
                    AND ds.period_start >= $2
                    AND ds.period_end <= $3
                WHERE d.client_id = $1
                GROUP BY u.id, u.full_name, u.email
                ORDER BY avg_score DESC
            `, [clientId, startDate, endDate]);

            // Calculate rankings
            const rankedDrivers = drivers.rows.map((d, index) => ({
                ...d,
                rank: index + 1,
                distanceKm: (d.total_distance / 1000).toFixed(2),
                score: parseFloat(d.avg_score).toFixed(1),
                safetyScore: this.calculateSafetyScore(d),
                efficiencyScore: this.calculateEfficiencyScore(d)
            }));

            return {
                reportId: `drivers-${clientId}-${startDate}-${endDate}`,
                generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
                period: { startDate, endDate },
                drivers: rankedDrivers,
                summary: {
                    totalDrivers: drivers.rows.length,
                    averageScore: drivers.rows.reduce((sum, d) => sum + parseFloat(d.avg_score), 0) / drivers.rows.length,
                    bestDriver: rankedDrivers[0] || null,
                    worstDriver: rankedDrivers[rankedDrivers.length - 1] || null,
                    totalIncidents: drivers.rows.reduce((sum, d) => 
                        sum + parseInt(d.total_overspeed) + 
                        parseInt(d.total_harsh_braking) + 
                        parseInt(d.total_harsh_acceleration), 0
                    )
                }
            };

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Generate driver report error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Generate fuel report
     */
    async generateFuelReport(clientId, startDate, endDate) {
        try {
            const fuelData = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    v.registration_number,
                    v.make,
                    v.model,
                    COUNT(DISTINCT t.id) as trip_count,
                    COALESCE(SUM(t.fuel_consumed), 0) as total_fuel,
                    COALESCE(SUM(t.distance_meters), 0) as total_distance,
                    COALESCE(AVG(t.fuel_avg_kmpl), 0) as avg_mileage,
                    COALESCE(SUM(CASE WHEN t.fuel_theft_detected THEN 1 ELSE 0 END), 0) as theft_events,
                    COALESCE(SUM(t.fuel_theft_amount), 0) as theft_amount,
                    (
                        SELECT AVG(f.level_percent)
                        FROM fuel_data f
                        WHERE f.vehicle_id = v.id
                        AND f.recorded_at >= $2
                        AND f.recorded_at <= $3
                    ) as avg_fuel_level
                FROM vehicles v
                LEFT JOIN trips t ON v.id = t.vehicle_id
                    AND t.start_time >= $2
                    AND t.end_time <= $3
                WHERE v.client_id = $1
                GROUP BY v.id, v.registration_number, v.make, v.model
                HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT t.id) > 0
            `, [clientId, startDate, endDate]);

            const fuelPricePerLiter = 1.5; // USD

            const report = {
                reportId: `fuel-${clientId}-${startDate}-${endDate}`,
                generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
                period: { startDate, endDate },
                vehicles: fuelData.rows.map(v => ({
                    ...v,
                    distanceKm: (v.total_distance / 1000).toFixed(2),
                    fuelLiters: parseFloat(v.total_fuel).toFixed(2),
                    mileage: parseFloat(v.avg_mileage).toFixed(2),
                    fuelCost: (v.total_fuel * fuelPricePerLiter).toFixed(2),
                    theftAmount: parseFloat(v.theft_amount).toFixed(2),
                    avgFuelLevel: parseFloat(v.avg_fuel_level)?.toFixed(1) || 0
                })),
                summary: {
                    totalFuel: fuelData.rows.reduce((sum, v) => sum + parseFloat(v.total_fuel), 0).toFixed(2),
                    totalCost: fuelData.rows.reduce((sum, v) => sum + (v.total_fuel * fuelPricePerLiter), 0).toFixed(2),
                    averageMileage: (fuelData.rows.reduce((sum, v) => 
                        sum + parseFloat(v.avg_mileage), 0) / fuelData.rows.length).toFixed(2),
                    theftEvents: fuelData.rows.reduce((sum, v) => sum + parseInt(v.theft_events), 0),
                    theftLoss: fuelData.rows.reduce((sum, v) => sum + parseFloat(v.theft_amount), 0).toFixed(2)
                }
            };

            return report;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Generate fuel report error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Generate alert summary report
     */
    async generateAlertReport(clientId, startDate, endDate) {
        try {
            const alerts = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    ae.*,
                    ar.name as rule_name,
                    ar.type as rule_type,
                    ar.severity as rule_severity,
                    v.registration_number,
                    v.make,
                    v.model,
                    u.full_name as acknowledged_by_name,
                    u2.full_name as resolved_by_name
                FROM alert_events ae
                JOIN alert_rules ar ON ae.rule_id = ar.id
                JOIN vehicles v ON ae.vehicle_id = v.id
                LEFT JOIN users u ON ae.acknowledged_by = u.id
                LEFT JOIN users u2 ON ae.resolved_by = u2.id
                WHERE v.client_id = $1
                AND ae.triggered_at >= $2
                AND ae.triggered_at <= $3
                ORDER BY ae.triggered_at DESC
            `, [clientId, startDate, endDate]);

            // Group by type and severity
            const byType = {};
            const bySeverity = { CRITICAL: 0, WARNING: 0, INFO: 0 };
            const byVehicle = {};

            alerts.rows.forEach(alert => {
                // By type
                if (!byType[alert.rule_type]) {
                    byType[alert.rule_type] = 0;
                }
                byType[alert.rule_type]++;

                // By severity
                bySeverity[alert.rule_severity]++;

                // By vehicle
                if (!byVehicle[alert.registration_number]) {
                    byVehicle[alert.registration_number] = 0;
                }
                byVehicle[alert.registration_number]++;
            });

            // Calculate response times
            const responseTimes = alerts.rows
                .filter(a => a.acknowledged_at)
                .map(a => (new Date(a.acknowledged_at) - new Date(a.triggered_at)) / 1000 / 60); // minutes

            const avgResponseTime = responseTimes.length > 0
                ? responseTimes.reduce((sum, t) => sum + t, 0) / responseTimes.length
                : 0;

            return {
                reportId: `alerts-${clientId}-${startDate}-${endDate}`,
                generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
                period: { startDate, endDate },
                totalAlerts: alerts.rows.length,
                byType,
                bySeverity,
                byVehicle,
                alerts: alerts.rows,
                statistics: {
                    avgResponseTime: avgResponseTime.toFixed(1),
                    resolutionRate: alerts.rows.length > 0
                        ? (alerts.rows.filter(a => a.status === 'RESOLVED').length / alerts.rows.length * 100).toFixed(1)
                        : 0,
                    mostActiveVehicle: Object.entries(byVehicle)
                        .sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])[0] || null
                }
            };

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Generate alert report error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Export to Excel
     */
    async exportToExcel(data, type) {
        const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();
        const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('Report');

        // Add title
        worksheet.mergeCells('A1:E1');
        const titleRow = worksheet.getCell('A1');
        titleRow.value = `${type.toUpperCase()} REPORT`;
        titleRow.font = { size: 16, bold: true };
        titleRow.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };

        // Add generated date
        worksheet.mergeCells('A2:E2');
        const dateRow = worksheet.getCell('A2');
        dateRow.value = `Generated: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}`;
        dateRow.font = { italic: true };
        dateRow.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };

        let currentRow = 4;

        switch(type) {
            case 'daily':
                currentRow = this.addDailySheet(worksheet, data, currentRow);
                break;
            case 'fleet':
                currentRow = this.addFleetSheet(worksheet, data, currentRow);
                break;
            case 'drivers':
                currentRow = this.addDriversSheet(worksheet, data, currentRow);
                break;
            case 'fuel':
                currentRow = this.addFuelSheet(worksheet, data, currentRow);
                break;
            case 'alerts':
                currentRow = this.addAlertsSheet(worksheet, data, currentRow);
                break;
        }

        return workbook;
    }

    /**
     * Export to PDF
     */
    async exportToPDF(data, type) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const doc = new PDFDocument({ margin: 50, size: 'A4' });
            const chunks = [];

            doc.on('data', chunk => chunks.push(chunk));
            doc.on('end', () => resolve(Buffer.concat(chunks)));
            doc.on('error', reject);

            // Add header
            doc.fontSize(20).text(`${type.toUpperCase()} REPORT`, { align: 'center' });
            doc.moveDown();
            doc.fontSize(10).text(`Generated: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}`, { align: 'center' });
            doc.moveDown();
            doc.moveDown();

            // Add content based on type
            switch(type) {
                case 'daily':
                    this.addDailyPDF(doc, data);
                    break;
                case 'fleet':
                    this.addFleetPDF(doc, data);
                    break;
                case 'drivers':
                    this.addDriversPDF(doc, data);
                    break;
                case 'fuel':
                    this.addFuelPDF(doc, data);
                    break;
                case 'alerts':
                    this.addAlertsPDF(doc, data);
                    break;
            }

            doc.end();
        });
    }

    /**
     * Add daily report to Excel
     */
    addDailySheet(worksheet, data, startRow) {
        // Summary section
        worksheet.addRow(['SUMMARY']);
        worksheet.getRow(startRow).font = { bold: true };
        startRow++;

        worksheet.addRow(['Date', data.date]);
        worksheet.addRow(['Total Vehicles', data.vehicleCount]);
        worksheet.addRow(['Active Vehicles', data.activeVehicles]);
        worksheet.addRow(['Total Trips', data.summary.trips.count]);
        worksheet.addRow(['Total Distance (km)', (data.summary.trips.totalDistance / 1000).toFixed(2)]);
        worksheet.addRow(['Total Alerts', data.summary.alerts.total]);
        startRow += 6;

        // Trips section
        worksheet.addRow(['TRIPS']);
        worksheet.getRow(startRow).font = { bold: true };
        startRow++;

        const tripsHeader = ['Vehicle', 'Start Time', 'End Time', 'Distance (km)', 'Duration (min)', 'Max Speed'];
        worksheet.addRow(tripsHeader);
        worksheet.getRow(startRow).font = { bold: true };
        startRow++;

        data.trips.forEach(trip => {
            worksheet.addRow([
                trip.registration_number,
                new Date(trip.start_time).toLocaleString(),
                new Date(trip.end_time).toLocaleString(),
                (trip.distance_meters / 1000).toFixed(2),
                Math.round(trip.duration_seconds / 60),
                trip.max_speed
            ]);
            startRow++;
        });

        startRow += 2;

        // Alerts section
        worksheet.addRow(['ALERTS']);
        worksheet.getRow(startRow).font = { bold: true };
        startRow++;

        const alertsHeader = ['Vehicle', 'Type', 'Severity', 'Time', 'Status'];
        worksheet.addRow(alertsHeader);
        worksheet.getRow(startRow).font = { bold: true };
        startRow++;

        data.alerts.forEach(alert => {
            worksheet.addRow([
                alert.registration_number,
                alert.rule_name,
                alert.severity,
                new Date(alert.triggered_at).toLocaleString(),
                alert.status
            ]);
            startRow++;
        });

        return startRow;
    }

    /**
     * Calculate safety score
     */
    calculateSafetyScore(driver) {
        const incidents = driver.total_overspeed + 
                         driver.total_harsh_braking + 
                         driver.total_harsh_acceleration;
        
        const baseScore = 100;
        const penalty = Math.min(incidents * 2, 50);
        
        return Math.max(0, baseScore - penalty).toFixed(1);
    }

    /**
     * Calculate efficiency score
     */
    calculateEfficiencyScore(driver) {
        // Based on fuel consumption, idle time, etc.
        // Simplified version
        return driver.avg_score;
    }
}

module.exports = new ReportService();
📦 File 3: /backend/jobs/kpi-processor.js
javascript
/**
 * KPI Processor Job
 * Pre-calculates KPIs for faster dashboard loading
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const kpiService = require('../services/kpi.service');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);

class KPIProcessor {
    constructor() {
        this.isRunning = false;
    }

    /**
     * Start the processor
     */
    start() {
        if (this.isRunning) return;
        
        this.isRunning = true;
        console.log('KPI processor started');

        // Update every 5 minutes
        setInterval(() => this.updateAllKPIs(), 5 * 60 * 1000);
        
        // Also run immediately
        this.updateAllKPIs();
    }

    /**
     * Update all KPIs
     */
    async updateAllKPIs() {
        try {
            console.log('Updating all KPIs...');

            // Get all clients
            const clients = await pool.query(`
                SELECT id FROM clients WHERE is_active = true
            `);

            // Update each client's KPIs
            for (const client of clients.rows) {
                await this.updateClientKPIs(client.id);
            }

            // Update admin KPIs
            await this.updateAdminKPIs();

            console.log(`KPI update completed for ${clients.rows.length} clients`);

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Update all KPIs error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Update client KPIs
     */
    async updateClientKPIs(clientId) {
        try {
            const timeRanges = ['today', 'yesterday', 'week', 'month', 'quarter', 'year'];

            for (const range of timeRanges) {
                const kpis = await kpiService.getClientKPIs(clientId, range);
                
                // Cache is already set by getClientKPIs
                // Store in Redis with appropriate TTL
                await redis.setex(
                    `kpi:precalc:client:${clientId}:${range}`,
                    3600, // 1 hour
                    JSON.stringify(kpis)
                );
            }

        } catch (error) {
            console.error(`Update client ${clientId} KPIs error:`, error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Update admin KPIs
     */
    async updateAdminKPIs() {
        try {
            const timeRanges = ['today', 'week', 'month', 'quarter', 'year'];

            for (const range of timeRanges) {
                const kpis = await kpiService.getAdminKPIs(range);
                
                await redis.setex(
                    `kpi:precalc:admin:${range}`,
                    3600,
                    JSON.stringify(kpis)
                );
            }

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Update admin KPIs error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Stop the processor
     */
    stop() {
        this.isRunning = false;
        console.log('KPI processor stopped');
    }
}

module.exports = new KPIProcessor();

/**
 * Reports API Routes
 */

const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const reportService = require('../../services/report.service');
const kpiService = require('../../services/kpi.service');
const auth = require('../../middlewares/auth');

/**
 * Get dashboard KPIs
 * GET /api/v1/reports/kpis
 */
router.get('/kpis', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { range = 'today' } = req.query;
        
        let kpis;
        if (req.user.role === 'ADMIN' || req.user.role === 'SUPER_ADMIN') {
            kpis = await kpiService.getAdminKPIs(range);
        } else {
            kpis = await kpiService.getClientKPIs(req.user.clientId, range);
        }

        res.json(kpis);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Get KPIs error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get KPIs' });
    }
});

/**
 * Generate daily report
 * GET /api/v1/reports/daily
 */
router.get('/daily', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { date = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] } = req.query;
        
        const report = await reportService.generateDailyReport(
            req.user.clientId,
            date
        );

        res.json(report);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Generate daily report error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to generate report' });
    }
});

/**
 * Generate fleet report
 * GET /api/v1/reports/fleet
 */
router.get('/fleet', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { startDate, endDate } = req.query;
        
        const report = await reportService.generateFleetReport(
            req.user.clientId,
            startDate,
            endDate
        );

        res.json(report);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Generate fleet report error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to generate report' });
    }
});

/**
 * Generate driver report
 * GET /api/v1/reports/drivers

router.get('/drivers', auth, async (req, res) => {

        const report = await reportService.generateDriverReport(
            req.user.clientId,
            startDate,
            endDate
        );

        res.json(report);

    } catch (error) {

        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to generate report' });
    }
});

/**
 * Generate fuel report
 * GET /api/v1/reports/fuel
 */
router.get('/fuel', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { startDate, endDate } = req.query;
        
        const report = await reportService.generateFuelReport(
            req.user.clientId,
            startDate,
            endDate
        );

        res.json(report);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Generate fuel report error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to generate report' });
    }
});

/**
 * Generate alert report
 * GET /api/v1/reports/alerts
 */
router.get('/alerts', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { startDate, endDate } = req.query;
        
        const report = await reportService.generateAlertReport(
            req.user.clientId,
            startDate,
            endDate
        );

        res.json(report);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Generate alert report error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to generate report' });
    }
});

/**
 * Export report
 * GET /api/v1/reports/export/:type
 */
router.get('/export/:type', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { type } = req.params;
        const { format = 'excel', ...params } = req.query;

        let data;
        switch(type) {
            case 'daily':
                data = await reportService.generateDailyReport(
                    req.user.clientId,
                    params.date
                );
                break;
            case 'fleet':
                data = await reportService.generateFleetReport(
                    req.user.clientId,
                    params.startDate,
                    params.endDate
                );
                break;
            case 'drivers':
                data = await reportService.generateDriverReport(
                    req.user.clientId,
                    params.startDate,
                    params.endDate
                );
                break;
            case 'fuel':
                data = await reportService.generateFuelReport(
                    req.user.clientId,
                    params.startDate,
                    params.endDate
                );
                break;
            case 'alerts':
                data = await reportService.generateAlertReport(
                    req.user.clientId,
                    params.startDate,
                    params.endDate
                );
                break;
            default:
                return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid report type' });
        }

        let fileBuffer;
        let contentType;
        let filename;

        if (format === 'excel') {
            const workbook = await reportService.exportToExcel(data, type);
            fileBuffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();
            contentType = 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet';
            filename = `${type}-report-${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.xlsx`;
        } else if (format === 'pdf') {
            fileBuffer = await reportService.exportToPDF(data, type);
            contentType = 'application/pdf';
            filename = `${type}-report-${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.pdf`;
        } else {
            return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid format' });
        }

        res.setHeader('Content-Type', contentType);
        res.setHeader('Content-Disposition', `attachment; filename="${filename}"`);
        res.send(fileBuffer);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Export report error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to export report' });
    }
});

module.exports = router;
