/**
 * Client Dashboard Page
 * Shows all KPIs and reports for client
 */

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import {
    LineChart, Line, BarChart, Bar, PieChart, Pie, Cell,
    XAxis, YAxis, CartesianGrid, Tooltip, Legend, ResponsiveContainer
} from 'recharts';
import { reportService } from '../services/report.service';
import KpiCards from '../components/dashboard/KpiCards';
import DateRangePicker from '../components/dashboard/DateRangePicker';
import ExportButtons from '../components/exports/ExportButtons';
import './ClientDashboard.css';

const ClientDashboard = () => {
    const [kpis, setKpis] = useState(null);
    const [dateRange, setDateRange] = useState({
        range: 'today',
        startDate: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0],
        endDate: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]
    });
    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('overview');

    // Load KPIs
    useEffect(() => {
        loadKPIs();
        
        // Refresh every 30 seconds
        const interval = setInterval(loadKPIs, 30000);
        
        return () => clearInterval(interval);
    }, [dateRange]);

    const loadKPIs = async () => {
        try {
            setLoading(true);
            const data = await reportService.getKPIs(dateRange.range);
            setKpis(data);
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Failed to load KPIs:', error);
        } finally {
            setLoading(false);
        }
    };

    if (loading || !kpis) {
        return (
            <div className="dashboard-loading">
                <div className="spinner"></div>
                <p>Loading dashboard...</p>
            </div>
        );
    }

    // Prepare chart data
    const fleetData = [
        { name: 'Online', value: kpis.fleet.online },
        { name: 'Offline', value: kpis.fleet.offline },
        { name: 'Moving', value: kpis.fleet.moving },
        { name: 'Idle', value: kpis.fleet.idle },
        { name: 'Stopped', value: kpis.fleet.stopped }
    ];

    const COLORS = ['#10b981', '#6b7280', '#3b82f6', '#f59e0b', '#ef4444'];

    const tripData = [
        { name: 'Distance', value: (kpis.trips.totalDistance / 1000).toFixed(1) },
        { name: 'Duration', value: Math.round(kpis.trips.totalDuration / 3600) },
        { name: 'Trips', value: kpis.trips.count }
    ];

    return (
        <div className="client-dashboard">
            {/* Header */}
            <div className="dashboard-header">
                <h1>Dashboard</h1>
                <div className="header-controls">
                    <DateRangePicker
                        value={dateRange}
                        onChange={setDateRange}
                    />
                    <ExportButtons
                        type="dashboard"
                        data={kpis}
                        dateRange={dateRange}
                    />
                </div>
            </div>

            {/* KPI Cards */}
            <KpiCards kpis={kpis} />

            {/* Tabs */}
            <div className="dashboard-tabs">
                <button
                    className={activeTab === 'overview' ? 'active' : ''}
                    onClick={() => setActiveTab('overview')}
                >
                    Overview
                </button>
                <button
                    className={activeTab === 'fleet' ? 'active' : ''}
                    onClick={() => setActiveTab('fleet')}
                >
                    Fleet
                </button>
                <button
                    className={activeTab === 'drivers' ? 'active' : ''}
                    onClick={() => setActiveTab('drivers')}
                >
                    Drivers
                </button>
                <button
                    className={activeTab === 'alerts' ? 'active' : ''}
                    onClick={() => setActiveTab('alerts')}
                >
                    Alerts
                </button>
                <button
                    className={activeTab === 'reports' ? 'active' : ''}
                    onClick={() => setActiveTab('reports')}
                >
                    Reports
                </button>
            </div>

            {/* Tab Content */}
            <div className="tab-content">
                {activeTab === 'overview' && (
                    <div className="overview-tab">
                        {/* Charts Row */}
                        <div className="charts-row">
                            <div className="chart-card">
                                <h3>Fleet Status</h3>
                                <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={300}>
                                    <PieChart>
                                        <Pie
                                            data={fleetData}
                                            cx="50%"
                                            cy="50%"
                                            labelLine={false}
                                            label={entry => entry.name}
                                            outerRadius={80}
                                            fill="#8884d8"
                                            dataKey="value"
                                        >
                                            {fleetData.map((entry, index) => (
                                                <Cell key={`cell-${index}`} fill={COLORS[index % COLORS.length]} />
                                            ))}
                                        </Pie>
                                        <Tooltip />
                                    </PieChart>
                                </ResponsiveContainer>
                            </div>

                            <div className="chart-card">
                                <h3>Trip Summary</h3>
                                <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={300}>
                                    <BarChart data={tripData}>
                                        <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" />
                                        <XAxis dataKey="name" />
                                        <YAxis />
                                        <Tooltip />
                                        <Bar dataKey="value" fill="#3b82f6" />
                                    </BarChart>
                                </ResponsiveContainer>
                            </div>

                            <div className="chart-card">
                                <h3>Alert Distribution</h3>
                                <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={300}>
                                    <PieChart>
                                        <Pie
                                            data={[
                                                { name: 'Critical', value: kpis.alerts.critical },
                                                { name: 'Warning', value: kpis.alerts.warning },
                                                { name: 'Info', value: kpis.alerts.info }
                                            ]}
                                            cx="50%"
                                            cy="50%"
                                            labelLine={false}
                                            label={entry => entry.name}
                                            outerRadius={80}
                                            fill="#8884d8"
                                            dataKey="value"
                                        >
                                            <Cell fill="#ef4444" />
                                            <Cell fill="#f59e0b" />
                                            <Cell fill="#3b82f6" />
                                        </Pie>
                                        <Tooltip />
                                    </PieChart>
                                </ResponsiveContainer>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        {/* Quick Stats */}
                        <div className="quick-stats">
                            <div className="stat-card">
                                <div className="stat-icon">🚗</div>
                                <div className="stat-content">
                                    <div className="stat-label">Fleet Utilization</div>
                                    <div className="stat-value">{kpis.utilization.currentUtilization}%</div>
                                    <div className="stat-trend positive">
                                        ↑ 5% from yesterday
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </div>

                            <div className="stat-card">
                                <div className="stat-icon">⚠️</div>
                                <div className="stat-content">
                                    <div className="stat-label">Active Alerts</div>
                                    <div className="stat-value">{kpis.alerts.active}</div>
                                    <div className="stat-trend negative">
                                        {kpis.alerts.critical} critical
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </div>

                            <div className="stat-card">
                                <div className="stat-icon">⛽</div>
                                <div className="stat-content">
                                    <div className="stat-label">Fuel Efficiency</div>
                                    <div className="stat-value">{kpis.fuel.averageMileage} km/l</div>
                                    <div className="stat-trend positive">
                                        Cost: ${kpis.fuel.costEstimate}
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </div>

                            <div className="stat-card">
                                <div className="stat-icon">👤</div>
                                <div className="stat-content">
                                    <div className="stat-label">Driver Score</div>
                                    <div className="stat-value">{kpis.drivers.averageScore}</div>
                                    <div className="stat-trend">
                                        {kpis.drivers.riskDistribution.low} low risk
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                )}

                {activeTab === 'fleet' && (
                    <div className="fleet-tab">
                        {/* Fleet details table */}
                        <table className="data-table">
                            <thead>
                                <tr>
                                    <th>Vehicle</th>
                                    <th>Status</th>
                                    <th>Trips</th>
                                    <th>Distance (km)</th>
                                    <th>Duration (hrs)</th>
                                    <th>Utilization</th>
                                </tr>
                            </thead>
                            <tbody>
                                {kpis.fleet.vehicles?.map(vehicle => (
                                    <tr key={vehicle.id}>
                                        <td>{vehicle.registration_number}</td>
                                        <td>
                                            <span className={`status-badge ${vehicle.current_status}`}>
                                                {vehicle.current_status}
                                            </span>
                                        </td>
                                        <td>{vehicle.trip_count}</td>
                                        <td>{(vehicle.total_distance / 1000).toFixed(1)}</td>
                                        <td>{(vehicle.total_duration / 3600).toFixed(1)}</td>
                                        <td>{vehicle.utilizationRate}%</td>
                                    </tr>
                                ))}
                            </tbody>
                        </table>
                    </div>
                )}

                {activeTab === 'drivers' && (
                    <div className="drivers-tab">
                        <div className="driver-stats">
                            <div className="score-card">
                                <h4>Top Drivers</h4>
                                {kpis.drivers.topDrivers.map((driver, index) => (
                                    <div key={index} className="driver-row">
                                        <span className="driver-rank">#{index + 1}</span>
                                        <span className="driver-name">{driver.driver_name}</span>
                                        <span className="driver-score">{driver.overall_score}</span>
                                    </div>
                                ))}
                            </div>

                            <div className="score-card">
                                <h4>Needs Improvement</h4>
                                {kpis.drivers.improvementNeeded.map((driver, index) => (
                                    <div key={index} className="driver-row">
                                        <span className="driver-rank">#{index + 1}</span>
                                        <span className="driver-name">{driver.driver_name}</span>
                                        <span className="driver-score warning">{driver.overall_score}</span>
                                    </div>
                                ))}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                )}

                {activeTab === 'alerts' && (
                    <div className="alerts-tab">
                        <div className="alert-summary">
                            <div className="alert-stat critical">
                                <span className="label">Critical</span>
                                <span className="value">{kpis.alerts.critical}</span>
                            </div>
                            <div className="alert-stat warning">
                                <span className="label">Warning</span>
                                <span className="value">{kpis.alerts.warning}</span>
                            </div>
                            <div className="alert-stat info">
                                <span className="label">Info</span>
                                <span className="value">{kpis.alerts.info}</span>
                            </div>
                            <div className="alert-stat">
                                <span className="label">Resolution Rate</span>
                                <span className="value">{kpis.alerts.resolutionRate}%</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <div className="alert-types">
                            {kpis.alerts.topTypes.map((type, index) => (
                                <div key={index} className="type-item">
                                    <span className="type-name">{type.type}</span>
                                    <div className="type-bar">
                                        <div 
                                            className="type-bar-fill"
                                            style={{ width: `${(type.count / kpis.alerts.total) * 100}%` }}
                                        ></div>
                                    </div>
                                    <span className="type-count">{type.count}</span>
                                </div>
                            ))}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                )}

                {activeTab === 'reports' && (
                    <div className="reports-tab">
                        <h3>Generate Reports</h3>
                        <div className="report-options">
                            <div className="report-card">
                                <h4>Daily Activity Report</h4>
                                <p>Summary of all vehicle activity for a specific day</p>
                                <button 
                                    className="btn-primary"
                                    onClick={() => window.open(`/api/reports/export/daily?format=pdf&date=${dateRange.startDate}`, '_blank')}
                                >
                                    Download PDF
                                </button>
                            </div>

                            <div className="report-card">
                                <h4>Fleet Utilization Report</h4>
                                <p>Detailed analysis of fleet usage and efficiency</p>
                                <button 
                                    className="btn-primary"
                                    onClick={() => window.open(`/api/reports/export/fleet?format=excel&startDate=${dateRange.startDate}&endDate=${dateRange.endDate}`, '_blank')}
                                >
                                    Download Excel
                                </button>
                            </div>

                            <div className="report-card">
                                <h4>Driver Performance Report</h4>
                                <p>Driver scores, incidents, and rankings</p>
                                <button 
                                    className="btn-primary"
                                    onClick={() => window.open(`/api/reports/export/drivers?format=pdf&startDate=${dateRange.startDate}&endDate=${dateRange.endDate}`, '_blank')}
                                >
                                    Download PDF
                                </button>
                            </div>

                            <div className="report-card">
                                <h4>Fuel Report</h4>
                                <p>Fuel consumption, efficiency, and theft analysis</p>
                                <button 
                                    className="btn-primary"
                                    onClick={() => window.open(`/api/reports/export/fuel?format=excel&startDate=${dateRange.startDate}&endDate=${dateRange.endDate}`, '_blank')}
                                >
                                    Download Excel
                                </button>
                            </div>

                            <div className="report-card">
                                <h4>Alert Summary</h4>
                                <p>All alerts with response times and resolution</p>
                                <button 
                                    className="btn-primary"
                                    onClick={() => window.open(`/api/reports/export/alerts?format=pdf&startDate=${dateRange.startDate}&endDate=${dateRange.endDate}`, '_blank')}
                                >
                                    Download PDF
                                </button>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                )}
            </div>
        </div>
    );
};

/**
 * Admin Dashboard Page
 * Shows system-wide KPIs and client management
 */

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { reportService } from '../services/report.service';
import './AdminDashboard.css';

const AdminDashboard = () => {
    const [kpis, setKpis] = useState(null);
    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    const [dateRange, setDateRange] = useState('today');

    useEffect(() => {
        loadKPIs();
    }, [dateRange]);

    const loadKPIs = async () => {
        try {
            setLoading(true);
            const data = await reportService.getAdminKPIs(dateRange);
            setKpis(data);
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Failed to load admin KPIs:', error);
        } finally {
            setLoading(false);
        }
    };

    if (loading || !kpis) {
        return (
            <div className="dashboard-loading">
                <div className="spinner"></div>
                <p>Loading admin dashboard...</p>
            </div>
        );
    }

    return (
        <div className="admin-dashboard">
            <div className="dashboard-header">
                <h1>Admin Dashboard</h1>
                <select 
                    value={dateRange}
                    onChange={(e) => setDateRange(e.target.value)}
                    className="range-select"
                >
                    <option value="today">Today</option>
                    <option value="week">This Week</option>
                    <option value="month">This Month</option>
                    <option value="quarter">This Quarter</option>
                    <option value="year">This Year</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            {/* Summary Cards */}
            <div className="summary-cards">
                <div className="summary-card">
                    <div className="card-icon">👥</div>
                    <div className="card-content">
                        <div className="card-label">Total Clients</div>
                        <div className="card-value">{kpis.summary.totalClients}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div className="summary-card">
                    <div className="card-icon">🚗</div>
                    <div className="card-content">
                        <div className="card-label">Total Vehicles</div>
                        <div className="card-value">{kpis.summary.totalVehicles}</div>
                        <div className="card-sub">{kpis.realtime.online} online</div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div className="summary-card">
                    <div className="card-icon">📊</div>
                    <div className="card-content">
                        <div className="card-label">Total Distance</div>
                        <div className="card-value">{kpis.summary.totalDistance} km</div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div className="summary-card">
                    <div className="card-icon">💰</div>
                    <div className="card-content">
                        <div className="card-label">Revenue</div>
                        <div className="card-value">${kpis.summary.totalRevenue}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div className="summary-card">
                    <div className="card-icon">⚠️</div>
                    <div className="card-content">
                        <div className="card-label">Total Alerts</div>
                        <div className="card-value">{kpis.summary.totalAlerts}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div className="summary-card">
                    <div className="card-icon">⚙️</div>
                    <div className="card-content">
                        <div className="card-label">System Health</div>
                        <div className="card-value">{kpis.system.commandSuccessRate}%</div>
                        <div className="card-sub">command success</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            {/* System Health */}
            <div className="system-health">
                <h2>System Health</h2>
                <div className="health-grid">
                    <div className="health-item">
                        <span className="health-label">Database</span>
                        <span className={`health-status ${kpis.system.database}`}>
                            {kpis.system.database}
                        </span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="health-item">
                        <span className="health-label">Redis</span>
                        <span className={`health-status ${kpis.system.redis}`}>
                            {kpis.system.redis}
                        </span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="health-item">
                        <span className="health-label">Errors (1h)</span>
                        <span className="health-status">{kpis.system.errorCount}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="health-item">
                        <span className="health-label">Uptime</span>
                        <span className="health-status">
                            {Math.floor(kpis.system.uptime / 3600)}h {Math.floor((kpis.system.uptime % 3600) / 60)}m
                        </span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            {/* Client Breakdown */}
            <div className="client-breakdown">
                <h2>Clients</h2>
                <table className="client-table">
                    <thead>
                        <tr>
                            <th>Client</th>
                            <th>Vehicles</th>
                            <th>Devices</th>
                            <th>Actions</th>
                        </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                        {kpis.clients.map(client => (
                            <tr key={client.id}>
                                <td>{client.name}</td>
                                <td>{client.vehicles}</td>
                                <td>{client.devices}</td>
                                <td>
                                    <button 
                                        className="btn-view"
                                        onClick={() => window.location.href = `/admin/clients/${client.id}`}
                                    >
                                        View
                                    </button>
                                </td>
                            </tr>
                        ))}
                    </tbody>
                </table>
            </div>
        </div>
    );
};

    cursor: pointer;
    font-size: 12px;
}

.btn-view:hover {
    background: #2563eb;
}
`;

const style = document.createElement('style');
style.textContent = styles;
document.head.appendChild(style);

export default AdminDashboard;

/**
 * Report Service
 * API calls for reports and KPIs
 */

import axios from 'axios';

const API_URL = process.env.REACT_APP_API_URL;

class ReportService {
    /**
     * Get client KPIs
     */
    async getKPIs(range = 'today') {
        const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/reports/kpis`, {
            params: { range },
            headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}` }
        });
        return response.data;
    }

    /**
     * Get admin KPIs
     */
    async getAdminKPIs(range = 'today') {
        const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/reports/kpis`, {
            params: { range, admin: true },
            headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}` }
        });
        return response.data;
    }

    /**
     * Generate daily report
     */
    async getDailyReport(date) {
        const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/reports/daily`, {
            params: { date },
            headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}` }
        });
        return response.data;
    }

    /**
     * Generate fleet report
     */
    async getFleetReport(startDate, endDate) {
        const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/reports/fleet`, {
            params: { startDate, endDate },
            headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}` }
        });
        return response.data;
    }

    /**
     * Generate driver report
     */
    async getDriverReport(startDate, endDate) {
        const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/reports/drivers`, {
            params: { startDate, endDate },
            headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}` }
        });
        return response.data;
    }

    /**
     * Generate fuel report
     */
    async getFuelReport(startDate, endDate) {
        const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/reports/fuel`, {
            params: { startDate, endDate },
            headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}` }
        });
        return response.data;
    }

    /**
     * Generate alert report
     */
    async getAlertReport(startDate, endDate) {
        const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/reports/alerts`, {
            params: { startDate, endDate },
            headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}` }
        });
        return response.data;
    }

    /**
     * Export report
     */
    async exportReport(type, format, params) {
        const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/reports/export/${type}`, {
            params: { format, ...params },
            headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}` },
            responseType: 'blob'
        });

        // Create download link
        const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([response.data]));
        const link = document.createElement('a');
        link.href = url;
        link.setAttribute('download', `report.${format === 'excel' ? 'xlsx' : 'pdf'}`);
        document.body.appendChild(link);
        link.click();
        link.remove();
    }
}

export const reportService = new ReportService();

javascript
/**
 * Billing Service
 * Main billing logic for subscriptions and payments
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const moment = require('moment');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);

class BillingService {
    /**
     * Create new subscription
     */
    async createSubscription(clientId, planId, options = {}) {
        const client = await pool.connect();
        
        try {
            await client.query('BEGIN');

            // Get plan details
            const plan = await client.query(`
                SELECT * FROM plans WHERE id = $1 AND is_active = true
            `, [planId]);

            if (plan.rows.length === 0) {
                throw new Error('Plan not found');
            }

            // Calculate dates
            const startDate = new Date();
            const endDate = this.calculateEndDate(startDate, plan.rows[0].billing_cycle);

            // Check for existing active subscription
            const existing = await client.query(`
                SELECT id FROM subscriptions 
                WHERE client_id = $1 
                AND status IN ('ACTIVE', 'GRACE')
            `, [clientId]);

            if (existing.rows.length > 0) {
                // Upgrade/downgrade existing subscription
                return await this.upgradeSubscription(
                    clientId, 
                    existing.rows[0].id, 
                    planId, 
                    options
                );
            }

            // Create new subscription
            const subscription = await client.query(`
                INSERT INTO subscriptions (
                    id, client_id, plan_id,
                    start_date, end_date,
                    status, auto_renew,
                    price_monthly, price_yearly,
                    setup_fee, device_limit,
                    created_by
                ) VALUES (
                    $1, $2, $3, $4, $5,
                    'ACTIVE', $6,
                    $7, $8, $9, $10,
                    $11
                ) RETURNING *
            `, [
                uuidv4(),
                clientId,
                planId,
                startDate,
                endDate,
                options.autoRenew ?? true,
                plan.rows[0].price_monthly,
                plan.rows[0].price_yearly,
                plan.rows[0].setup_fee || 0,
                plan.rows[0].max_vehicles,
                options.createdBy || null
            ]);

            // Create initial invoice if setup fee exists
            if (plan.rows[0].setup_fee > 0) {
                await this.createInvoice(clientId, subscription.rows[0].id, {
                    amount: plan.rows[0].setup_fee,
                    type: 'SETUP',
                    dueDate: new Date()
                });
            }

            // Update client's current plan
            await client.query(`
                UPDATE clients 
                SET current_plan_id = $1,
                    updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $2
            `, [planId, clientId]);

            // Log audit
            await this.logAudit({
                clientId,
                action: 'SUBSCRIPTION_CREATED',
                details: {
                    planId,
                    startDate,
                    endDate
                }
            });

            await client.query('COMMIT');

            // Clear cache
            await redis.del(`billing:client:${clientId}`);
            await redis.del(`subscription:client:${clientId}`);

            return subscription.rows[0];

        } catch (error) {
            await client.query('ROLLBACK');
            console.error('Create subscription error:', error);
            throw error;
        } finally {
            client.release();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Upgrade/downgrade subscription
     */
    async upgradeSubscription(clientId, subscriptionId, newPlanId, options) {
        const client = await pool.connect();
        
        try {
            await client.query('BEGIN');

            // Get current subscription
            const current = await client.query(`
                SELECT s.*, p.name as plan_name
                FROM subscriptions s
                JOIN plans p ON s.plan_id = p.id
                WHERE s.id = $1
            `, [subscriptionId]);

            if (current.rows.length === 0) {
                throw new Error('Subscription not found');
            }

            // Get new plan
            const newPlan = await client.query(`
                SELECT * FROM plans WHERE id = $1
            `, [newPlanId]);

            if (newPlan.rows.length === 0) {
                throw new Error('New plan not found');
            }

            // Calculate prorated amount
            const proratedAmount = await this.calculateProratedAmount(
                current.rows[0],
                newPlan.rows[0]
            );

            // End current subscription
            await client.query(`
                UPDATE subscriptions 
                SET status = 'UPGRADED',
                    end_date = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
                    updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $1
            `, [subscriptionId]);

            // Create new subscription
            const startDate = new Date();
            const endDate = this.calculateEndDate(startDate, newPlan.rows[0].billing_cycle);

            const newSubscription = await client.query(`
                INSERT INTO subscriptions (
                    id, client_id, plan_id,
                    start_date, end_date,
                    status, auto_renew,
                    price_monthly, price_yearly,
                    setup_fee, device_limit,
                    previous_subscription_id,
                    created_by
                ) VALUES (
                    $1, $2, $3, $4, $5,
                    'ACTIVE', $6,
                    $7, $8, $9, $10,
                    $11, $12
                ) RETURNING *
            `, [
                uuidv4(),
                clientId,
                newPlanId,
                startDate,
                endDate,
                options.autoRenew ?? true,
                newPlan.rows[0].price_monthly,
                newPlan.rows[0].price_yearly,
                newPlan.rows[0].setup_fee || 0,
                newPlan.rows[0].max_vehicles,
                subscriptionId,
                options.createdBy || null
            ]);

            // Create invoice for prorated amount if > 0
            if (proratedAmount > 0) {
                await this.createInvoice(clientId, newSubscription.rows[0].id, {
                    amount: proratedAmount,
                    type: 'PRORATED_UPGRADE',
                    dueDate: new Date(),
                    metadata: {
                        previousPlan: current.rows[0].plan_name,
                        newPlan: newPlan.rows[0].name
                    }
                });
            }

            // Log audit
            await this.logAudit({
                clientId,
                action: 'SUBSCRIPTION_UPGRADED',
                details: {
                    fromPlan: current.rows[0].plan_id,
                    toPlan: newPlanId,
                    proratedAmount
                }
            });

            await client.query('COMMIT');

            return newSubscription.rows[0];

        } catch (error) {
            await client.query('ROLLBACK');
            console.error('Upgrade subscription error:', error);
            throw error;
        } finally {
            client.release();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Cancel subscription
     */
    async cancelSubscription(subscriptionId, reason, cancelledBy) {
        const client = await pool.connect();
        
        try {
            await client.query('BEGIN');

            const subscription = await client.query(`
                UPDATE subscriptions 
                SET status = 'CANCELLED',
                    cancelled_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
                    cancellation_reason = $1,
                    cancelled_by = $2,
                    auto_renew = false,
                    updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $3
                RETURNING *
            `, [reason, cancelledBy, subscriptionId]);

            if (subscription.rows.length === 0) {
                throw new Error('Subscription not found');
            }

            // Update client
            await client.query(`
                UPDATE clients 
                SET current_plan_id = NULL,
                    updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $1
            `, [subscription.rows[0].client_id]);

            // Disable all devices
            await client.query(`
                UPDATE devices 
                SET is_subscription_active = false,
                    status = 'suspended',
                    updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE client_id = $1
            `, [subscription.rows[0].client_id]);

            // Log audit
            await this.logAudit({
                clientId: subscription.rows[0].client_id,
                action: 'SUBSCRIPTION_CANCELLED',
                details: { reason }
            });

            await client.query('COMMIT');

            // Clear cache
            await redis.del(`subscription:client:${subscription.rows[0].client_id}`);

            return subscription.rows[0];

        } catch (error) {
            await client.query('ROLLBACK');
            console.error('Cancel subscription error:', error);
            throw error;
        } finally {
            client.release();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get client subscription
     */
    async getClientSubscription(clientId) {
        try {
            // Try cache first
            const cached = await redis.get(`subscription:client:${clientId}`);
            if (cached) {
                return JSON.parse(cached);
            }

            const subscription = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    s.*,
                    p.name as plan_name,
                    p.description as plan_description,
                    p.features,
                    p.price_monthly,
                    p.price_yearly,
                    p.max_vehicles,
                    p.max_drivers,
                    p.data_retention_days,
                    p.support_level,
                    (
                        SELECT COUNT(*) 
                        FROM vehicles v 
                        WHERE v.client_id = s.client_id 
                        AND v.is_active = true
                    ) as current_vehicles,
                    (
                        SELECT COUNT(*) 
                        FROM devices d 
                        JOIN vehicles v ON d.id = v.current_device_id
                        WHERE v.client_id = s.client_id 
                        AND d.is_active = true
                    ) as current_devices
                FROM subscriptions s
                JOIN plans p ON s.plan_id = p.id
                WHERE s.client_id = $1
                AND s.status IN ('ACTIVE', 'GRACE')
                ORDER BY s.created_at DESC
                LIMIT 1
            `, [clientId]);

            if (subscription.rows.length === 0) {
                return null;
            }

            const result = {
                ...subscription.rows[0],
                daysRemaining: this.calculateDaysRemaining(subscription.rows[0].end_date),
                isExpired: new Date(subscription.rows[0].end_date) < new Date(),
                isInGrace: subscription.rows[0].status === 'GRACE',
                usage: {
                    vehicles: parseInt(subscription.rows[0].current_vehicles),
                    devices: parseInt(subscription.rows[0].current_devices),
                    vehicleLimit: subscription.rows[0].max_vehicles,
                    deviceLimit: subscription.rows[0].max_vehicles, // Usually same as vehicles
                    vehiclePercentage: (subscription.rows[0].current_vehicles / subscription.rows[0].max_vehicles * 100).toFixed(1),
                    canAddVehicles: subscription.rows[0].current_vehicles < subscription.rows[0].max_vehicles
                }
            };

            // Cache for 5 minutes
            await redis.setex(`subscription:client:${clientId}`, 300, JSON.stringify(result));

            return result;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Get client subscription error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Check subscription status
     */
    async checkSubscriptionStatus(deviceId) {
        try {
            const device = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    d.*,
                    s.status as subscription_status,
                    s.end_date as subscription_end_date,
                    s.grace_period_end
                FROM devices d
                LEFT JOIN subscriptions s ON d.client_id = s.client_id
                WHERE d.id = $1
                AND s.status IN ('ACTIVE', 'GRACE')
            `, [deviceId]);

            if (device.rows.length === 0) {
                return {
                    active: false,
                    reason: 'NO_ACTIVE_SUBSCRIPTION'
                };
            }

            const sub = device.rows[0];
            const now = new Date();

            // Check if expired
            if (new Date(sub.subscription_end_date) < now) {
                // Check grace period
                if (sub.grace_period_end && new Date(sub.grace_period_end) > now) {
                    return {
                        active: true,
                        inGrace: true,
                        graceDaysRemaining: Math.ceil((new Date(sub.grace_period_end) - now) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24))
                    };
                }
                return {
                    active: false,
                    reason: 'EXPIRED'
                };
            }

            return {
                active: true,
                inGrace: false,
                expiresIn: Math.ceil((new Date(sub.subscription_end_date) - now) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24))
            };

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Check subscription status error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Create invoice
     */
    async createInvoice(clientId, subscriptionId, data) {
        try {
            const invoice = await pool.query(`
                INSERT INTO invoices (
                    id, subscription_id, client_id,
                    invoice_number, amount, tax_amount,
                    total_amount, currency, due_date,
                    status, items, created_at
                ) VALUES (
                    $1, $2, $3,
                    $4, $5, $6,
                    $7, $8, $9,
                    'PENDING', $10, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                ) RETURNING *
            `, [
                uuidv4(),
                subscriptionId,
                clientId,
                await this.generateInvoiceNumber(),
                data.amount,
                data.taxAmount || 0,
                data.amount + (data.taxAmount || 0),
                data.currency || 'USD',
                data.dueDate,
                JSON.stringify(data.items || [{ description: data.type, amount: data.amount }])
            ]);

            // Queue invoice email
            await redis.lpush('email:queue', JSON.stringify({
                type: 'invoice',
                clientId,
                invoiceId: invoice.rows[0].id
            }));

            return invoice.rows[0];

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Create invoice error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Process payment
     */
    async processPayment(invoiceId, paymentMethod, paymentData) {
        const client = await pool.connect();
        
        try {
            await client.query('BEGIN');

            // Get invoice
            const invoice = await client.query(`
                SELECT * FROM invoices WHERE id = $1
            `, [invoiceId]);

            if (invoice.rows.length === 0) {
                throw new Error('Invoice not found');
            }

            // Create payment record
            const payment = await client.query(`
                INSERT INTO payments (
                    id, invoice_id, client_id,
                    amount, payment_method, payment_provider,
                    transaction_id, status, provider_response,
                    paid_at
                ) VALUES (
                    $1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8, $9,
                    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                ) RETURNING *
            `, [
                uuidv4(),
                invoiceId,
                invoice.rows[0].client_id,
                invoice.rows[0].total_amount,
                paymentMethod,
                paymentData.provider,
                paymentData.transactionId,
                'COMPLETED',
                JSON.stringify(paymentData)
            ]);

            // Update invoice
            await client.query(`
                UPDATE invoices 
                SET status = 'PAID',
                    paid_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
                    payment_id = $1,
                    updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $2
            `, [payment.rows[0].id, invoiceId]);

            // Update subscription if this is the first payment
            if (invoice.rows[0].type === 'SETUP' || invoice.rows[0].type === 'RENEWAL') {
                await client.query(`
                    UPDATE subscriptions 
                    SET last_payment_date = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
                        last_invoice_id = $1,
                        updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                    WHERE id = $2
                `, [invoiceId, invoice.rows[0].subscription_id]);
            }

            // Log audit
            await this.logAudit({
                clientId: invoice.rows[0].client_id,
                action: 'PAYMENT_RECEIVED',
                details: {
                    invoiceId,
                    amount: invoice.rows[0].total_amount,
                    method: paymentMethod
                }
            });

            await client.query('COMMIT');

            // Send receipt
            await redis.lpush('email:queue', JSON.stringify({
                type: 'payment_receipt',
                clientId: invoice.rows[0].client_id,
                paymentId: payment.rows[0].id
            }));

            return payment.rows[0];

        } catch (error) {
            await client.query('ROLLBACK');
            console.error('Process payment error:', error);
            throw error;
        } finally {
            client.release();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Calculate prorated amount for upgrade
     */
    async calculateProratedAmount(currentSub, newPlan) {
        const now = new Date();
        const endDate = new Date(currentSub.end_date);
        const daysRemaining = Math.ceil((endDate - now) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
        const totalDays = 30; // Assume monthly billing

        const currentDailyRate = currentSub.price_monthly / totalDays;
        const newDailyRate = newPlan.price_monthly / totalDays;
        const rateDiff = newDailyRate - currentDailyRate;

        // Only charge if new plan is more expensive
        if (rateDiff <= 0) return 0;

        return rateDiff * daysRemaining;
    }

    /**
     * Calculate end date based on billing cycle
     */
    calculateEndDate(startDate, cycle) {
        const date = moment(startDate);
        
        switch(cycle) {
            case 'MONTHLY':
                return date.add(1, 'month').toDate();
            case 'YEARLY':
                return date.add(1, 'year').toDate();
            case 'QUARTERLY':
                return date.add(3, 'months').toDate();
            default:
                return date.add(1, 'month').toDate();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Calculate days remaining
     */
    calculateDaysRemaining(endDate) {
        const now = new Date();
        const end = new Date(endDate);
        const diff = end - now;
        
        if (diff <= 0) return 0;
        return Math.ceil(diff / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    }

    /**
     * Generate invoice number
     */
    async generateInvoiceNumber() {
        const year = new Date().getFullYear();
        const month = String(new Date().getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
        
        const result = await pool.query(`
            SELECT COUNT(*) + 1 as next
            FROM invoices
            WHERE EXTRACT(YEAR FROM created_at) = $1
            AND EXTRACT(MONTH FROM created_at) = $2
        `, [year, month]);

        const next = result.rows[0].next;
        return `INV-${year}${month}-${String(next).padStart(4, '0')}`;
    }

    /**
     * Log audit entry
     */
    async logAudit({ clientId, action, details }) {
        await pool.query(`
            INSERT INTO audit_logs (
                user_id, action, entity_type, entity_id, details
            ) VALUES (
                $1, $2, 'BILLING', $3, $4
            )
        `, [null, action, clientId, JSON.stringify(details)]);
    }
}

module.exports = new BillingService();
📦 File 2: /backend/jobs/expiry-checker.js
javascript
/**
 * Expiry Checker Job
 * Checks for expiring subscriptions and sends reminders
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const moment = require('moment');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);

class ExpiryChecker {
    constructor() {
        this.isRunning = false;
    }

    /**
     * Start the checker
     */
    start() {
        if (this.isRunning) return;
        
        this.isRunning = true;
        console.log('Expiry checker started');

        // Check every hour
        setInterval(() => this.checkExpiring(), 60 * 60 * 1000);
        
        // Also check immediately
        this.checkExpiring();
    }

    /**
     * Check for expiring subscriptions
     */
    async checkExpiring() {
        try {
            console.log('Checking expiring subscriptions...');

            // Check subscriptions expiring in 7 days
            await this.checkExpiringInDays(7, '7 days');
            
            // Check subscriptions expiring in 3 days
            await this.checkExpiringInDays(3, '3 days');
            
            // Check subscriptions expiring today
            await this.checkExpiringToday();
            
            // Check expired subscriptions for grace period
            await this.checkExpired();

            console.log('Expiry check completed');

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Expiry check error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Check subscriptions expiring in X days
     */
    async checkExpiringInDays(days, label) {
        try {
            const expiring = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    s.*,
                    c.id as client_id,
                    c.company_name,
                    c.billing_email,
                    u.email as user_email,
                    u.full_name,
                    p.name as plan_name
                FROM subscriptions s
                JOIN clients c ON s.client_id = c.id
                JOIN users u ON c.user_id = u.id
                JOIN plans p ON s.plan_id = p.id
                WHERE s.status = 'ACTIVE'
                AND s.end_date::date = CURRENT_DATE + INTERVAL '${days} days'
                AND s.auto_renew = true
            `);

            for (const sub of expiring.rows) {
                // Check if reminder already sent
                const reminderKey = `reminder:sent:${sub.id}:${days}`;
                const sent = await redis.get(reminderKey);
                
                if (!sent) {
                    // Send reminder email
                    await this.sendReminderEmail(sub, days, label);
                    
                    // Mark as sent
                    await redis.setex(reminderKey, 24 * 60 * 60, '1');
                    
                    console.log(`Sent ${days} day reminder to ${sub.company_name}`);
                }
            }

        } catch (error) {
            console.error(`Check expiring in ${days} days error:`, error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Check subscriptions expiring today
     */
    async checkExpiringToday() {
        try {
            const expiring = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    s.*,
                    c.id as client_id,
                    c.company_name,
                    c.billing_email,
                    u.email as user_email,
                    u.full_name
                FROM subscriptions s
                JOIN clients c ON s.client_id = c.id
                JOIN users u ON c.user_id = u.id
                WHERE s.status = 'ACTIVE'
                AND s.end_date::date = CURRENT_DATE
                AND s.auto_renew = true
            `);

            for (const sub of expiring.rows) {
                // Auto-renew if possible
                await this.autoRenewSubscription(sub);
            }

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Check expiring today error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Check expired subscriptions
     */
    async checkExpired() {
        try {
            // Move to grace period
            const expired = await pool.query(`
                UPDATE subscriptions 
                SET status = 'GRACE',
                    grace_period_end = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP + INTERVAL '3 days',
                    updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE status = 'ACTIVE'
                AND end_date < CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                RETURNING *
            `);

            for (const sub of expired.rows) {
                // Send expiry notification
                await this.sendExpiryNotification(sub);
                
                console.log(`Subscription ${sub.id} moved to grace period`);
            }

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Check expired error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Auto-renew subscription
     */
    async autoRenewSubscription(subscription) {
        try {
            // Get default payment method
            const paymentMethod = await pool.query(`
                SELECT * FROM payment_methods 
                WHERE client_id = $1 
                AND is_default = true
            `, [subscription.client_id]);

            if (paymentMethod.rows.length === 0) {
                // No payment method - send payment reminder
                await this.sendPaymentReminder(subscription);
                return;
            }

            // Process payment
            const invoice = await pool.query(`
                INSERT INTO invoices (
                    id, subscription_id, client_id,
                    invoice_number, amount,
                    due_date, status, type
                ) VALUES (
                    $1, $2, $3, $4, $5,
                    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP + INTERVAL '7 days',
                    'PENDING', 'RENEWAL'
                ) RETURNING *
            `, [
                uuidv4(),
                subscription.id,
                subscription.client_id,
                await this.generateInvoiceNumber(),
                subscription.price_monthly
            ]);

            // Attempt payment
            await this.attemptPayment(invoice.rows[0], paymentMethod.rows[0]);

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Auto-renew error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send reminder email
     */
    async sendReminderEmail(subscription, days, label) {
        await redis.lpush('email:queue', JSON.stringify({
            type: 'subscription_reminder',
            to: subscription.billing_email || subscription.user_email,
            data: {
                name: subscription.full_name,
                company: subscription.company_name,
                days,
                label,
                endDate: moment(subscription.end_date).format('MMMM Do, YYYY'),
                planName: subscription.plan_name
            }
        }));
    }

    /**
     * Send expiry notification
     */
    async sendExpiryNotification(subscription) {
        await redis.lpush('email:queue', JSON.stringify({
            type: 'subscription_expired',
            to: subscription.billing_email || subscription.user_email,
            data: {
                name: subscription.full_name,
                company: subscription.company_name,
                graceEnd: moment(subscription.grace_period_end).format('MMMM Do, YYYY')
            }
        }));

        // Also send push notification
        await redis.lpush('push:queue', JSON.stringify({
            userId: subscription.user_id,
            title: 'Subscription Expired',
            body: 'Your subscription has expired. Service will be suspended after grace period.',
            data: { type: 'subscription_expired' }
        }));
    }

    /**
     * Send payment reminder
     */
    async sendPaymentReminder(subscription) {
        await redis.lpush('email:queue', JSON.stringify({
            type: 'payment_required',
            to: subscription.billing_email || subscription.user_email,
            data: {
                name: subscription.full_name,
                company: subscription.company_name,
                amount: subscription.price_monthly,
                endDate: moment(subscription.end_date).format('MMMM Do, YYYY')
            }
        }));
    }

    /**
     * Attempt payment
     */
    async attemptPayment(invoice, paymentMethod) {
        // This would integrate with Stripe/PayPal/etc.
        // For now, just mark as paid for testing
        await pool.query(`
            UPDATE invoices 
            SET status = 'PAID',
                paid_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
            WHERE id = $1
        `, [invoice.id]);

        // Extend subscription
        await pool.query(`
            UPDATE subscriptions 
            SET end_date = end_date + INTERVAL '1 month',
                last_payment_date = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
                updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
            WHERE id = $1
        `, [invoice.subscription_id]);
    }

    /**
     * Generate invoice number
     */
    async generateInvoiceNumber() {
        const year = new Date().getFullYear();
        const month = String(new Date().getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
        
        const result = await pool.query(`
            SELECT COUNT(*) + 1 as next
            FROM invoices
            WHERE EXTRACT(YEAR FROM created_at) = $1
            AND EXTRACT(MONTH FROM created_at) = $2
        `, [year, month]);

        const next = result.rows[0].next;
        return `INV-${year}${month}-${String(next).padStart(4, '0')}`;
    }
}

module.exports = new ExpiryChecker();
📦 File 3: /backend/jobs/service-suspender.js
javascript
/**
 * Service Suspender Job
 * Suspends services for expired subscriptions
 */

const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');

const pool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);

class ServiceSuspender {
    constructor() {
        this.isRunning = false;
    }

    /**
     * Start the suspender
     */
    start() {
        if (this.isRunning) return;
        
        this.isRunning = true;
        console.log('Service suspender started');

        // Check every 30 minutes
        setInterval(() => this.checkSuspensions(), 30 * 60 * 1000);
        
        // Also check immediately
        this.checkSuspensions();
    }

    /**
     * Check for suspensions
     */
    async checkSuspensions() {
        try {
            console.log('Checking for suspensions...');

            // Suspend expired grace periods
            await this.suspendExpiredGrace();
            
            // Restore recently paid
            await this.restorePaidSubscriptions();

            console.log('Suspension check completed');

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Suspension check error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Suspend clients with expired grace period
     */
    async suspendExpiredGrace() {
        try {
            const expired = await pool.query(`
                SELECT 
                    s.*,
                    c.id as client_id,
                    c.company_name
                FROM subscriptions s
                JOIN clients c ON s.client_id = c.id
                WHERE s.status = 'GRACE'
                AND s.grace_period_end < CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
            `);

            for (const sub of expired.rows) {
                await this.suspendClient(sub.client_id, sub);
            }

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Suspend expired grace error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Suspend a client
     */
    async suspendClient(clientId, subscription) {
        const client = await pool.connect();
        
        try {
            await client.query('BEGIN');

            // Update subscription
            await client.query(`
                UPDATE subscriptions 
                SET status = 'SUSPENDED',
                    updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE id = $1
            `, [subscription.id]);

            // Suspend all devices
            const devices = await client.query(`
                UPDATE devices 
                SET is_subscription_active = false,
                    status = 'suspended',
                    updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE client_id = $1
                AND is_active = true
                RETURNING id, imei
            `, [clientId]);

            // Disconnect active TCP sessions
            for (const device of devices.rows) {
                await redis.publish('device:suspend', JSON.stringify({
                    deviceId: device.id,
                    imei: device.imei
                }));
            }

            // Log audit
            await client.query(`
                INSERT INTO audit_logs (
                    action, entity_type, entity_id, details
                ) VALUES (
                    'SERVICE_SUSPENDED', 'CLIENT', $1, $2
                )
            `, [clientId, JSON.stringify({
                reason: 'Subscription expired',
                deviceCount: devices.rows.length
            })]);

            // Send notification
            await this.sendSuspensionNotification(clientId, subscription);

            await client.query('COMMIT');

            console.log(`Suspended client ${clientId} with ${devices.rows.length} devices`);

        } catch (error) {
            await client.query('ROLLBACK');
            console.error('Suspend client error:', error);
        } finally {
            client.release();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Restore recently paid subscriptions
     */
    async restorePaidSubscriptions() {
        try {
            const restored = await pool.query(`
                UPDATE subscriptions s
                SET status = 'ACTIVE',
                    grace_period_end = NULL,
                    updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                FROM invoices i
                WHERE s.id = i.subscription_id
                AND s.status = 'SUSPENDED'
                AND i.status = 'PAID'
                AND i.paid_at > s.updated_at
                RETURNING s.*
            `);

            for (const sub of restored.rows) {
                await this.restoreClient(sub.client_id);
                
                console.log(`Restored client ${sub.client_id}`);
            }

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Restore paid subscriptions error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Restore a client
     */
    async restoreClient(clientId) {
        try {
            // Reactivate devices
            await pool.query(`
                UPDATE devices 
                SET is_subscription_active = true,
                    status = 'offline',
                    updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                WHERE client_id = $1
            `, [clientId]);

            // Send notification
            await this.sendRestoreNotification(clientId);

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Restore client error:', error);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send suspension notification
     */
    async sendSuspensionNotification(clientId, subscription) {
        const client = await pool.query(`
            SELECT u.id as user_id, u.email, u.full_name
            FROM clients c
            JOIN users u ON c.user_id = u.id
            WHERE c.id = $1
        `, [clientId]);

        if (client.rows.length > 0) {
            await redis.lpush('email:queue', JSON.stringify({
                type: 'service_suspended',
                to: client.rows[0].email,
                data: {
                    name: client.rows[0].full_name
                }
            }));

            await redis.lpush('push:queue', JSON.stringify({
                userId: client.rows[0].user_id,
                title: 'Service Suspended',
                body: 'Your service has been suspended due to non-payment',
                data: { type: 'service_suspended' }
            }));
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send restore notification
     */
    async sendRestoreNotification(clientId) {
        const client = await pool.query(`
            SELECT u.id as user_id, u.email, u.full_name
            FROM clients c
            JOIN users u ON c.user_id = u.id
            WHERE c.id = $1
        `, [clientId]);

        if (client.rows.length > 0) {
            await redis.lpush('email:queue', JSON.stringify({
                type: 'service_restored',
                to: client.rows[0].email,
                data: {
                    name: client.rows[0].full_name
                }
            }));

            await redis.lpush('push:queue', JSON.stringify({
                userId: client.rows[0].user_id,
                title: 'Service Restored',
                body: 'Your service has been restored',
                data: { type: 'service_restored' }
            }));
        }
    }
}

module.exports = new ServiceSuspender();

/**
 * Billing API Routes
 */

const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const billingService = require('../../services/billing.service');
const auth = require('../../middlewares/auth');

/**
 * Get all plans
 * GET /api/v1/billing/plans
 */
router.get('/plans', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const plans = await pool.query(`
            SELECT * FROM plans 
            WHERE is_active = true 
            ORDER BY price_monthly ASC
        `);

        res.json(plans.rows);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Get plans error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get plans' });
    }
});

/**
 * Get current subscription
 * GET /api/v1/billing/subscription
 */
router.get('/subscription', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const subscription = await billingService.getClientSubscription(
            req.user.clientId
        );

        res.json(subscription || { active: false });

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Get subscription error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get subscription' });
    }
});

/**
 * Create subscription
 * POST /api/v1/billing/subscribe
 */
router.post('/subscribe', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { planId, autoRenew } = req.body;

        const subscription = await billingService.createSubscription(
            req.user.clientId,
            planId,
            {
                autoRenew,
                createdBy: req.user.id
            }
        );

        res.json(subscription);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Subscribe error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: error.message || 'Failed to subscribe' });
    }
});

/**
 * Cancel subscription
 * POST /api/v1/billing/cancel
 */
router.post('/cancel', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { reason } = req.body;

        const subscription = await billingService.cancelSubscription(
            req.body.subscriptionId,
            reason,
            req.user.id
        );

        res.json(subscription);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Cancel subscription error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to cancel subscription' });
    }
});

/**
 * Get invoices
 * GET /api/v1/billing/invoices
 */
router.get('/invoices', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { limit = 12, offset = 0 } = req.query;

        const invoices = await pool.query(`
            SELECT * FROM invoices 
            WHERE client_id = $1 
            ORDER BY created_at DESC
            LIMIT $2 OFFSET $3
        `, [req.user.clientId, limit, offset]);

        res.json(invoices.rows);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Get invoices error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get invoices' });
    }
});

/**
 * Get single invoice
 * GET /api/v1/billing/invoices/:invoiceId
 */
router.get('/invoices/:invoiceId', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const invoice = await pool.query(`
            SELECT i.*, 
                   p.transaction_id, p.paid_at as payment_date,
                   p.payment_method
            FROM invoices i
            LEFT JOIN payments p ON i.id = p.invoice_id
            WHERE i.id = $1 AND i.client_id = $2
        `, [req.params.invoiceId, req.user.clientId]);

        if (invoice.rows.length === 0) {
            return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Invoice not found' });
        }

        res.json(invoice.rows[0]);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Get invoice error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get invoice' });
    }
});

/**
 * Get payment methods
 * GET /api/v1/billing/payment-methods
 */
router.get('/payment-methods', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const methods = await pool.query(`
            SELECT * FROM payment_methods 
            WHERE client_id = $1 
            ORDER BY is_default DESC, created_at DESC
        `, [req.user.clientId]);

        res.json(methods.rows);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Get payment methods error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get payment methods' });
    }
});

/**
 * Add payment method
 * POST /api/v1/billing/payment-methods
 */
router.post('/payment-methods', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { type, details, isDefault } = req.body;

        // If this is default, remove default from others
        if (isDefault) {
            await pool.query(`
                UPDATE payment_methods 
                SET is_default = false 
                WHERE client_id = $1
            `, [req.user.clientId]);
        }

        const method = await pool.query(`
            INSERT INTO payment_methods (
                id, client_id, type, details, is_default
            ) VALUES (
                $1, $2, $3, $4, $5
            ) RETURNING *
        `, [uuidv4(), req.user.clientId, type, JSON.stringify(details), isDefault || false]);

        res.json(method.rows[0]);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Add payment method error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to add payment method' });
    }
});

/**
 * Delete payment method
 * DELETE /api/v1/billing/payment-methods/:methodId
 */
router.delete('/payment-methods/:methodId', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        await pool.query(`
            DELETE FROM payment_methods 
            WHERE id = $1 AND client_id = $2
        `, [req.params.methodId, req.user.clientId]);

        res.json({ success: true });

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Delete payment method error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to delete payment method' });
    }
});

/**
 * Process payment
 * POST /api/v1/billing/pay/:invoiceId
 */
router.post('/pay/:invoiceId', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { paymentMethod, paymentData } = req.body;

        const payment = await billingService.processPayment(
            req.params.invoiceId,
            paymentMethod,
            paymentData
        );

        res.json(payment);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Process payment error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to process payment' });
    }
});

/**
 * Get billing summary
 * GET /api/v1/billing/summary
 */
router.get('/summary', auth, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const summary = await pool.query(`
            SELECT 
                COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE status = 'PAID') as paid_invoices,
                COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE status = 'PENDING') as pending_invoices,
                COALESCE(SUM(total_amount) FILTER (WHERE status = 'PAID'), 0) as total_paid,
                COALESCE(SUM(total_amount) FILTER (WHERE status = 'PENDING'), 0) as total_pending,
                MAX(created_at) FILTER (WHERE status = 'PAID') as last_payment_date
            FROM invoices
            WHERE client_id = $1
        `, [req.user.clientId]);

        res.json(summary.rows[0]);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Get billing summary error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get billing summary' });
    }
});

module.exports = router;
